ID 0 — No-Bake Nut Cookies 
In a heavy two-quart saucepan, combine 1 cup firmly packed brown sugar, 1/2 cup evaporated milk, 2 tablespoons butter or margarine, and 1/2 cup broken pecans. Cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the mixture bubbles across the surface. Continue boiling and stirring for 5 minutes. Remove from heat and stir in 1/2 teaspoon vanilla, then add 3 1/2 cups bite-size shredded rice biscuits and mix thoroughly. Using two teaspoons, drop the mixture onto wax paper to form about 30 clusters. Let stand for approximately 30 minutes, until firm.

ID 1 — Jewell Ball’s Chicken 
Spread 1 small jar of chipped beef, cut into pieces, over the bottom of a baking dish. Place 4 boneless chicken breasts on top. In a bowl, mix together 1 can cream of mushroom soup and 1 carton sour cream, then pour the mixture evenly over the chicken. Bake uncovered at 275°F for 3 hours.

ID 2 — Creamy Corn 
Place 2 packages (16 oz each) frozen corn into a slow cooker along with 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese cut into cubes, 1/3 cup butter cut into pieces, 1/2 teaspoon garlic powder, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and 1/4 teaspoon pepper. Cover and cook on low heat for about 4 hours, until heated through and creamy, stirring before serving.

ID 3 — Chicken Funny
Boil 1 large whole chicken until fully cooked, then debone and cut into bite-size pieces. Place the chicken in a medium square casserole dish. Pour over 2 cans (10 1/2 oz each) chicken gravy and 1 can cream of mushroom soup, spreading evenly. Prepare 1 box (6 oz) Stove Top stuffing according to package directions, keeping it slightly dry, and spread it over the chicken mixture. Sprinkle 4 oz shredded cheese on top and bake at 350°F for about 20 minutes, until bubbly and lightly golden.

ID 4 — Reese’s Cups Candy
Mix together 1 cup peanut butter, 3/4 cup graham cracker crumbs, 1 cup melted butter, and 1 pound powdered sugar until smooth. Press the mixture firmly into an ungreased 13 x 9-inch pan. Melt 1 large package of chocolate chips and spread evenly over the top. Refrigerate for about 20 minutes, then cut into pieces before the chocolate fully hardens. Store in the refrigerator.

ID 5 — Cheeseburger Potato Soup
Wash 6 baking potatoes and prick them several times with a fork. Microwave with a damp paper towel on high for 6 to 8 minutes, until tender, then let cool slightly. Cut in half lengthwise, scoop out the pulp, and discard the skins. Brown 1 pound extra-lean ground beef in a skillet, drain, and set aside. In a large kettle, melt 2/3 cup butter or margarine over low heat, add flour and stir until smooth, then cook for 1 minute. Gradually add 6 cups milk, stirring constantly until thickened and bubbly. Stir in the potatoes, ground beef, 3/4 teaspoon salt, 1/2 teaspoon pepper, 1 cup shredded Cheddar cheese, 2 tablespoons chopped green onion, and 1/2 cup cooked crumbled bacon. Heat gently without boiling. Stir in 1 carton (8 oz) sour cream if desired. Garnish with remaining cheese, bacon, and green onions.

ID 6 — Rhubarb Coffee Cake
Cream together 1 1/2 cups sugar and 1/2 cup butter. Add 1 egg and beat well. Alternately add 1 cup buttermilk and a mixture of 2 cups flour, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and 1 teaspoon soda. Mix thoroughly, then stir in 2 cups finely chopped rhubarb and 1 teaspoon vanilla. Pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan and add topping as desired before baking.

ID 7 — Scalloped Corn
Mix together 1 can cream-style corn, 1 can whole kernel corn, about 20 crushed saltine crackers, 1 beaten egg, 2 teaspoons melted butter, and pepper to taste. Transfer to a buttered baking dish, dot the top with the remaining 4 teaspoons butter, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 8 — Nolan’s Pepper Steak
Roll 1 1/2 pounds round steak cut into strips in flour. Brown in a skillet, then season with salt and pepper. Combine the reserved tomato liquid from 1 can of tomatoes with 1 3/4 cups water and 1/2 cup onions. Add the browned steak, cover, and simmer for 1 hour and 15 minutes. Uncover, stir in 1 1/2 tablespoons Worcestershire sauce, then add the tomatoes and 2 diced green peppers. Simmer for 5 minutes and serve over hot cooked rice.

ID 9 — Millionaire Pie
Empty 1 large container Cool Whip into a bowl. Drain 1 large can crushed pineapple and mix it into the whipped topping. Add 1 can condensed milk, then squeeze the juice from 3 lemons, removing seeds, and stir it in. Chop 1 cup pecans and fold into the mixture. Pour into 2 graham cracker crusts, cover, and chill overnight before serving.

ID 10 — Double Cherry Delight
Drain 1 can (17 oz) dark sweet pitted cherries, reserving the syrup, and cut the cherries in half. Add 1/2 cup ginger ale to the syrup and enough water to make 1 1/2 cups liquid total. Dissolve 1 package (6 oz) cherry-flavored gelatin in 2 cups boiling water. Stir in the measured liquid and add 1/8 teaspoon almond extract. Chill until very thick. Fold in 1 cup miniature marshmallows and the cherries, then spoon into a 6-cup mold. Chill until firm, at least 4 hours or overnight.

ID 11 — Buckeye Candy
Mix together 1 box powdered sugar, 8 oz soft butter, and 1 jar (8 oz) peanut butter until smooth. Roll the mixture into small balls and place on a cookie sheet. Freeze for at least 30 minutes. Melt 12 oz chocolate chips together with paraffin in a double boiler. Using a toothpick, dip each ball about three-quarters of the way into the chocolate mixture, leaving the top exposed.

ID 12 — Quick Barbecue Wings
Clean chicken wings in the quantity desired. Coat lightly with flour and fry until fully cooked. Transfer the wings to a microwave-safe bowl, add barbecue sauce to taste, and stir well. Microwave on high for 4 minutes, stirring once during cooking.

ID 13 — Taco Salad Chip Dip
Mix together 8 oz taco sauce, 8 oz sour cream, and 8 oz cream cheese until smooth. Spread the mixture onto a pizza pan. Brown 1 lb ground beef, drain excess fat, and mix with 1 package taco seasoning. Spread the meat over the cream mixture. Layer with shredded lettuce, 1 diced tomato, 1 diced onion, 1 diced green pepper, and shredded Colby or Cheddar cheese. Serve with chips.

ID 14 — Pink Stuff Frozen Dessert
Mix together 1 can cherry or strawberry pie filling, 1 can crushed pineapple drained, 1 can sweetened condensed milk, 1 container (8 oz) thawed whipped topping, and 2 tablespoons lemon juice. Pour into a 9 x 13-inch pan and freeze until firm. Let stand about 15 minutes before serving.

ID 15 — Fresh Strawberry Pie
Combine 1 1/2 cups water, 4 tablespoons cornstarch, 1 cup sugar, and 1/8 teaspoon salt in a saucepan. Bring to a boil, stirring constantly, until thick and clear. Remove from heat and stir in 4 tablespoons strawberry gelatin. Cool slightly without letting it set. Layer 1 quart cleaned strawberries in a baked pie shell, pour glaze over them, refrigerate, and serve with whipped cream.

ID 16 — Easy German Chocolate Cake
Prepare 1/2 package chocolate fudge cake mix and 1/2 package white cake mix according to package directions, adding 1/4 cup Wesson oil. Pour into a 9 x 13-inch pan and bake as directed until done.

ID 17 — Broccoli Salad
Trim and wash 1 large head broccoli, then cut into bite-size pieces. Add 10 slices cooked, crumbled bacon, 5 sliced green onions or 1/4 cup chopped red onion, and 1/2 cup raisins. In a separate bowl, mix 1 cup mayonnaise, 2 tablespoons vinegar, and 1/4 cup sugar. Toss dressing with broccoli mixture and refrigerate for 2 to 3 hours before serving.

ID 18 — Strawberry Whatever
Dissolve 1 large package strawberry gelatin in 1 1/2 cups boiling water. Add 1 lb frozen strawberries in juice, 1 can crushed pineapple, 3 mashed ripe bananas, and 1 cup chopped pecans. Spread half the mixture in a pan and freeze for 30 minutes. Spread 1 pint sour cream over the top, then add remaining mixture. Chill until set.

ID 19 — Eggless Milkless Applesauce Cake
Cream together 1/2 cup shortening and 3/4 cup sugar. Add 1 1/2 cups applesauce, 1 cup raisins, and 1 cup nuts. Sift together 2 cups flour, 3 teaspoons soda, and 1 teaspoon each cinnamon, cloves, and nutmeg, then add to the mixture. Pour into a greased pan and bake at 350°F for 45 to 60 minutes.

ID 20 — Grandma Hanrath’s Banana Bread
Cream 1 cup sugar and 1/2 cup shortening. Add 2 eggs one at a time, then stir in 1 teaspoon salt and 2 teaspoons soda. Add 2 chopped overripe bananas, 2 cups flour, and 1/4 cup nuts. Mix well and bake in a loaf pan at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 21 — Chocolate Frango Mints
Mix together 1 package devil’s food cake mix, 1 package instant chocolate fudge pudding, 8 oz sour cream, 3/4 cup water, 1/2 cup Wesson oil, and 4 eggs. Beat for 5 minutes, scraping bowl often. Fold in 6 oz chopped Frango mints and bake at 350°F for 35 to 40 minutes.

ID 22 — Cuddy Farms Marinated Turkey
Mix together 2 cups 7-Up or Sprite, 1 cup vegetable oil, 1 cup soy sauce, and garlic salt to taste. Cut a whole turkey breast into hand-sized pieces and pour marinade over the meat. Refrigerate for at least 8 hours, up to 48 hours, before cooking.

ID 23 — Spaghetti Sauce to Can
Cook chopped peppers and onions in 1 cup oil for 30 minutes. Cook 1/2 bushel tomatoes and 1/4 cup minced garlic, then mill or process. Combine tomatoes with 6 cans tomato paste, 1 1/2 cups sugar, 1/2 cup salt, 1 tablespoon basil, 2 tablespoons oregano, and 1 teaspoon Italian seasoning. Cook 1 hour and seal in jars.

ID 24 — Prize-Winning Meat Loaf
Mix together 1 1/2 lb ground beef, 1 cup tomato juice, 3/4 cup oats, 1 beaten egg, 1/4 cup chopped onion, 1/4 teaspoon pepper, and 1 1/2 teaspoons salt. Press into a loaf pan and bake at 350°F for 1 hour. Let rest 5 minutes before slicing.

ID 25 — Smothered Round Steak
Dredge 2 lb round steak in flour and brown briefly in 1/2 cup vegetable oil. Add chopped onions, celery, bell peppers, beef stock, salt, black pepper, white pepper, and red pepper. Cover and cook slowly over low heat until tender.

ID 26 — Corral Barbecued Beef Steak Strips
Brown 2 lb sliced round steak in 2 tablespoons oil. Combine 1 can tomato sauce, 1/3 cup water, 2 tablespoons brown sugar, 1 tablespoon mustard, and 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce. Add sauce and sliced onion to meat and simmer 30 minutes until tender.

ID 27 — Easy Fudge
Heat 1 can sweetened condensed milk with 1 package semi-sweet chocolate chips and optional unsweetened chocolate over low heat, stirring until smooth. Remove from heat, stir in chopped nuts and 1 teaspoon vanilla, then spread into a buttered pan.

ID 28 — Taco-Filled Green Pepper
Brown 1 lb ground beef and mix with taco seasoning, kidney beans, and 1 cup salsa. Cut 4 green peppers in half and boil for 3 minutes. Fill peppers with meat mixture and bake covered at 350°F for 15 to 20 minutes. Top with tomato, cheese, and sour cream.

ID 29 — One Hour Rolls
Heat 1 cup milk, 2 tablespoons sugar, 1 tablespoon salt, and 3 tablespoons oil until boiling, then cool to lukewarm. Add 1 package yeast and mix into 2 cups flour. Roll dough, cut, let rise 1 hour, and bake at 350°F for 20 minutes.

ID 30 — Punch Bowl Fruit Salad
Combine 2 cans sliced peaches, 2 cans fruit cocktail, 1 can diced pineapple with juice, 1 quart strawberries, 4 bananas, and assorted apples and grapes. Mix well and chill before serving.

ID 31 — Summer Chicken
Marinate chicken cutlets in 1/2 cup oil, 1/3 cup red vinegar, 2 tablespoons oregano, and 2 tablespoons garlic salt. Cook as desired.

ID 32 — Cherry Pizza
Spread 2 cans cherry pie filling in a greased baking pan. Sprinkle dry white cake mix over cherries, top with ground nuts and melted butter, then bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 33 — Potato and Cheese Pie
Beat 3 eggs with 1 teaspoon salt and 1/4 teaspoon pepper. Stir in 2 cups half-and-half, 3 cups shredded potatoes, 1 cup Cheddar cheese, and 1/3 cup green onions. Bake at 400°F for 35 to 40 minutes.

ID 34 — Tuna Macaroni Casserole
Prepare 1 box macaroni and cheese as directed. Stir in 1 can drained tuna, 1 jar pimentos, and 1 chopped onion. Serve hot or cold.

ID 35 — Artichoke Dip
Drain and chop 2 cans artichoke hearts and mix with 1 cup mayonnaise and 1 cup Parmesan cheese. Bake uncovered at 350°F for 20 to 30 minutes.

ID 36 — Broccoli Dip for Crackers
Mix 16 oz sour cream, 1 package dry vegetable soup mix, 10 oz thawed chopped broccoli, and half of 6 oz grated Cheddar cheese. Top with remaining cheese and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 37 — Summer Spaghetti
Cook 1 lb thin spaghetti, drain, and toss with butter. Marinate overnight with Salad Supreme seasoning and Italian dressing. Add vegetables before serving.

ID 38 — Pear-Lime Salad
Drain 1 can pear halves and reserve juice. Boil juice and dissolve lime gelatin in it. Cool slightly, then mix with softened cream cheese and lemon yogurt. Stir in pears and chill until set.

ID 39 — Watermelon Rind Pickles
Cut 7 lb watermelon rind into cubes and parboil until tender. Boil 7 cups sugar with 2 cups vinegar, 1/2 teaspoon oil of cloves, and 1/2 teaspoon oil of cinnamon. Pour over rind, soak overnight, reheat twice, then seal in jars.

ID 40 — Chicken Stew
Remove meat from 3 lb boiled chicken and reserve the broth. In a large pot combine the chicken, 4 diced medium potatoes, 2 chopped onions, 1 can (16 oz) creamed corn, 1 can English peas, 1 can field peas, 1 can butter beans, 1 can tomatoes, 1 can (46 oz) tomato juice, and 1 small box macaroni. Add 1 tablespoon salt, 1 tablespoon black pepper, and 1 tablespoon sugar. Cook over medium heat until all vegetables are tender.

ID 41 — Quick Coffee Cake
Cream together 3 tablespoons softened butter or margarine and 1/2 cup granulated sugar. Add 1 egg and beat until creamy. Mix 1 cup flour, 1 1/4 teaspoons baking powder, and 1/4 teaspoon salt, then add alternately with 1/3 cup milk. Stir in 1/4 teaspoon vanilla. Spread batter in a greased 8-inch square pan. Mix 1/3 cup packed brown sugar with 1/2 teaspoon cinnamon, sprinkle on top, dot with 2 tablespoons butter, and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 42 — Angel Biscuits
Mix together 5 cups flour, 3 tablespoons sugar, 4 teaspoons baking powder, and 1 teaspoon soda. Cut in 1 1/2 sticks margarine. Dissolve 1 1/2 packages dry yeast in 1/2 cup warm water, stir into 2 cups buttermilk, then combine with dry ingredients. Cover and chill before baking as biscuits.

ID 43 — Quick Peppermint Puffs
Dip 8 marshmallows in 2 tablespoons melted margarine, then roll in 1/4 cup crushed peppermint candy. Wrap each marshmallow completely with crescent roll dough from 1 can. Dip again in margarine, place in greased muffin tin, and bake at 375°F for 10 to 15 minutes.

ID 44 — Fruit Pizza
Mix together 1 box yellow cake mix, 1/4 cup water, 1/4 cup brown sugar, 1/2 cup soft butter, 2 eggs, and 1/2 cup chopped nuts. Spread into greased pizza pans and bake at 350°F for 15 to 20 minutes.

ID 45 — Chocolate Mint Bars
Mix together 1 cup flour, 1 cup sugar, 1/2 cup softened oleo, 4 eggs, and 1 can chocolate syrup. Pour into a 9 x 13-inch pan and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes, until the top springs back lightly when touched.

ID 46 — Beer Bread
Stir together 3 cups self-rising flour, 1 tablespoon sugar, and 1 can (12 oz) beer. Pour into a greased loaf pan and bake at 425°F for 50 minutes. Drizzle melted butter over the top if desired.

ID 47 — Chicken Divan
Melt 1/4 cup margarine in a skillet and sauté 1/4 cup chopped onion and celery to taste. Remove from heat and stir in 1/4 cup flour and 1/8 teaspoon curry powder. Drain 1 can mushrooms and reserve juice, adding water to make 1/2 cup liquid. Stir liquid and 1 can cream of celery soup into mixture and cook until thick. Arrange chopped broccoli and cubed cooked chicken in a baking dish, spoon sauce over, top with shredded Monterey Jack cheese, and bake at 350°F until cheese melts.

ID 48 — Mexican Cookie Rings
Sift together 1 1/2 cups flour, 1/2 teaspoon baking powder, and 1/2 teaspoon salt. Cream 1/2 cup butter with 2/3 cup sugar, add 3 egg yolks and 1 teaspoon vanilla. Mix in dry ingredients, shape dough into rings, dip into multi-colored candies, and bake at 375°F for 10 to 12 minutes.

ID 49 — Vegetable-Burger Soup
Brown 1/2 lb ground beef lightly in a soup pot and drain excess fat. Add 2 cups water, 1 can stewed tomatoes, 1 can tomato sauce, 1 package onion soup mix, 1 package frozen mixed vegetables, 1 teaspoon sugar, and simmer for 20 minutes.

ID 50 — Chicken Ole
Dice 4 cooked chicken breasts and mix with 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 can green chili salsa sauce, 1 can green chilies, 1 cup milk, 1 grated onion, and pieces of corn tortillas. Let stand overnight, then bake at 375°F for 1 1/2 hours.

ID 51 — Creamy Coleslaw
In a large bowl combine 4 cups shredded cabbage, 1/2 cup shredded carrots, 1/4 cup chopped green pepper, and 2 tablespoons chopped onion. Mix separately 1/2 cup mayonnaise, 1 tablespoon vinegar, 2 teaspoons sugar, 1 teaspoon celery seed, and 1/4 teaspoon salt, then toss with vegetables.

ID 52 — Creole Flounder
Arrange 2 lb flounder fillets in a baking dish. Mix together chopped tomatoes, green pepper, lemon juice, salad oil, salt, onion, basil, black pepper, and red pepper sauce. Spoon mixture over fish and bake at 500°F for 5 to 8 minutes, until fish flakes easily.

ID 53 — Three Bean Salad
Combine 1 can green beans, 1 can yellow beans, and 1 can kidney beans, all drained. Mix together 1 cup sugar, 1/2 cup salad oil, 2/3 cup vinegar, and 1/3 cup water until sugar dissolves, then pour over beans and let stand overnight.

ID 54 — Dave’s Corn Casserole
Mix 1 can whole kernel corn, 1 can cream-style corn, 1 cup sour cream, 1 package corn bread mix, and 1 stick melted margarine. Pour into greased pan and bake at 350°F for 50 minutes.

ID 55 — Casserole Italiano
Brown 1 lb ground beef with 1/3 cup chopped onion. Add 1 can tomato soup, 1/3 cup water, 1/2 teaspoon oregano, and 1/2 teaspoon salt. Stir in 2 cups cooked noodles, place in casserole, top with 1 cup cheese, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 56 — Corned Beef and Cabbage Casserole
Combine 1 shredded cabbage, 1 teaspoon dry mustard, 1 can flaked corned beef, 1 can cream of celery soup, and 1 chopped onion. Cook uncovered over low heat until cabbage is tender, about 20 minutes.

ID 57 — Crab Cakes
Mix together 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce, 1 teaspoon dry mustard, 2 tablespoons mayonnaise, 1 egg, and Old Bay seasoning to taste. Gently fold in 1 lb lump crab meat and refrigerate before cooking.

ID 58 — Taco Dip
Mix 2 packages softened cream cheese with 1/2 cup mayonnaise. Spread on a platter and chill briefly. Spread 8 oz taco sauce over top, then layer green onions, green pepper, tomato, Mozzarella cheese, Cheddar cheese, and optional olives. Serve with tortilla chips.

ID 59 — Bonbon Cookies
Cream together 1/2 lb soft butter and 1/2 cup peanut butter. Add 1/2 lb graham cracker crumbs, 2 cups coconut, 1/2 cup nut meats, and a dash of vanilla. Mix well, form into balls, and chill several hours.

ID 60 — Forever Amber
Mix together 1 lb chopped orange slice candy, 2 cans Angel Flake coconut, 2 cups chopped pecans, 2 cans condensed milk, 1 teaspoon vanilla, and 1 teaspoon orange flavoring. Spread in buttered pan and bake at 275°F for 30 minutes. While hot, sift powdered sugar over top and drop by teaspoons onto waxed paper to dry.

ID 61 — Gooey Coffee Cake
Mix 1 yellow cake mix with 2 eggs and 1 stick melted oleo. Spread into greased 9 x 13-inch pan and sprinkle with 1 cup chopped nuts. Mix 2 eggs with 8 oz cream cheese and 1 lb powdered sugar and spread on top. Bake 15 minutes at 325°F, then 20 minutes at 350°F.

ID 62 — Phylis’ Pineapple-Banana Salad
Drain 1 large can chunk pineapple and reserve juice. Cut 4 to 5 bananas into chunks similar in size to pineapple. Combine gently and chill.

ID 63 — Chicken Casserole
Mix together 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can cream of celery soup, 1 cut-up chicken, 1/2 cup melted butter, and 1 1/2 cups uncooked rice. Cover and bake at 350°F for 2 1/2 hours, uncovering for the last 45 minutes.

ID 64 — Pineapple Nut Pie
Cream 1 package cream cheese until smooth, beat in 1 can sweetened condensed milk, then add 1/2 cup crushed pineapple, 1/3 cup chopped nuts, and 1/3 cup lemon juice. Pour into graham cracker crust and chill.

ID 65 — Annie’s Diabetic Candy
Mix together 1 package sugar-free vanilla pudding mix, 8 oz light cream cheese, 2 tablespoons butter, and 2 tablespoons peanut butter. Form into small balls, roll in chopped peanuts, and refrigerate.

ID 66 — Frozen Peach Mousse
Puree 4 peeled chopped peaches. Blend in 1 to 1 1/4 cups sugar, 1 1/4 cups sour cream, 1/4 cup lemon juice, and 3/4 to 1 teaspoon vanilla. Pour into container and freeze.

ID 67 — Strawberry Pie
Mix together 16 oz Cool Whip, 2 packages frozen strawberries, 1 3/4 cups sugar, and 12 oz cream cheese. Spoon into deep pie crusts and chill before serving.

ID 68 — Blueberry Surprise
Mix 1 stick melted margarine with 1 1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs and 1/4 cup sugar. Press two-thirds of mixture into bottom of baking dish.

ID 69 — Moist Devil’s Food Cake
Sift together 2 cups flour, 1 1/2 teaspoons baking soda, and 1/4 teaspoon salt. Cream 1/2 cup shortening with 1 1/2 cups sugar. Add 2 egg yolks, then stir in cocoa mixture made with cocoa, water, and vanilla. Alternate flour mixture with 1 cup milk, fold in beaten egg whites, and bake at 375°F for 30 minutes.

ID 70 — Dot’s Civil War Cake
Cook together 3 chopped apples, 2 cups raisins, 1 cup brown sugar, 1 cup granulated sugar, 2 tablespoons shortening, and 2 cups water. Boil 5 minutes and cool. Stir in 3 cups flour, 2 teaspoons soda, spices, and nuts. Bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 71 — Potato Casserole
Mix 6 cups diced potatoes with 1/2 cup chopped onion, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 cup sour cream, and 1 cup Cheddar cheese. Transfer to casserole dish, top with crushed cornflakes mixed with melted butter, and bake at 350°F for 50 minutes.

ID 72 — Dream Pie
Mix vanilla wafer crumbs with butter until combined. Press into pie dish and chill.

ID 73 — Divinity Fudge
Boil together 2 2/3 cups sugar, 2/3 cup white corn syrup, and 2/3 cup water until it forms a hard ball in cold water. Pour slowly over stiffly beaten 2 egg whites, beating constantly. Add 1 teaspoon vanilla and 1 cup chopped nuts, then drop onto wax paper.

ID 74 — Apple Crisp
Spread apples in baking dish. Mix 1/2 cup sugar with cinnamon and sprinkle over apples. Combine remaining sugar, flour, salt, cornflake crumbs, and oleo, then spread on top.

ID 75 — Sausage Balls
Mix 2 cups Bisquick with 1 lb sausage and 8 oz grated Cheddar cheese. Roll into balls and bake at 350°F for 15 minutes.

ID 76 — Consomme Chicken
Mix cream of chicken soup and consomme with water to make 4 cups liquid. Add chicken parts, season with salt and pepper, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 77 — Spanish Hamburgers
Brown celery, onions, and 1 lb ground beef in butter. Add vinegar, lemon juice, brown sugar, mustard, salt, pepper, catsup, and water. Simmer 30 minutes.

ID 78 — Egg Drop Soup
Stir chicken broth into cornstarch in saucepan and cook until slightly thickened. Slowly pour in beaten egg, stirring gently once. Remove from heat and garnish with sliced green onion.

ID 79 — Mulled Cider
Simmer 1/2 gallon apple juice with allspice, whole cloves, cinnamon stick, and 1 cup brown sugar. Strain into mugs and finish with a dash of nutmeg.

ID 80 — Sesame Ginger Chicken
Mix together 1 tablespoon toasted sesame seeds, 2 teaspoons grated ginger, 2 tablespoons honey, and 2 tablespoons reduced-sodium soy sauce. Flatten 4 skinned chicken breast halves to 1/4-inch thickness. Grill the chicken, basting frequently with the sauce, cooking about 4 minutes per side. Garnish with thin green onion strips before serving.

ID 81 — Egg Casserole
Sauté 1 chopped Vidalia onion, 16 oz sliced mushrooms, chopped green peppers, and 1 clove garlic in olive oil. In a separate pan combine buttered bread pieces, 6 eggs, and milk to desired consistency. Layer vegetables and egg mixture in a baking dish, refrigerate overnight, add cheese if desired, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 82 — Cranberry-Apple-Orange Salad
Grind 2 cups raw cranberries, 1 peeled apple, and 1 peeled orange in a food processor. Mix with 1 cup sugar and set aside. Prepare orange gelatin using slightly less water. Chill until thickened, then fold in fruit mixture and optional nuts. Chill until set.

ID 83 — Brown Rice
Place 1 cup raw rice, 1 can beef consommé, 1 can French onion soup, 1 can mushrooms, and 1/2 stick margarine in a covered baking dish. Bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 84 — Cranberry Salad
Blend softened cream cheese with margarine and sugar. Stir in whole berry cranberry sauce, drained crushed pineapple, and chopped walnuts. Whip cream and fold into mixture. Freeze in mold for several hours before serving.

ID 85 — Cheese Dip
Dice Italian tomatoes and green chili peppers. Combine with Velveeta cheese, minced onion, garlic, and salt in a double boiler. Heat for 30 minutes until smooth and serve hot with corn chips.

ID 86 — Funnel Cake
Sift together flour, salt, soda, sugar, and baking powder. Mix egg and milk and combine with dry ingredients to form smooth batter. Pour batter through funnel into hot oil and fry until golden. Drain and dust with powdered sugar.

ID 87 — Fast Real Good Fudge
Mix confectioners sugar, cocoa, and chopped nuts in a bowl. Melt margarine and Velveeta together, add vanilla, then pour over sugar mixture. Stir quickly, spread in buttered pan, cool, and cut into squares.

ID 88 — Squash Casserole
Cook squash, onions, and carrots until tender, then mash. Melt butter and stir in stuffing mix. Combine squash with sour cream and soup. Layer squash and stuffing in baking dish and bake at 350°F for 35 minutes.

ID 89 — Cheese Ball
Blend cream cheese with shredded Cheddar. Add chopped pimento, green pepper, onion, lemon juice, Worcestershire sauce, Tabasco, and salt. Mix well, shape into ball, and coat with chopped nuts.

ID 90 — Apricot Salad
Dissolve apricot gelatin in boiling water and sugar. Blend in cream cheese. Add crushed pineapple and apricot baby food. Chill until beginning to set, then fold in whipped evaporated milk. Chill fully before serving.

ID 91 — Pound Cake
Mix flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt. Add eggs, margarine, Crisco, milk, and flavoring. Beat until smooth. Pour into greased tube pan and bake at 325°F for 1 hour and 20 minutes.

ID 92 — Monkey Bread
Break frozen bread into balls and place in greased pan. Melt butter with brown sugar, pudding mix, milk, and cinnamon. Pour mixture over dough, allow to rise several hours, then bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 93 — Chicken Roll-Ups
Unroll crescent dough. Fill each piece with cooked diced chicken and grated cheese. Roll tightly and place in baking dish. Mix cream of chicken soup with milk and pour over rolls. Bake until golden.

ID 94 — Beef and Spanish Rice Casserole
Layer canned Spanish rice, corned beef, diced onion, and Cheddar cheese in greased casserole. Bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 95 — Baked Beans
Cook onions and bell pepper in oil until soft. Add ground beef and brown. Mix with pork and beans, catsup, brown sugar, salt, and pepper. Bake at 350°F for 45 minutes or cook in slow cooker.

ID 96 — Sweet-and-Sour Chicken
Sauté onion in shortening. Add carrots, water, and bouillon cubes and simmer. Mix brown sugar, cornstarch, ginger, catsup, vinegar, and soy sauce, then add to pot. Stir until thickened, add chicken, peppers, and pineapple, and heat through.

ID 97 — Ambrosia
Combine diced oranges, coconut, pecans, cherries, sugar, and orange juice. Chill overnight before serving.

ID 98 — Crazy Peanut Butter Cookies
Mix together peanut butter, sugar, and egg. Roll into balls, flatten with fork, and bake until set.

ID 99 — Brickle Bars
Mix cake mix, egg, and margarine and press into pan. Combine condensed milk, egg, pecans, and brickle bits and pour over base. Bake at 350°F for 30 minutes and cool before cutting.

ID 100 — Pancakes
Mix flour, soda, salt, and sugar. Add egg, melted margarine, and buttermilk. Stir until smooth. Cook on greased griddle until bubbles form, flip, and cook until golden.

ID 101 — Rustic Garlic Chicken
Season 4 chicken thighs with 1 teaspoon salt, ½ teaspoon black pepper, and 1 teaspoon paprika. Heat 2 tablespoons olive oil in a skillet and brown the chicken on both sides. Add 5 crushed garlic cloves and cook for 1 minute. Pour in 1 cup chicken broth, cover, and simmer for 35 minutes until tender.

ID 102 — Simple Lemon Pasta
Boil 250 g spaghetti in salted water. In a pan heat 3 tablespoons olive oil and add the zest of 1 lemon. Drain the pasta and add it to the pan with 2 tablespoons lemon juice, ½ teaspoon salt, and 30 g grated Parmesan cheese. Toss and serve.

ID 103 — Simple Chicken and Rice Bake
Cook 1 cup long-grain rice in 2 cups water until just tender. In a baking dish, combine the cooked rice with 300 g cooked chicken pieces, 1 cup chicken broth, ½ teaspoon salt, and ¼ teaspoon black pepper. Stir gently, cover with foil, and bake at 180°C (350°F) for 25 minutes until hot and slightly creamy.

ID 104 — Garlic Butter Potatoes
Peel and dice 600 g potatoes into small cubes. Boil in salted water for 12 minutes until tender, then drain well. Melt 2 tablespoons butter in a pan, add 2 minced garlic cloves, and sauté for 30 seconds. Add the potatoes, ½ teaspoon salt, and cook until lightly golden.

ID 105 — Creamy Tomato Chicken
Heat 1 tablespoon olive oil in a pan and brown 400 g chicken breast pieces. Add 1 cup crushed tomatoes, ½ cup cream, 1 teaspoon salt, and ¼ teaspoon pepper. Simmer uncovered for 20 minutes until the sauce thickens and coats the chicken.

ID 106 — Soft Scrambled Eggs
Crack 4 eggs into a bowl and beat with 2 tablespoons milk and a pinch of salt. Melt 1 tablespoon butter in a non-stick pan over low heat. Pour in the eggs and stir gently for 4–5 minutes until softly set.

ID 107 — Lentil Vegetable Stew
Rinse 1 cup dried lentils and place in a pot with 3 cups water. Add 1 chopped onion, 1 diced carrot, 1 teaspoon salt, and ½ teaspoon paprika. Simmer for 35 minutes until lentils are soft and stew is thick.

ID 108 — Oven Baked Sausages
Place 6 pork sausages in a baking tray. Add 1 sliced onion and 1 tablespoon olive oil. Sprinkle with ½ teaspoon salt and black pepper. Bake at 190°C (375°F) for 40 minutes, turning once.

ID 109 — Creamy Mushroom Pasta
Cook 250 g pasta in salted water. In a pan, sauté 200 g sliced mushrooms in 1 tablespoon butter. Add ½ cup cream, ½ teaspoon salt, and cooked pasta. Toss over low heat for 2 minutes.

ID 110 — Simple Tuna Rice Bowl
Cook 1 cup rice. Drain 1 can (160 g) tuna and mix with 1 tablespoon olive oil and a pinch of salt. Serve tuna over warm rice.

ID 111 — Baked Chicken Drumsticks
Season 6 chicken drumsticks with 1 teaspoon salt, ½ teaspoon paprika, and 1 tablespoon oil. Arrange on a baking tray and bake at 200°C (400°F) for 45 minutes until crisp and cooked through.

ID 112 — Garlic Spinach Skillet
Heat 1 tablespoon olive oil in a pan. Add 2 minced garlic cloves and sauté briefly. Add 300 g fresh spinach and ¼ teaspoon salt. Cook until wilted, about 3 minutes.

ID 113 — Creamy Oatmeal
Bring 2 cups milk to a simmer. Stir in 1 cup rolled oats and 1 tablespoon sugar. Cook over low heat for 6–8 minutes until thick and creamy.

ID 114 — Tomato Egg Stir Fry
Heat 1 tablespoon oil in a pan. Add 1 cup chopped tomatoes and cook for 3 minutes. Crack in 3 eggs, add ½ teaspoon salt, and stir gently until eggs are just set.

ID 115 — Simple Beef Mince Skillet
Heat 1 tablespoon oil in a pan. Brown 400 g ground beef with 1 chopped onion. Add 1 teaspoon salt and ½ teaspoon black pepper. Cook for 12 minutes until fully browned.

ID 116 — Buttered Pasta
Cook 200 g pasta in salted water. Drain and toss with 2 tablespoons butter and ¼ teaspoon salt until evenly coated.

ID 117 — Quick Chickpea Stew
Drain 1 can chickpeas and place in a pot with 1 cup crushed tomatoes, ½ cup water, 1 teaspoon salt, and ½ teaspoon cumin. Simmer for 15 minutes.

ID 118 — Baked Cheese Toast
Place bread slices on a baking tray. Top each with 30 g shredded cheese. Bake at 190°C (375°F) for 8 minutes until melted and bubbly.

ID 119 — Creamy Carrot Soup
Boil 500 g sliced carrots with 1 chopped onion in 1 liter water and 1 teaspoon salt for 25 minutes. Blend until smooth and stir in ½ cup cream.

ID 120 — Simple Chicken Wrap Filling
Cook 300 g diced chicken in 1 tablespoon oil with ½ teaspoon salt and pepper. Cook until golden and use as filling for wraps.

ID 121 — Rice with Fried Egg
Cook 1 cup rice. Fry 2 eggs in 1 tablespoon oil until whites are set. Serve eggs over rice with a pinch of salt.

ID 122 — Baked Zucchini Rounds
Slice 2 medium zucchini into rounds. Toss with 1 tablespoon olive oil and ½ teaspoon salt. Bake at 200°C (400°F) for 20 minutes.

ID 123 — Creamy Mashed Potatoes
Boil 700 g potatoes until soft. Mash with 2 tablespoons butter, ½ cup milk, and 1 teaspoon salt until smooth.

ID 124 — Simple Tomato Rice
Cook 1 cup rice in 1½ cups water mixed with ½ cup tomato sauce and 1 teaspoon salt until tender.

ID 125 — Garlic Chicken Skillet
Cook 400 g chicken strips in 1 tablespoon oil. Add 2 minced garlic cloves, ½ teaspoon salt, and cook 10 minutes until golden.

ID 126 — Soft Pancakes
Mix 1 cup flour, 1 cup milk, 1 egg, and 1 tablespoon sugar. Cook small pancakes in a lightly buttered pan until golden.

ID 127 — Warm Apple Cinnamon Bowl
Slice 3 apples and cook with 2 tablespoons sugar, ¼ cup water, and ½ teaspoon cinnamon for 10 minutes.

ID 128 — Creamy Corn Skillet
Heat 2 cups corn with 1 tablespoon butter, ¼ cup cream, and ½ teaspoon salt until heated through.

ID 129 — Simple Lentil Rice
Cook ½ cup lentils and 1 cup rice together with 3 cups water and 1 teaspoon salt until tender.

ID 130 — Cheese Omelet
Beat 3 eggs with salt. Cook in butter and add 50 g shredded cheese before folding.

ID 131 — Garlic Butter Chicken
Cook 400 g chicken in 2 tablespoons butter with 2 garlic cloves, salt, and pepper for 20 minutes.

ID 132 — Warm Milk with Honey
Heat 2 cups milk and stir in 1 tablespoon honey until dissolved.

ID 133 — Simple Baked Fish
Place 400 g white fish in a dish. Add 1 tablespoon oil, ½ teaspoon salt, and bake at 190°C for 20 minutes.

ID 134 — Tomato Pasta Toss
Cook 250 g pasta. Heat 1 cup tomato sauce with ½ teaspoon salt and toss with pasta.

ID 135 — Fried Potatoes and Onions
Slice 500 g potatoes and 1 onion. Fry in 2 tablespoons oil with salt until golden.

ID 136 — Creamy Yogurt Fruit Bowl
Mix 1 cup yogurt with 1 sliced banana and 1 teaspoon honey.

ID 137 — Simple Chicken Soup
Simmer 300 g chicken, 1 carrot, 1 onion, 1 teaspoon salt, and 1 liter water for 40 minutes.

ID 138 — Baked Egg Cups
Crack 1 egg into each greased muffin cup. Add salt and bake at 180°C for 12 minutes.

ID 139 — Rice with Butter and Salt
Cook 1 cup rice and stir in 1 tablespoon butter and ½ teaspoon salt.

ID 140 — Creamy Tomato Eggs
Cook 1 cup tomato sauce, crack in 3 eggs, cover, and simmer until eggs are set.

ID 141 — Simple Beef Rice
Cook 400 g ground beef with salt. Serve over 1 cup cooked rice.

ID 142 — Garlic Green Beans
Cook 300 g green beans. Toss with 1 tablespoon butter and 1 minced garlic clove.

ID 143 — Baked Chicken Breast
Season 2 chicken breasts with salt and bake at 190°C for 30 minutes.

ID 144 — Warm Oat Milk
Heat 2 cups oat milk with 1 tablespoon sugar.

ID 145 — Simple Tomato Sandwich
Layer sliced tomatoes with salt and butter between bread slices.

ID 146 — Fried Egg Toast
Fry 1 egg in butter and serve on toasted bread with salt.

ID 147 — Creamy Rice Pudding
Simmer ½ cup rice with 2 cups milk and 2 tablespoons sugar for 30 minutes.

ID 148 — Simple Chicken Stir Fry
Cook 400 g chicken strips in oil with salt for 10 minutes.

ID 149 — Buttered Carrots
Boil 400 g carrots and toss with butter and salt.

ID 150 — Soft Chocolate Pudding
Heat 2 cups milk with 2 tablespoons sugar and 2 tablespoons cocoa, thickened with cornstarch.

ID 151 — Garlic Bread Slices
Mix butter with minced garlic, spread on bread, and bake until crisp.

ID 152 — Rice and Lentil Bowl
Serve cooked rice with seasoned lentils and salt.

ID 153 — Simple Fried Fish
Pan-fry 300 g fish in oil with salt until golden.

ID 154 — Creamy Egg Rice
Stir soft scrambled eggs into warm rice with butter.

ID 155 — Garlic Butter Shrimp Rice
Cook 1 cup rice. Sauté 250 g shrimp in 2 tablespoons butter with 2 garlic cloves. Serve over rice.

ID 156 — Oven Baked Eggs
Crack 4 eggs into a greased dish. Add salt and pepper. Bake at 180°C for 12 minutes.

ID 157 — Lentil Tomato Curry
Simmer 1 cup lentils with 1 can tomatoes, 1 teaspoon curry powder, and 2 cups water for 30 minutes.

ID 158 — Cheese and Ham Omelet
Beat 3 eggs with salt. Cook in butter and fill with 50 g ham and 40 g cheese before folding.

ID 159 — Fried Zucchini Slices
Slice 2 zucchini. Fry in 2 tablespoons oil until golden. Sprinkle with salt.

ID 160 — Simple Vanilla Pudding
Heat 2 cups milk with 3 tablespoons sugar. Stir in 2 tablespoons cornstarch dissolved in water and cook until thick.

ID 160 — Simple Vanilla Pudding
Heat 2 cups of whole milk in a saucepan over medium heat until steaming but not boiling. In a small bowl, dissolve 2 tablespoons of cornstarch in 3 tablespoons of cold water, then stir it into the milk together with 3 tablespoons of granulated sugar. Cook while stirring continuously for about 5 minutes until thickened. Remove from heat and let cool slightly before serving.

ID 161 — Chicken Tomato Wraps
Warm 4 flour tortillas in a dry pan. Fill each tortilla with about 50 g of cooked shredded chicken, 2 tablespoons of chopped fresh tomatoes, and 1 tablespoon of plain yogurt. Roll tightly and serve warm.

ID 162 — Creamy Corn Soup
Place 2 cups of corn kernels, 1 cup of milk, and 1 cup of water in a saucepan. Add ½ teaspoon of salt and simmer gently for 15 minutes. Blend partially with an immersion blender, leaving some texture, and serve hot.

ID 163 — Baked Pasta with Cheese
Mix 300 g of cooked pasta with 1 cup of tomato sauce and 100 g of grated cheese. Transfer to a baking dish and bake at 190°C for 25 minutes until bubbly and lightly browned on top.

ID 164 — Simple Fried Eggs
Heat 1 tablespoon of butter in a frying pan over medium heat. Crack 2 eggs into the pan and cook for about 3 minutes until the whites are set. Season with ¼ teaspoon of salt and serve immediately.

ID 165 — Honey Glazed Chicken
Place 400 g of chicken breast pieces in a pan with 2 tablespoons of honey, 1 tablespoon of soy sauce, and ½ cup of water. Cook over medium heat for 20 minutes, turning occasionally, until the sauce thickens and coats the chicken.

ID 166 — Buttered Green Peas
Heat 2 cups of frozen peas in a small saucepan with 1 tablespoon of butter and ¼ teaspoon of salt. Cook for 6–8 minutes until tender, stirring occasionally.

ID 167 — Soft Chocolate Mug Cake
In a microwave-safe mug, mix 4 tablespoons of flour, 2 tablespoons of sugar, 2 tablespoons of cocoa powder, 3 tablespoons of milk, and 2 tablespoons of vegetable oil. Microwave on high for 90 seconds until set.

ID 168 — Simple Tomato Sandwich
Slice 1 large tomato and season with ¼ teaspoon of salt. Spread 1 tablespoon of butter on each of 2 bread slices, layer the tomato between them, and serve immediately.

ID 169 — Rice and Beans
Cook 1 cup of rice in 2 cups of water with ½ teaspoon of salt. In a separate saucepan, heat 1 can (400 g) of cooked beans with ¼ teaspoon of salt. Serve the beans over the rice.

ID 170 — Creamy Garlic Chicken
Brown 500 g of chicken breast pieces in a pan with 1 tablespoon of olive oil for 5 minutes. Add 2 minced garlic cloves and cook briefly, then pour in ½ cup of cream, add 1 teaspoon of salt and ½ teaspoon of black pepper, and simmer for 25 minutes.

ID 171 — Cinnamon Toast
Toast 2 slices of bread until golden. Spread each slice with 1 tablespoon of butter, then sprinkle with a mixture of 1 teaspoon sugar and ¼ teaspoon cinnamon.

ID 172 — Simple Beef Patties
Mix 400 g of ground beef with 1 teaspoon of salt and ½ teaspoon of black pepper. Shape into patties and fry in a pan for 4 minutes per side until cooked through.

ID 173 — Tomato Lentil Soup
Combine 1 cup of dry lentils, 1 can (400 g) of chopped tomatoes, 1 chopped onion, 1 teaspoon of salt, and 1.5 liters of water. Simmer gently for 35 minutes until lentils are tender.

ID 174 — Fried Rice with Egg
Heat 1 tablespoon of oil in a pan and add 2 cups of cooked rice. Push rice aside, crack in 1 egg, scramble it lightly, then mix with the rice and add 2 tablespoons of soy sauce. Cook for 5 minutes.

ID 175 — Creamy Banana Smoothie
Blend 2 ripe bananas with 1 cup of milk and ½ cup of plain yogurt until smooth. Serve chilled.

ID 176 — Baked Chicken Thighs
Season 4 chicken thighs with 1 teaspoon of salt and ½ teaspoon of pepper. Place in a baking dish and bake at 190°C for 45 minutes until golden and fully cooked.

ID 177 — Garlic Mashed Beans
Mash 2 cups of cooked white beans with 1 minced garlic clove, 1 tablespoon of olive oil, and ½ teaspoon of salt until creamy.

ID 178 — Warm Berry Compote
Cook 2 cups of mixed berries with 2 tablespoons of sugar over medium heat for 10 minutes until softened and syrupy.

ID 179 — Simple Cheese Quesadilla
Fill a tortilla with 80 g of grated cheese and cook in a dry pan for 3 minutes per side until melted and lightly browned.

ID 180 — Buttered Carrots
Boil 400 g of sliced carrots in salted water for 12 minutes. Drain and toss with 1 tablespoon of butter and ½ teaspoon of salt.

ID 181 — Classic Chicken Stir Fry
Heat 2 tablespoons of vegetable oil in a wok and cook 400 g of sliced chicken breast for 5 minutes. Add 1 sliced onion, 1 sliced bell pepper, and 3 tablespoons of soy sauce, then stir-fry for another 5 minutes.

ID 182 — Creamy Potato Soup
Boil 600 g of peeled potatoes and 1 chopped onion in 1 liter of water with 1 teaspoon of salt for 25 minutes. Mash slightly, add ½ cup of cream, and simmer 5 more minutes.

ID 183 — Garlic Lemon Rice
Cook 1 cup of rice in 2 cups of water with ½ teaspoon of salt. Stir in 1 tablespoon of butter, juice from ½ lemon, and 1 minced garlic clove before serving.

ID 184 — Baked Cheese Omelet
Whisk 4 eggs with ¼ cup of milk and ½ teaspoon of salt. Pour into a greased baking dish, sprinkle with 80 g of grated cheese, and bake at 180°C for 15 minutes.

ID 185 — Tomato Basil Pasta
Cook 250 g of pasta until al dente. Heat 1 tablespoon of olive oil and sauté 1 garlic clove, then add 1 cup of chopped tomatoes, ½ teaspoon of salt, and fresh basil. Toss with pasta.

ID 186 — Simple Beef and Potatoes
Brown 400 g of beef cubes in 2 tablespoons of oil. Add 500 g of diced potatoes, 1 cup of water, 1 teaspoon of salt, and ½ teaspoon of pepper. Cover and cook for 35 minutes.

ID 187 — Warm Cinnamon Milk
Heat 2 cups of milk with 1 tablespoon of sugar and ¼ teaspoon of cinnamon until steaming.

ID 188 — Roasted Bell Peppers
Slice 3 bell peppers and toss with 1 tablespoon of olive oil and ½ teaspoon of salt. Roast at 200°C for 25 minutes.

ID 189 — Creamy Egg Salad
Chop 4 hard-boiled eggs and mix with 3 tablespoons of mayonnaise, 1 teaspoon of mustard, and ¼ teaspoon of salt.

ID 190 — Simple Chicken Sandwich
Fill bread slices with 120 g of cooked chicken, a few lettuce leaves, and 1 tablespoon of mayonnaise.

ID 191 — Pan-Fried Gnocchi
Heat 1 tablespoon of butter in a pan and fry 400 g of gnocchi for 6 minutes until golden. Sprinkle with 30 g of grated Parmesan and salt to taste.

ID 192 — Honey Oat Breakfast Bowl
Mix 1 cup of cooked oats with 1 tablespoon of honey and ¼ cup of warm milk.

ID 193 — Tomato Egg Skillet
Heat 1 tablespoon of oil in a pan and cook 1 cup of chopped tomatoes for 3 minutes. Crack in 2 eggs, cover, and cook until set.

ID 194 — Garlic Chicken Rice Soup
Simmer 300 g of chicken pieces with ½ cup of rice, 1 minced garlic clove, 1 teaspoon of salt, and 1.5 liters of water for 40 minutes.

ID 195 — Simple Cheese Sauce
Melt 1 tablespoon of butter, stir in 1 tablespoon of flour, then whisk in 1 cup of milk. Add 80 g of grated cheese and ½ teaspoon of salt, stirring until smooth.

ID 196 — Warm Apple Compote
Cook 3 sliced apples with 2 tablespoons of sugar and ¼ cup of water for 12 minutes until soft.

ID 197 — Fried Polenta Slices
Slice 400 g of cooked polenta and fry in 2 tablespoons of oil for 4 minutes per side until crisp. Season with ½ teaspoon of salt.

ID 198 — Yogurt Banana Bowl
Slice 1 banana and mix with 1 cup of plain yogurt and 1 teaspoon of honey.

ID 199 — Simple Lentil Rice
Cook ½ cup of lentils together with 1 cup of rice in 2½ cups of water and 1 teaspoon of salt until tender.

ID 200 — Butter Garlic Toast
Mix 1 tablespoon of softened butter with 1 minced garlic clove and spread over toasted bread slices. Serve warm.

ID 201 — Beef Brisket
In a bowl, mix 1 cup catsup with 1 cup water, 1/2 minced onion, 2 tablespoons cider vinegar, 1 tablespoon prepared horseradish, 1 tablespoon prepared mustard, 1 teaspoon salt, and 1/2 teaspoon pepper to make a tangy sauce. Place a 4 lb beef brisket fat-side up in a shallow dish, pour the sauce over it, cover, and refrigerate for several hours or overnight so the flavors soak in. Roast the brisket in a preheated 300°F (about 150°C) oven for 3 1/2 to 4 hours, until very tender. Slice against the grain and serve with the sauce from the pan.

ID 202 — Fruit Medley
In a saucepan, combine 3 tablespoons tapioca, 1 cup water, and 1/2 cup sugar, and let it stand for 5 minutes. Cook over medium heat, stirring, until the tapioca turns clear, then add 1 1/2 cups water and 1 can (6 oz) thawed frozen orange juice concentrate. Stir in 1 can (11 oz) mandarin oranges (drained) and 1 can (16 oz) peach slices (drained and cut in half). Chill thoroughly, preferably overnight. Just before serving, add 1 bag (16 oz) frozen whole strawberries (thawed) and 2 large bananas (sliced), mixing gently so the fruit stays intact. Serve in dessert bowls and top each portion with a scoop of lime sherbet; this makes about 8 servings.

ID 203 — Nana’s Cornbread (9-inch skillet or 8x8 pan)
Preheat the oven to 425°F (about 220°C) and place 1/4 cup bacon fat in the 9-inch iron skillet (or 8x8 pan) to melt as the oven heats. In a bowl, stir 1/2 teaspoon baking soda into 1 cup buttermilk, then add 1 cup corn meal, 1 cup flour, 1 to 2 tablespoons sugar (depending on how sweet you like it), 1/2 teaspoon salt, 2 teaspoons baking soda, and 1 egg. Mix until just combined, then carefully pour the batter into the hot pan with the melted bacon fat. Bake for 20 to 25 minutes, until golden brown and set in the center.

ID 204 — Marinated Pork Roast
In a bowl, combine 1/2 cup sherry, 1/2 cup soy sauce, 1 tablespoon dry mustard, 1 teaspoon thyme, 2 minced garlic cloves, and 1 teaspoon ginger to make a marinade. Place 1 rolled pork roast (4 to 5 lb) into a large plastic bag set inside a deep bowl, pour in the marinade, and seal tightly. Let it marinate 2 to 3 hours at room temperature or overnight in the refrigerator, pressing the bag against the meat occasionally to distribute the marinade. Remove the roast, place it uncovered in a roasting pan, and cook at 325°F (about 165°C) for about 3 hours, basting with the marinade during the last hour. Slice and serve.

ID 205 — Dad’s Chili
Heat 1 tablespoon oil in a saucepan over medium heat and fry 2 lb pork tenderloin cut into cubes until lightly browned. Add 1 tablespoon minced garlic and cook briefly, then drain excess fat if needed. Dice 6 to 10 roasted and peeled Pueblo green chilies and add them to the pot along with 1 can stewed tomatoes and garlic salt to taste. Pour in 3 cups of the 4 cups water and bring to a steady simmer. In a small bowl, dissolve 3 teaspoons cornstarch in the remaining 1 cup water, then stir it into the chili to thicken. Simmer over medium heat until slightly thickened and the pork is tender, adjusting garlic salt (and salt if needed) before serving.

ID 206 — Spoon Rolls
Dissolve 1 package dry yeast in 2 cups lukewarm water, then stir in 1/4 cup sugar, 3/4 cup melted Crisco, and 1 egg. Add 4 cups self-rising flour and mix until you have a thick batter. Spoon the batter into a well-greased muffin tin, filling each cup about 2/3 full. Bake at 425°F (about 220°C) for about 20 minutes, until golden brown. If you want to bake later, the batter can be kept sealed in the refrigerator for up to 2 weeks.

ID 207 — Chicago Crunchy Chocolate Chip Cookies
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C). Sift together 3 1/2 cups flour, 3 teaspoons baking soda, and 1 teaspoon salt. In a large bowl, beat 1/2 cup butter with 1 cup packed brown sugar and 1 cup granulated sugar until blended, then beat in 1 egg, 1 tablespoon milk, and 2 tablespoons vanilla. Mix in 1 cup vegetable oil, then stir in 1 cup quick oats, 1 cup cornflakes, and 1 package (12 oz) semi-sweet chocolate pieces. Add the flour mixture and stir until a dough forms. Drop spoonfuls onto baking sheets and bake until set and crisp at the edges, about 10 to 12 minutes.

ID 208 — Salad Dressing
Place 2 tablespoons lemon juice (or wine vinegar), 1 tablespoon honey, 1 diced garlic clove, 1 tablespoon rosemary, 2 tablespoons water, 1 small diced onion, 1 tablespoon flax seed, and 1 teaspoon parsley into a blender. Blend until smooth, then taste and adjust acidity or sweetness if needed. Chill before serving for best flavor.

ID 209 — Leroy’s Heavenly Hash
In a large bowl, combine 1 No. 2 can fruit cocktail (about 29 oz), 4 bananas (cut up), 1 small bag miniature marshmallows, 1 package (8 oz) pecan pieces, 1 pint Cool Whip, and 1 small can crushed pineapple. Mix gently until evenly combined, then refrigerate until cold and serve.

ID 210 — Banana Cream Pie
Whisk together 2 1/2 cups milk, 1/4 cup heavy cream, and 2 egg yolks. In a heavy saucepan, combine 2/3 cup sugar with 4 tablespoons cornstarch, then whisk in the milk mixture. Cook over medium heat, stirring occasionally for about 5 minutes, then stir constantly until it comes to a boil, about 7 minutes more. Boil for 1 minute while stirring, then remove from heat and stir in 2 teaspoons vanilla and 3 tablespoons room-temperature butter. Fold in 1 to 2 sliced bananas, pour into a baked pie shell, smooth the top, and finish with meringue or whipped cream.

ID 211 — Marinated Onions and Blue Cheese
Whisk together 1/2 cup olive oil, 2 teaspoons lemon juice, 1 teaspoon salt, a dash of pepper, and 1/2 teaspoon sugar. Stir in 1/4 cup crumbled blue cheese, then add 2 cups sliced red or yellow onions and toss until coated. Chill briefly before serving so the flavors blend.

ID 212 — Cheese Cake (Graham Cracker Base)
Grease a springform pan (or a 13x9-inch pan). Mix 1 1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs with 1/2 cup melted butter, 1/4 teaspoon cinnamon, and 1/4 cup sugar. Press the mixture firmly into the bottom of the pan and slightly up the sides. In a bowl, beat 1 package (16 oz) cream cheese with 1/3 cup milk, 1/2 cup sugar, 3 eggs, and 4 tablespoons lemon juice until smooth, then pour over the crust and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until set (typically 40–55 minutes depending on pan size). Chill before slicing.

ID 213 — Carrot Bread
In a bowl, mix 1 cup sugar with 2/3 cup oil, then beat in 2 eggs. Add 1 1/2 cups flour, 1 teaspoon baking soda, 1 teaspoon baking powder, and 1 teaspoon cinnamon, mixing until smooth. Stir in 1 jar junior strained carrots (baby food) and 1/2 cup nuts. Pour into a greased loaf pan and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 1 hour, until a toothpick comes out clean.

ID 214 — Mistletoe Punch
In a punch bowl, combine 1 can (6 oz) thawed frozen lemonade concentrate, 1 can (6 oz) thawed frozen orange juice concentrate, and 6 cups water. Stir in about 1/2 cup grenadine syrup (the original text is unclear on the exact amount, but 1/2 cup works well for color and sweetness). Chill the mixture thoroughly. Just before serving, add ice and pour in 1 quart chilled ginger ale, stirring gently. Garnish each cup with wafer-thin lemon slices and maraschino cherries; this serves about 30.

ID 215 — Mixed Vegetable Casserole
Mix together 1 can Veg-All (drained), 1/2 cup chopped onion, 1/2 cup sliced water chestnuts, 1/2 cup grated Cheddar cheese, and 1/3 cup plus 2 level tablespoons mayonnaise. Spread into a casserole dish. Top with 1/2 roll crushed Ritz crackers mixed with 1/2 stick melted margarine, then bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 30 minutes until hot and lightly golden.

ID 216 — Cheeseburger Crescent Bake
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C). Press 1 package (8 oz) crescent rolls into a 13x9-inch pan to form a crust, pushing the dough about 1/2 inch up the sides. Brown 1 lb ground beef with 1/8 cup chopped onion, drain the grease, then stir in 1 teaspoon Worcestershire sauce, 1 teaspoon lemon juice, 1/2 teaspoon paprika, 1/4 teaspoon garlic powder, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and 1/8 teaspoon pepper. Stir in 2 cups shredded cheese and 1 beaten egg, then spread the mixture over the crust. Bake for 20 to 25 minutes until set and golden.

ID 217 — Do-Unkles Pumpkin Cake
Mix 2 cups sugar, 2 cups flour, 2 cups pumpkin, 1/2 teaspoon salt, 2 teaspoons cinnamon, 1 teaspoon nutmeg, 2 teaspoons baking soda, 2 teaspoons baking powder, 1 cup oil, 4 eggs, and 1 cup chopped walnuts. Beat at medium speed for about 3 minutes until smooth, then pour into a 9x13-inch pan. Bake at 325°F (about 165°C) for about 45 minutes, then cool and frost with cream cheese frosting or your favorite frosting.

ID 218 — Colonial Cheese Biscuits
In a large bowl, combine 2 cups plus 2 tablespoons flour with 1 1/2 teaspoons salt and 1 1/2 teaspoons paprika. Cut in 2 sticks softened butter, then work in 1 1/2 lb sharp Cheddar cheese until a stiff dough forms. Shape or roll and cut into small biscuit shapes, place on baking sheets, and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until set and lightly browned, about 12 to 15 minutes. Dust lightly with confectioners sugar if desired (the ingredient list includes it, but it’s optional and unusual—use only if you want a sweet-salty finish).

ID 219 — Simple Salsa Dip
In a microwave-safe bowl, combine 1 jar salsa (any size), 1 lb shredded American cheese, and 1 can refried beans. Microwave in short bursts, stirring between each, until the cheese is fully melted and the dip is hot and smooth. Serve with tortilla chips.

ID 220 — Any Flavor Pan Dessert
Mix 1 cup flour with 1 stick melted butter (or oleo), 1 tablespoon sugar, and 1/2 cup chopped pecans (optional). Press into a 9x13-inch pan and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 8 to 10 minutes, then cool. Blend 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese with 1 cup powdered sugar and 1 cup frozen whipped topping, then spread over the cooled base and chill. Prepare 2 packages instant pudding with 3 cups milk, spread over the cream cheese layer, chill 15 minutes, and top with the remaining whipped topping. Chill before slicing; this makes about 16 servings.

ID 221 — Mexican Casserole
Cover the bottom of a 9x13-inch baking dish with Fritos or Doritos (enough to make a solid layer). Brown 1 lb ground beef with 1 chopped onion, then stir in 1 can Rotel, 1 can mushroom soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, and 1 can (12 oz) Pet milk. Pour the mixture over the chips, top with grated cheese (as much as you like), and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 25 to 30 minutes until bubbly.

ID 222 — Apple Sour Cream Coffee Cake
Combine 2 cups flour, 1 teaspoon baking soda, and 1/2 teaspoon salt. In another bowl, cream 1/2 cup butter (or margarine) with 1 cup sugar until fluffy, then beat in 2 eggs and 1 teaspoon vanilla. Add the flour mixture alternately with 1 cup sour cream until smooth. In a separate bowl, toss 1 1/4 cups peeled thinly sliced apples with 1/2 cup sugar, 1 teaspoon cinnamon, and 1/2 cup chopped nuts. Spoon half the batter into a greased 9-inch tube or Bundt pan, sprinkle with half the apple mixture, add the remaining batter, then top with the remaining apple mixture. Bake at 375°F (about 190°C) for 40 to 50 minutes, cool 10 minutes, and unmold.

ID 223 — Snickerdoodles
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C). Beat together 1 1/2 cups sugar, 1/2 cup margarine, 1/2 cup vegetable shortening, and 2 eggs until smooth. In another bowl, combine 2 3/4 cups flour, 2 teaspoons cream of tartar, 1 teaspoon baking soda, and 1/4 teaspoon salt, then stir into the wet mixture until a soft dough forms. Mix together 2 teaspoons sugar and 2 teaspoons cinnamon for coating. Roll dough into small balls (about 1 tablespoon each), roll in the cinnamon-sugar, and place on a cookie sheet about 2 inches apart. Bake for 8 to 10 minutes until set.

ID 224 — Spaghetti Salad
Cook 1 lb spaghetti until tender, drain, and cool completely. In a large bowl, combine the cooled spaghetti with 3 diced cucumbers, 4 diced tomatoes, 2 diced celery stalks, 1 diced green pepper, and 2 diced onions. Pour in 1 small bottle Wish-Bone Italian dressing and add 1/2 bottle Salad Supreme seasoning, then toss well. Chill before serving for best flavor.

ID 225 — Spanish Meat Balls
Mix 1 lb ground meat with 2 slices cubed bread, 1 grated onion, 1/2 cup uncooked rice, 1 teaspoon chili powder, 1/2 teaspoon allspice, 2 eggs, 1 teaspoon salt, and 1 green pepper (optional). Shape into small meatballs and place in a greased casserole dish. In a saucepan, heat 2 cans tomato soup with 2 1/2 soup cans of water and the remaining 1 teaspoon chili powder, then pour over the meatballs. Cover and bake at 375°F (about 190°C) for about 2 hours; this yields about 6 servings.

ID 226 — Broccoli Cornbread
In a large bowl, combine 1 box Jiffy corn muffin mix with 1 1/2 sticks melted margarine. Add 2 whole eggs and 2 egg whites, 1 cup sour cream, 1 package (10 oz) frozen chopped broccoli (thawed but not drained), and 1 medium chopped onion. Mix well, pour into an ungreased 9x13-inch pan, and bake at 400°F (about 200°C) for 20 to 25 minutes until golden.

ID 227 — Fried Onion Rings
Slice 2 large sweet onions into 1/2-inch rings and separate them. Soak the rings in ice water for 30 minutes, then drain well. Make a batter by whisking 1 egg with 2/3 cup water, 1 tablespoon vegetable oil, and 1 teaspoon lemon juice, then stir in 1 cup all-purpose flour, 1 1/2 teaspoons baking powder, 1 to 1 1/4 teaspoons salt, and 1/8 to 1/4 teaspoon cayenne pepper. Heat deep frying oil in a pot, dip onion rings into the batter, and fry until golden, then drain on paper towels and salt lightly if needed.

ID 228 — Mayonnaise Rolls
Mix 1 cup White Lily self-rising flour with 1/3 cup mayonnaise, 1/2 cup sweet milk, and a pinch of salt. Stir until smooth, spoon into greased muffin pans filling each about 1/3 full, and bake at 400°F (about 200°C) until browned, about 12 to 15 minutes. This makes about 6 rolls.

ID 229 — Cheeseburger Loaf
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C) and lightly grease a loaf pan. In a bowl, mix 1 1/2 lb ground chuck with 1/2 cup evaporated milk, 1 egg, 1 cup cracker crumbs, 4 tablespoons finely chopped onion, 1 1/2 teaspoons salt, 1 teaspoon dry mustard, and 1 tablespoon ketchup. Press 1/3 of the meat mixture into the pan, sprinkle 1/2 cup grated American cheese over it (keeping cheese away from the edges), add another 1/3 meat layer, another 1/2 cup cheese, and finish with the remaining meat. Bake for 1 hour, let stand 10 to 15 minutes, then slice; it yields about 6 servings.

ID 230 — One Bowl Chocolate Fudge (Microwave)
In a microwave-safe bowl, combine 1 package (8 oz) semi-sweet chocolate with 2/3 cup sweetened condensed milk. Microwave on high for 1 minute, stir well, then microwave 1 minute more and stir until completely smooth. Stir in 1 teaspoon vanilla, 1/8 teaspoon salt, and 1 cup chopped nuts. Spread into a greased 9x5-inch loaf pan and refrigerate about 30 minutes until firm, then cut into squares.

ID 231 — Ranch Style Baked Beans Casserole
Brown 1 lb ground beef in 2 tablespoons margarine, then stir in 1 package onion soup mix, 1/2 cup water, 1 cup catsup, 2 tablespoons prepared mustard, 2 teaspoons vinegar, 2 cans (1 lb each) pork and beans in tomato sauce, and 1 can (1 lb) kidney beans (drained). Pour into a bean pot or 2-quart casserole dish and bake at 400°F (about 200°C) for 30 minutes; this makes about 10 to 12 servings.

ID 232 — Etta’s Hungarian Coffee Cake
In a bowl, mix 1 cup brown sugar with 1/3 cup shortening until blended, then work in 1 cup flour and a pinch of salt until crumbly. Reserve 1/2 cup of these crumbs for the topping. To the remaining mixture, add 1 beaten egg. Stir 1 teaspoon baking soda and 1/2 teaspoon baking powder into 1/2 cup sour milk (made by adding 1 tablespoon vinegar or lemon juice to milk), then mix into the batter. Spread into a greased 9-inch cake pan or pie plate, sprinkle the reserved crumbs over the top, and bake for about 35 minutes until set.

ID 233 — Beer Biscuits
Stir 1 1/2 tablespoons sugar into 6 oz warm beer until dissolved, then pour into 2 cups biscuit mix and stir just until combined. Bake according to the biscuit mix package directions.

ID 234 — Baked Spaghetti
In a large skillet, sauté 1 cup chopped onion and 1 cup chopped green pepper in 1 tablespoon butter until tender. Add 1 can (28 oz) tomatoes with liquid (cut up), 1 can (4 oz) drained mushroom stems and pieces, 1 can (2 1/4 oz) drained sliced ripe olives, and 2 teaspoons dried oregano, plus 1 lb browned ground beef if using. Simmer uncovered for 10 minutes. In a greased 13x9-inch baking dish, layer half of 12 oz cooked and drained spaghetti, half the sauce mixture, and 1 cup of the 2 cups shredded Cheddar cheese. Repeat the layers. Stir 1 can (10 3/4 oz) condensed cream of mushroom soup with 1/4 cup water, spread over the top, sprinkle with 1/4 cup grated Parmesan, and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until hot and bubbly.

ID 235 — Easy Apple Dumplings
Peel 5 cooking apples and cut into quarters. Separate and roll out 1 can biscuits (10 count), then cut each biscuit in half. Wrap one apple quarter in each biscuit half and place in a buttered baking dish. In a saucepan, mix 1/2 cup granulated sugar, 1/2 cup brown sugar, 1 1/2 cups water, 1 teaspoon apple pie spice, and 1 teaspoon vanilla, then pour over the dumplings. Cut 1 stick butter (or margarine) over the top and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until apples are tender. Baste with the syrup and continue baking until golden; this yields about 8 to 10 portions.

ID 236 — Twinkie Dessert
Line the bottom of a 13x9-inch pan with 14 Twinkies. Dissolve 1 large box strawberry Jell-O in 2 cups hot water, then stir in 1 package (10 oz) frozen strawberries (thawed) or 2 cups fresh strawberries. Pour the strawberry mixture over the Twinkies and let set for at least 30 minutes. Prepare 1 large box vanilla instant pudding as directed, spread it over the set Jell-O layer, then top with 1 large container Cool Whip. Chill before serving and decorate with extra strawberries if desired.

ID 237 — Gooey Butter Cake
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C). Mix 1 box yellow or chocolate cake mix with 1 egg and 1 stick melted butter, then press into a greased and floured 9x12-inch pan. Beat together 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese with 2 eggs, 1 box powdered sugar, and 1 teaspoon vanilla until smooth, then pour over the crust. Bake for about 35 to 40 minutes, cool completely, and cut into squares.

ID 238 — Corn Pudding
Mix 1 tablespoon flour with 3 tablespoons sugar, 1 teaspoon salt, and 1/8 teaspoon pepper. Stir this into 1 can (1 lb) cream-style corn, then add 1 tablespoon melted butter and 4 well-beaten eggs. Stir in 1 cup scalded milk, pour into a greased casserole dish, and set the dish in a pan of hot water. Bake at 325°F (about 165°C) for about 1 hour until set; this serves about 6.

ID 239 — Honey Cake
Preheat the oven to 325°F (about 165°C) and grease and flour a 9x13-inch pan. Beat 3 eggs with an unknown amount of honey (the source text shows “??? c. honey,” so the exact quantity is missing; a common workable amount would be 1 cup honey, but the original recipe does not specify). Add 1/2 cup sugar and mix again. Stir 2 teaspoons baking powder into 1 cup strong black coffee and add it, along with 3 tablespoons soft margarine, to the egg mixture. Add 1 teaspoon baking soda, 4 cups flour, and 1 teaspoon cinnamon, then beat until smooth. Pour into the pan and bake for 55 minutes to 1 hour.

ID 240 — Enchiladas
In a saucepan, combine 1 can (12 oz) tomato paste with 1 quart water, 2 minced garlic cloves, and 5 teaspoons chili powder, then simmer for 20 minutes to make the sauce. In a skillet, brown 1 lb lean ground beef with 1/2 cup chopped green onions, drain fat, then stir in 1 1/2 cups shredded Monterey Jack cheese and 1 cup of the sauce. Spoon 1/4 cup sauce into a shallow 3-quart baking dish. Dip corn tortillas (1 dozen) quickly into the remaining sauce to soften, fill each with some of the beef mixture, roll up, and place seam-side down in the dish. Pour remaining sauce over the top, sprinkle with the remaining 1/2 cup cheese and extra onions, and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 20 minutes; this makes about 6 servings.

ID 241 — Zucchini in Tomato Juice (Weight Watchers Style)
Cut zucchini into cubes (halve lengthwise first, then cube). Place the zucchini in a saucepan with 12 oz tomato juice, a dash of oregano, a dash of parsley flakes, a dash of garlic powder, 2 tablespoons bell pepper, 2 tablespoons dehydrated onions, salt to taste, and 1 chicken bouillon cube. Simmer until the zucchini is tender.

ID 242 — Pineapple Casserole
Mix 1 cup sugar with 6 tablespoons flour and 2 cups grated Cheddar cheese. Stir in 2 cans (15 1/2 oz each) pineapple chunks (drained), then spread into a greased 10x10-inch casserole dish. Top with 1 1/2 cups crushed Ritz crackers and drizzle with 1 stick melted margarine. Bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 30 minutes until hot and golden.

ID 243 — Brunswick Stew
Bring 1 whole chicken (about 2 lb) to a boil in 3 cups water with 1 1/2 teaspoons salt, then reduce heat and simmer about 1 hour until tender. Remove the chicken and set aside. Add 3 potatoes (diced), 1 chopped onion, 1 box (10 oz) frozen lima beans, 1 cup corn (frozen or canned), and 1 can tomatoes to the broth and simmer until the vegetables are tender. Strip the chicken from the bones in large pieces and return it to the pot for the last 5 minutes of cooking. Finish with 1/4 cup butter and salt and pepper to taste.

ID 244 — Cheese Ball
Beat 2 packages (8 oz each) cream cheese with 2 tablespoons mayonnaise and 1 teaspoon lemon juice until smooth. Finely chop 5 to 6 green onions, 1 package (6 oz) smoked deli beef, 1 small can chopped black olives, and 1 small green bell pepper, then stir into the cheese mixture. Chill at least 6 hours. Shape into a ball, roll in chopped nuts, and serve with Ritz crackers.

ID 245 — Marinated Carrots
Cook 2 lb carrots cut into diagonal slices until tender, drain, and cool. Toss with 1 large onion sliced into rings. In a saucepan, combine 1 can (10 oz) undiluted tomato soup with 1 cup sugar, 1/2 cup salad oil, 3/4 cup vinegar, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and 1/2 teaspoon pepper, then bring to a boil just until the sugar dissolves. Pour the hot marinade over the carrots and onions, mix well, cover, and refrigerate overnight.

ID 246 — Blueberry Cake
Beat 4 egg whites until stiff, then gradually add 1 cup of the 2 cups sugar and set aside. Cream 1 cup shortening with 1 teaspoon salt, the remaining 1 cup sugar, and 2 teaspoons vanilla, then beat in 4 egg yolks until creamy. Add 2 teaspoons baking powder, 3 cups flour, and 2/3 cup milk alternately, mixing until smooth. Fold in the egg white mixture, then gently fold in 3 cups floured blueberries. Pour into a well-greased and floured 9x13-inch pan, sprinkle a little sugar over the top if desired, and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 50 minutes.

ID 247 — Summer Squash Casserole
Cook 6 cups sliced yellow squash with 1 cup finely chopped onion using a little water or steaming, then drain well. Mix 1 can cream of chicken soup (undiluted) with 8 oz sour cream and stir into the squash mixture. Melt 1 stick butter and combine with 1 package (8 oz) stuffing mix. Spread a layer of stuffing in the bottom of a 6x10-inch baking dish, add a layer of squash mixture, then alternate layers, ending with stuffing on top. Bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 20 to 25 minutes until hot and lightly crisp on top.

ID 248 — Skor Cake
Bake 1 box German chocolate cake mix according to package directions in a 9x13-inch pan. As soon as the cake comes out of the oven, poke holes all over the surface and pour 1 can Eagle Brand sweetened condensed milk and 1 jar Smucker’s caramel sauce evenly over the cake. Let cool completely, then spread 1 container Cool Whip over the top. Crush 6 Skor candy bars and sprinkle them over the frosting, then refrigerate.

ID 249 — Never Fail Pie Crust (Double Crust)
In a bowl, combine 4 cups sifted flour with 1 teaspoon sugar and 1/2 teaspoon salt. Cut in 1 1/2 cups shortening using a pastry blender until the mixture resembles coarse crumbs. In another bowl, beat 1 egg with 1/2 cup ice-cold water, then stir in 1 tablespoon vinegar. Add the liquid to the flour mixture and mix until the dough comes together. Divide into two portions and roll out on a floured surface for a double-crust pie.

ID 250 — Best Brownies
Preheat the oven to 350°F (about 175°C) and grease a 9x13-inch pan. Melt 1/4 lb butter (about 1 stick) and pour into a mixing bowl. Beat in 1/2 cup cocoa and 2 cups sugar until smooth, then beat in 4 eggs one at a time and stir in 2 teaspoons vanilla. Add 1 1/2 cups flour, 1/4 teaspoon salt, and 1 cup flaked coconut, stirring just until combined. Spread in the pan and bake for about 25 minutes, then cool and cut into bars.

ID 251 — Stuffed Mushroom Caps
Carefully remove stems from 20 to 24 large white mushrooms and hollow out the caps, reserving the stems. Fry the mushroom stems, chop them, and drain. Brown and drain 1 lb sweet sausage, then mix it with the cooked stems, 3/4 cup Mozzarella cheese, and 1/2 cup seasoned bread crumbs. Fill each mushroom cap with the mixture, place in a shallow baking dish, add a little wine (amount not specified—just enough to lightly moisten the bottom), and bake at 400°F (about 200°C) for 15 to 20 minutes until the cheese is melted. Serve immediately.

ID 252 — Toffee Brickle
Line the bottom of a lasagna-size pan with unsalted soda crackers in a single layer. In a saucepan, boil 3/4 cup packed brown sugar with 2 sticks butter for about 8 minutes, stirring frequently, then pour the hot toffee evenly over the crackers. Bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 15 minutes, remove from the oven, and immediately sprinkle 1 bag (12 oz) chocolate chips over the top. Let sit briefly so the chips melt, then spread the chocolate smooth with a knife. Cool completely, crack into pieces, and store airtight.

ID 253 — Stir-Fried Veggies Medley
Cut 2 medium carrots and 2 celery stalks into thin strips, thinly slice 1 medium onion (or 2 small onions), cut 1 medium bunch broccoli into 2 x 1/2-inch pieces, and quarter 1/2 lb mushrooms (halve if small). Heat 1/4 cup salad oil or olive oil in a large skillet over high heat and stir-fry the vegetables quickly for 3 to 4 minutes. Add the mushrooms, 1/4 cup water, 1 1/4 teaspoons salt, 1/2 teaspoon pepper, and 1 level teaspoon sugar, then cover and cook 5 to 6 minutes longer until tender-crisp, stirring occasionally.

ID 254 — Bacon and Egg Breakfast Bake
Preheat the oven to 450°F (about 230°C). Spread 4 oz diced fully cooked Canadian bacon or ham in the bottom of a 9-inch pie plate and sprinkle with 1/2 cup finely chopped cheese (Muenster, Cheddar, or Monterey Jack). Beat 4 eggs with 1 1/2 cups skim milk and 1/2 teaspoon pepper, then pour into the dish. Bake for 15 minutes, reduce heat to 350°F (about 175°C), and bake another 10 to 15 minutes until browned and firm in the center. Cool 10 minutes before cutting into wedges.

ID 255 — Spiced Tea Mix
In a jar or bowl, mix 1 1/4 cups Tang with 1/2 cup sugar, 1/3 cup instant tea, 1/2 teaspoon cinnamon, 1/4 teaspoon cloves, and a dash of salt. To serve, stir 3 to 4 teaspoons of the mix into 1 mug of hot water.

ID 256 — Fruit Pizza (Cookie Dough Base)
Press 1 tube cookie dough into a circular baking pan and bake according to the package directions, then cool completely. Beat 1 package cream cheese with 1/3 cup Marshmallow Fluff until smooth, spread over the cooled cookie crust, and top with sliced blueberries, peaches, kiwi, and strawberries (amounts not specified, so use as much as needed to cover the surface). Chill briefly before slicing.

ID 257 — Ham Roll-Ups
Lay 6 thin slices prosciutto ham on a cutting board and cut them into 1/2-inch strips lengthwise without separating the stacked strips. Mix 3 oz soft cream cheese with 1 small finely chopped onion, then spread a thin layer over the ham. Roll tightly into bite-size roll-ups; this makes about 30 pieces.

ID 258 — Pineapple Soufflé
Melt 1/4 cup butter in a 9x9-inch baking dish. In a bowl, mix 1 1/2 cups sugar with 1 large can drained pineapple, 3 slices cubed bread, 3 beaten eggs, and 1/4 cup milk, then pour into the dish over the butter. Sprinkle with cinnamon (amount to taste), plus 1 tablespoon sugar, and top with roasted pecans (amount not specified). Bake at 300°F (about 150°C) for about 40 minutes.

ID 259 — Real Whipped Cream That Keeps
Soften 1/2 teaspoon unflavored gelatin in 4 teaspoons cold water in a small heatproof bowl. Set the bowl in a saucepan of hot water until the gelatin dissolves, then remove and let cool for 1 minute. Whip 1 cup heavy cream with a pinch of salt until almost stiff, then add the dissolved gelatin, 1/2 teaspoon real vanilla, and 1 teaspoon sugar. Continue whipping until stiff; this makes about 2 1/2 cups.

ID 260 — Montana Mud Cake
Cream 2 sticks margarine with 2 cups sugar and 2 tablespoons cocoa until smooth. Beat in 4 eggs and 1 teaspoon vanilla, then stir in 1 1/2 cups flour, 1 1/3 cups coconut, and 1 cup chopped pecans. Pour into a greased and floured 9x12-inch pan and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 30 minutes. While still warm, spread a jar of marshmallow cream over the cake and finish with frosting if desired.

ID 261 — Diane’s Quick Quiche
Whisk 3 eggs with 1/4 teaspoon salt and pepper to taste, then stir in 1/2 cup Bisquick and 1 1/2 cups melted margarine. Fold in 1 cup shredded Swiss cheese, 1/2 cup crisp fried bacon (crumbled), 1/4 cup chopped onion, a pinch of basil, a pinch of marjoram, and 1 cup broccoli (or another favorite vegetable). Pour into a greased pie dish and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until set in the center, about 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 262 — Egg Drop Soup
Heat 2 tablespoons peanut oil in a large pot over medium heat and cook 1 cup chopped onion with 1 1/2 teaspoons minced garlic and 1 teaspoon minced ginger root for 2 minutes. Add 1 lb lean pork cut into strips and cook until no longer pink. Pour in 7 cups chicken broth, add 2 tablespoons soy sauce and 1/4 teaspoon pepper, and bring to a boil. Add 1 cup thinly sliced carrots and simmer 15 minutes, then add 1 can (8 oz) bamboo shoots (drained), 1 can (8 oz) sliced water chestnuts (drained), and 6 oz frozen pea pods. Stir in 1/4 teaspoon sesame oil, reduce heat to low, and slowly drizzle in 2 well-beaten eggs while stirring with a fork to create strands.

ID 263 — Summer Berry Sauce
In a bowl, stir together 3/4 cup thawed frozen raspberry (or raspberry blend) juice concentrate with 2 tablespoons honey. Add 1 cup sliced fresh strawberries, 1 cup blueberries (fresh or partially thawed), and 1 cup raspberries (fresh or partially thawed), then toss gently. Chill before serving; this makes about 3 cups.

ID 264 — Cherry Pie (No-Bake Style)
Let 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese come close to room temperature. Blend the cream cheese with 1 can condensed milk, 1/3 cup lemon juice, and 1 teaspoon vanilla until smooth, then pour into a 9-inch graham cracker crust. Chill for about 2 hours, spread 1 can cherry pie filling on top, then chill another hour before serving.

ID 265 — Baked Bean Casserole
In a large bowl, combine 1 large can pork and beans, 1 regular can red kidney beans, and 1 can small green lima beans. Stir in 3 medium sliced onions, 4 tablespoons bacon drippings, 1/2 cup catsup, 1/2 cup brown sugar, 1/4 cup vinegar, 1 teaspoon dry mustard, 3 tablespoons garlic salt, 1 teaspoon salt, and 1/2 teaspoon black pepper. Pour into a 2-quart casserole and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for 1 3/4 hours.

ID 266 — Pumpkin Bread
Mix 2 cups canned pumpkin with 1 cup salad oil and 3 cups sugar, then beat in 4 beaten eggs. Add 3 1/4 cups flour, 2 teaspoons salt, 1 teaspoon baking powder, 1 teaspoon baking soda, 1 teaspoon cinnamon, 1 teaspoon cloves, and 1 teaspoon nutmeg, and mix until smooth. Divide into 2 greased loaf pans and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for at least 1 1/4 hours, until a tester comes out clean.

ID 267 — Fried Rice
Cook 1/4 cup chopped onions and 2 tablespoons chopped green pepper in 2 tablespoons salad oil until the onion is tender. Add 2 cups cooked rice, 3 oz sliced mushrooms, and 2 tablespoons soy sauce, then cook over low heat for about 10 minutes, stirring frequently. Stir in 3 beaten eggs and cook 2 to 3 minutes longer until the eggs are set throughout.

ID 268 — Paw Paw’s Pancakes
Beat 2 eggs, then mix in 1 1/2 tablespoons sugar. Add 1 1/2 cups self-rising flour and 1 cup milk and beat until smooth. Stir in 3 to 4 tablespoons melted oleo (margarine) and add vanilla to taste. Pour batter onto a preheated skillet or griddle and cook until bubbles form, then flip and cook until golden.

ID 269 — Speedy White Clam Sauce
Drain 1 can minced clams, reserving the liquid if you want extra clam flavor. Heat 1/2 cup olive oil in a skillet and lightly brown 2 minced garlic cloves. Add 1 tablespoon minced parsley, the clams, and salt and pepper to taste, then heat for about 2 minutes. Serve over cooked spaghetti.

ID 270 — Pineapple Cranberry Pie Filling Cook 3 cups cranberries with 1 1/2 cups crushed pineapple until the cranberries burst. Mix 1 1/4 cups sugar with 1 tablespoon flour, 3/4 teaspoon cinnamon, 1/2 teaspoon nutmeg, and 1/4 teaspoon salt, then stir into the fruit and cook until thickened. Cool slightly, pour into a 9-inch unbaked pie shell, and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 30 minutes.

ID 271 — Strawberry Yum-Yum
Melt 1 stick margarine and stir in 2 cups graham cracker crumbs. Press half of the crumb mixture into the bottom of a baking dish. Prepare 2 packages Dream Whip according to package directions, then beat it with 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese, 1 cup sugar, and 1 cup cold milk until smooth. Spread half the cream mixture over the crumbs, layer on 2 cups strawberries, then spread the remaining cream mixture over the strawberries. Top with the remaining crumbs and chill at least 3 hours before serving.

ID 272 — Blueberry Cream Pie
Beat 1 cup sour cream with 2 tablespoons flour, 3/4 cup sugar, 1 teaspoon vanilla extract, 3/4 teaspoon salt, and 1 beaten egg for about 5 minutes until smooth. Fold in 2 1/2 cups fresh blueberries, then pour into 1 unbaked 9-inch pastry shell. For the topping, cut together 3 tablespoons flour with 3 tablespoons softened butter and 3 tablespoons chopped black walnuts, then sprinkle over the pie. Bake at 400°F (about 200°C) for about 25 minutes.

ID 273 — Western Style Barbecue
Brown 4 frankfurters cut into 1-inch pieces in 2 tablespoons butter in a saucepan. Add 1 can (19 1/4 oz) Campbell’s chunky old fashioned beans with ham soup, 1 can (12 oz) whole kernel golden corn with sweet peppers (drained), 1 can (8 oz) lima beans (drained), and 1/2 cup barbecue sauce. Heat through, stirring occasionally, and garnish with green pepper rings if desired; this makes about 5 cups.

ID 274 — Lemon Jell-O Cheese Cake
Dissolve 1 package lemon Jell-O in 1 cup boiling water, then stir in 3 tablespoons lemon juice and cool slightly.
