In another bowl, beat 1 package (8 oz) cream cheese with 1 cup sugar, 1 small can drained crushed pineapple, and 2 teaspoons vanilla. Whip 1 large can Milnot until stiff. Crush 2 packages graham crackers and mix with 1/2 cup oleo (1 stick melted) and press half into the bottom of a pan. Combine the cream cheese mixture with the Jell-O mixture, fold in the whipped Milnot, and pour over the crust. Top with the remaining graham cracker crumbs and chill several hours.

ID 275 — Angel Food Cake
Sift together 1 cup sifted cake flour and 1 1/2 cups sugar four times. Beat 1 1/2 cups egg whites (about 12 whites) until foamy, add 1 1/2 teaspoons cream of tartar and 3/4 teaspoon salt, and beat until soft peaks form. Gradually add the remaining sugar, then add 1 teaspoon vanilla and 1/2 teaspoon almond flavoring. Fold in the flour mixture gently. Pour into an ungreased angel food cake pan and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) until it springs back lightly when touched, about 35 to 45 minutes, then cool upside down.

ID 276 — Plum Nutty Cake
Mix 2 cups self-rising flour with 2 cups sugar, then stir in 1 cup oil, 2 jars strained plum baby food, 3 eggs, 1 teaspoon cinnamon, 1 teaspoon allspice, and 1 cup pecans broken into small pieces. Pour into a greased pan and bake at 300°F (about 150°C) for about 1 hour, or until done.

ID 277 — Pinto Bean Pie
Mix 3 cups sugar with 2 sticks melted margarine, then stir in 1 cup mashed pinto beans, 4 beaten eggs, and 1 tablespoon vanilla. Pour into 3 unbaked pie shells and bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 35 minutes.

ID 278 — Speedy Little Devils
Combine 1 devil’s food cake mix with 1 stick melted oleo (margarine) until crumbly. Reserve 1 1/4 cups of crumbs for topping, then press the rest into an ungreased 13x9-inch pan. Spread 3/4 cup peanut butter mixed with 1 jar (7 oz) marshmallow cream evenly over the base, then crumble the reserved cake mixture over the top. Bake at 350°F (about 175°C) for about 20 minutes, cool completely, and cut into bars (about 3 dozen).

ID 279 — Martha Washington Candy
Mix 1 box confectioners sugar with 1 can Eagle Brand sweetened condensed milk and 1 teaspoon vanilla, then stir in 7 oz coconut until thick and add pecans as desired. Chill or freeze the mixture for 2 to 3 hours until very firm, then roll into balls, dusting and rolling with the second box of confectioners sugar. For the coating, melt 1/2 to 3/4 block paraffin with 1 box Baker’s semi-sweet chocolate, then dip the candy balls and let set.

ID 280 — 24 Hour Salad
In a large bowl, layer 1 head lettuce (chopped), 1 cup chopped celery, 1 cup cauliflower pieces, 1 cup frozen peas, and 1 cup chopped onion. Sprinkle 1/2 cup bacon bits over the top. Mix 2 cups mayonnaise with 3 tablespoons sugar and spread it evenly over the salad, sealing the surface so it stays fresh. Cover and refrigerate overnight, then sprinkle 1 package shredded Swiss cheese on top just before serving.

ID 281 — Rocky Road Fudge
Grease an 8x8-inch pan. In a saucepan over low heat, melt 1/2 cup margarine, then stir in 2/3 cup unsweetened cocoa, 1/2 cup light corn syrup, 1 tablespoon water, and 1 teaspoon vanilla until smooth. Remove from heat and gradually beat in 1 lb confectioners sugar until smooth. Stir in 1 cup miniature marshmallows and 1/2 cup chopped nuts, spread into the pan, cover, and refrigerate until firm before cutting.

ID 282 — Ice Cream
Beat 2 eggs with 2 cups sugar, 1 can Eagle Brand sweetened condensed milk, 1/2 pint cream, 2 teaspoons vanilla, and a pinch of salt using an electric mixer. Stir in 2 quarts milk, pour into an ice cream freezer, and freeze according to your machine’s directions (the original recipe simply says “put in freezer,” but an ice-cream maker gives the intended result).

ID 283 — No-Bake Persimmon Pudding
Mix 1 cup persimmon pulp with 1 cup powdered sugar, then stir in 1/2 cup chopped peanuts and 1/2 cup miniature marshmallows. Add 2 cups graham cracker crumbs and mix until the mixture holds together. Shape into a roll, adding more crumbs if needed, then chill thoroughly and serve sliced with whipped cream.

ID 284 — Fruitcake Cookies
Cream 1 cup light brown sugar (the ingredient list does not specify butter, but the directions say “cream butter and sugar,” so use about 1/2 cup softened butter) until fluffy, then beat in 3 eggs. Mix in 3 cups self-rising flour, 1 teaspoon cinnamon, and 1/2 cup milk, then fold in 2 lb candied fruit (or use 6 slices candied pineapple plus 2 cups candied cherries) and 3 to 4 cups pecans. Drop by teaspoonfuls onto a cookie sheet and bake at 300°F (about 150°C) for 20 to 30 minutes.

ID 285 — Chicken And Tortilla Casserole Boil 1 medium chicken until cooked, remove bones and cut meat into pieces. Add 1 large chopped onion and 1 large chopped green pepper. Mix together 1 can mushroom soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can tomatoes and green chilies, 1/2 teaspoon chili powder and 1/2 teaspoon garlic salt. Dip 12 soft tortillas in chicken broth and place in a buttered 9 x 12-inch baking dish. Layer tortillas, half the chicken, half the soup mixture and half of 1 pound grated Cheddar cheese. Repeat layers and bake at 350°F for 30 to 40 minutes until cheese is melted.

ID 286 — Fruit Pizza Press 1 tube refrigerated sugar cookie dough evenly onto a 13-inch pizza pan or cookie sheet and bake according to package directions. Cream together 8 ounces softened cream cheese with 1/2 cup powdered sugar and spread over cooled crust. Top with assorted sliced fresh or canned fruit and sprinkle with coconut to make one pizza.

ID 287 — Harvard Beets Melt 2 tablespoons butter or margarine and stir in 2 tablespoons flour. Gradually add 1/4 cup boiling water, cooking and stirring until thickened. Add 1/4 cup vinegar, 1/3 cup brown sugar, 1/2 teaspoon salt, 1/8 teaspoon pepper and 1/8 teaspoon ground cloves, mixing until sugar dissolves. Add 2 1/2 cups diced cooked beets and cook until thoroughly heated.

ID 288 — Clam Chowder Dice 6 to 8 slices lean bacon and 1 cup onion and sauté in a soup pot. Add 2 cups diced cooked potatoes, 2 cans minced clams with 1 cup reserved clam juice, 2 cups half-and-half, 1 cup water, 2 tablespoons butter, and salt and pepper to taste. Heat gently without boiling and thicken if desired.

ID 289 — Easy Cranberry Relish In a food processor combine 2 small packages fresh cranberries, 1 cup sugar and 1 whole orange cut into pieces. Process until chopped, transfer to a bowl, stir in chopped walnuts, chill and serve.

ID 290 — Banana Omelette Melt 3 tablespoons butter in a skillet and sauté 4 sliced bananas for about 5 minutes, turning frequently, then set aside. Beat 6 egg yolks with 1/2 teaspoon salt, a dash of cayenne pepper and 1/4 cup milk. Beat egg whites until stiff and fold together with yolks. Pour into a buttered 7 x 10-inch casserole, arrange bananas on top and bake at 350°F for 20 minutes until lightly browned. Sprinkle with chopped parsley and serve.

ID 291 — Taco Soup Brown 1 pound hamburger with 1 chopped onion and drain. Add 1/2 package dry taco seasoning, 1 can kidney beans, 1 can butter beans, 1 can tomatoes, 1 small can tomato sauce and 1 can tomato juice or V-8 juice. Simmer for 20 minutes and serve with Cheddar cheese, sour cream, crushed corn chips and chopped avocado, letting each person add their own toppings.

ID 292 — Frosty Pudding Cones In a bowl mix 2/3 cup sweetened condensed milk with 2 tablespoons lemon juice. Add 8 ounces fruit yogurt and mix well. Spoon mixture into 6 sugar cones, stand upright in glasses and freeze for 3 hours. Top each cone with 1 tablespoon whipped cream before serving.

ID 293 — Easy Marinade Mix together 1/2 cup soy sauce, 1/4 cup oil, 1/4 cup red wine vinegar, 1 teaspoon oregano, 1 teaspoon basil, 1 teaspoon minced onion and 1/4 teaspoon pepper. Pour over chicken and marinate for at least 1 hour or overnight for juicier results.

ID 294 — Pina Colada Muffins Prepare 1 box yellow cake mix according to package directions using an electric mixer. Stir in 1 teaspoon coconut flavoring, 1 teaspoon rum flavoring, 1 cup coconut, 1/2 cup chopped nuts and 1 cup drained crushed pineapple. Pour into greased or lined muffin pans and bake at 350°F for 15 to 20 minutes. Frost with cream cheese frosting if desired.

ID 295 — Oriental Tossed Salad Mix together 3/4 cup sugar, 1/2 cup red wine vinegar, 1 cup oil and 3 tablespoons soy sauce. Just before serving add 2 packages crushed ramen noodles, 1 cup chopped walnuts, 1 bunch chopped green onions, 1 bunch broccoli florets and 2 packages romaine lettuce. Toss well and serve.

ID 296 — Applesauce Cake Beat together 1/2 cup white sugar, 2 cups brown sugar and 1/2 cup oil. Add 2 eggs and beat again, then mix in 2 cups applesauce, 1 cup ground raisins, 2 teaspoons soda, 1/2 teaspoon salt and 2 1/2 cups flour. Stir in 1/2 cup walnuts or pecans and bake in a 13 x 18-inch pan at 350°F until done.

ID 297 — Mayonnaise Lightly mix 1 egg yolk, then add 1 pint oil a drop at a time until the mixture thickens, then continue adding oil slowly. Stir in juice of 1/2 lemon and 1 teaspoon honey and store refrigerated.

ID 298 — Shepherd’s Pie Fry 1 pound hamburger with 1/4 cup chopped onion until browned and drain. Season with 1/4 teaspoon salt and 1/8 teaspoon pepper. Spoon into a 1-quart casserole, top with 1 cup mashed potatoes, dot with butter and sprinkle with paprika. Bake at 425°F for 15 minutes.

ID 299 — Fresh Apple Cake Mix together 3 cups chopped raw apples, 2 cups flour, 2 cups sugar, 1/2 cup shortening, 2 eggs, 1/2 teaspoon salt, 1 teaspoon baking soda, 2 teaspoons vanilla, 1/2 teaspoon nutmeg, 1/2 teaspoon cinnamon and 1 cup chopped nuts. Bake in a greased and floured 13 x 9-inch pan at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 300 — Brown Rice Pizza (Light) Combine 1 1/2 cups cooked brown rice, 1/2 cup shredded part-skim mozzarella, 1 beaten egg and 1/2 teaspoon oregano. Press into a Pam-sprayed 12-inch pizza pan and bake at 400°F for 25 minutes. Sauté 1 cup broccoli florets, 1 cup sliced zucchini, 1 cup sliced mushrooms and 1 small sliced onion in a Pam-coated skillet until tender. Mix 8 ounces tomato sauce with remaining oregano, spread over crust, top with vegetables and remaining 1 cup cheese and bake 10 minutes until heated through and cheese melts.

ID 301 — Creamy Shells With Broccoli And Ham Cook 1 (1 lb.) box medium macaroni shells according to package directions. Sauté 1 crushed garlic clove, 1/2 lb. cooked ham cut into cubes and 1 (10 oz.) package frozen broccoli, thawed and cut, in 1/2 cup margarine for about 5 minutes until broccoli is tender. Stir in 1 cup heavy cream and cook 3 minutes, then add 1 cup grated Parmesan cheese and cook on low heat until melted. Drain shells and toss with sauce before serving.

ID 302 — Chicken Over Rice Boil 1 chopped onion, 2 chopped bell peppers, 1/2 bunch celery, 2 chopped potatoes and 1 can chicken broth until tender, seasoning lightly with soy sauce and thickening with a small amount of cornstarch if desired. Serve hot over cooked rice.

ID 303 — Meatball Chop Suey Mix 2 lb. ground beef with 1/2 cup bread crumbs, 1 cup milk, 2/3 cup chopped onion, 1 egg, 1 tsp. salt and 1/8 tsp. pepper, shape into about 24 meatballs and brown in 3 Tbsp. lard or drippings. Dissolve 2 beef bouillon cubes in 3 cups hot water and add to meatballs with remaining onion, 1/4 cup soy sauce and 2 cups celery strips, simmer 15 minutes. Remove meatballs, thicken sauce with 3 Tbsp. cornstarch mixed with 2 Tbsp. cold water, add 2 cups bean sprouts and 1 cup mushroom stems and serve with meatballs over rice or chow mein noodles.

ID 304 — Vegetable Beef Soup Place 1 lb. cooked and drained ground beef, 1 large can whole tomatoes, 1 can tomato soup and 1 chopped small onion in crock-pot. Add 2 cups water, 1 package frozen mixed vegetables, 1 cup cooked diced potatoes, 1 cup diced celery, 1/4 tsp. salt and 1/4 tsp. pepper. Stir well and cook on low 4 to 6 hours.

ID 305 — Hawaiian Marshmallow Pie Microwave 24 large marshmallows or 3 cups miniature marshmallows with 1/2 cup reserved pineapple liquid until smooth, stirring halfway. Chill 30 minutes, then fold in 2 cans (8 oz. each) drained crushed pineapple and 2 cups thawed Cool Whip. Pour into 1 prepared 6 oz. graham cracker crust and refrigerate several hours or overnight.

ID 306 — Sugar-Free Sweet-N-Sour Stir-Fry Heat 1 tsp. vegetable oil in skillet and cook 2 stalks sliced celery, 1 head shredded cabbage, 3 sliced carrots, 1 chopped onion and 2 sliced zucchini for 2 minutes, then add 1/2 cup water chestnuts and 1/4 cup chopped green pepper. Cook until crisp-tender and stir in prepared sugar-free sweet-and-sour sauce.

ID 307 — Graham Cracker Bars Preheat oven to 350°F and grease pan. Line bottom with graham crackers. Melt together 1 stick butter and 1 stick margarine, add 1/2 cup sugar and boil 2 minutes, remove from heat, stir in chopped pecans to taste, pour over crackers and bake 6 minutes on bottom rack.

ID 308 — Red Cabbage Sauté 1 chopped onion in 3 Tbsp. bacon drippings or olive oil until tender. Add 1 large shredded red cabbage and sauté 10 minutes, then add 2 chopped cooking apples, 1/2 cup wine vinegar, 1 Tbsp. sugar and 1 tsp. salt. Cover and simmer 2 hours, stir occasionally, add 1/2 jar currant jelly and simmer 30 minutes more.

ID 309 — Ambrosia Salad Drain 1 can chunk pineapple, 1 can mandarin oranges and 1 small jar maraschino cherries, combine with 1 container sour cream, 1 small package miniature marshmallows and 1 can flaked coconut, mix well and refrigerate before serving.

ID 310 — Sour Cream Pound Cake Cream together 3 cups sugar, 2 sticks margarine and 1/4 cup Crisco. Add 6 eggs one at a time, beating on low speed. Mix in 3 cups sifted cake flour, 8 oz. sour cream and 1 tsp. vanilla and bake at 325°F for about 1 hour and 15 minutes.

ID 311 — Soft Delicious Pumpkin Bars Mix together 2 cups flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. soda, 1/2 tsp. salt, 2 tsp. cinnamon, 2 cups sugar, 1 cup oil, 4 eggs, 2 cups pumpkin and 1 cup nuts. Pour into pan and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 312 — Barbecue Sauce Combine 1 can tomato sauce, 1/4 cup brown sugar, 1/4 cup vinegar, 1/2 cup minced onion, salt and pepper to taste and 1 tsp. garlic powder. Simmer over medium heat 5 to 8 minutes.

ID 313 — Sausage Strata Arrange 6 slices crustless bread in greased 10 x 6-inch dish. Brown and drain 1 1/2 lb. sausage and spoon over bread, sprinkle with 1 cup grated Swiss cheese. Mix 4 beaten eggs with 1 1/2 cups milk, 3/4 cup light cream, 1/2 tsp. salt, a dash of pepper, a dash of nutmeg and 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, pour over all and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 314 — Pepperoni Spaghetti Cook 1 chopped large onion, 1 chopped green pepper, 1 lb. ground beef and 1 (3 oz.) package chopped pepperoni until beef is browned. Add 1 (32 oz.) jar spaghetti sauce with mushrooms and simmer 20 minutes. Serve over cooked 12 oz. spaghetti and top with 1 cup shredded mozzarella and 1 Tbsp. Parmesan cheese.

ID 315 — Florida Punch Bring 1 cup sugar and 2 cups water to a boil until sugar dissolves. Add 4 cups cranberry juice, 4 cups pineapple juice and 2 cups orange juice, chill and add 1 quart ginger ale just before serving.

ID 316 — “Peachy” Cake Beat 4 eggs, then add 3 cups flour, 1 cup oil, 3 tsp. vanilla, 2 cups sugar, 3 tsp. baking powder and 1/2 cup peach juice, beat until creamy. Layer batter and 1 (20–29 oz.) can drained sliced peaches with sugar and cinnamon in greased tube pan and bake at 350°F for 1 to 1 1/2 hours.

ID 317 — Fruity Ice Blend 2 peeled oranges, 2 peeled bananas, 2 cups crushed ice, 2 cups unsweetened applesauce and 1/2 tsp. cinnamon until smooth.

ID 318 — Five Way Chili Lightly brown 2 lb. ground beef, add 3 cups water, 1 (15 oz.) can tomato sauce, 2 bay leaves, 1/2 tsp. salt, 2 tsp. cumin, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 1/2 tsp. vinegar, 1 1/2 tsp. allspice and 2 Tbsp. chili powder and simmer uncovered 3 hours.

ID 319 — Hot Tomatoes And Cucumbers Sauté 2 sliced cucumbers and 1 sliced onion in 2 Tbsp. butter for 5 minutes, add 4 tomato wedges, season with 1/2 tsp. salt and dash of pepper, heat briefly and sprinkle with 1 Tbsp. fresh dill.

ID 320 — Fluffy White Icing Beat together 2 cups powdered sugar, 2 Tbsp. flour, 1 egg white, 1/2 cup Crisco, 1 Tbsp. butter and 1 tsp. vanilla, then slowly beat in 2 Tbsp. milk until fluffy.

ID 321 — Dishpan Cookies Cream 2 cups brown sugar, 2 cups granulated sugar, 2 cups oil and 4 eggs, add 1/4 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. salt, 4 cups flour and 1 1/2 cups oats, then mix in 2 cups coconut, 4 cups corn flakes, 6 oz. chocolate chips and 1 cup nuts. Drop on sheets and bake at 325°F for 10–12 minutes.

ID 322 — Toll House Pie Beat 2 eggs until foamy, add 1/2 cup flour, 1/2 cup sugar and 1/2 cup brown sugar, blend in 1 cup melted butter, stir in 6 oz. chocolate chips and 1 cup walnuts, pour into 9-inch pie shell and bake at 325°F for 1 hour.

ID 323 — Crunchy Onion Burger Mix 1 1/2 lb. ground beef with 2/3 cup French fried onions, 3/4 tsp. salt and 1/4 tsp. pepper, shape into 6 patties and grill or broil until done, serving on rolls topped with remaining onions.

ID 324 — Cheese Ball Mix 16 oz. softened cream cheese, 1 1/2 lb. grated Cheddar, 1 tsp. lemon juice, 2 tsp. grated onion, 1 tsp. dry mustard, 1 tsp. soy sauce, 1/2 tsp. paprika, 1/2 tsp. salt and 2 Tbsp. parsley. Chill, shape into ball, roll in chopped pecans and refrigerate overnight.

ID 325 — Pumpkin Squares Combine 1 cup flour, 1/2 cup oats, 1/2 cup brown sugar and 1/2 cup butter, press into 13 x 9-inch pan and bake 15 minutes at 350°F. Mix 1 can pumpkin, 1 can evaporated milk, 2 eggs, 3/4 cup sugar, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1/2 tsp. ginger and 1/4 tsp. cloves, pour over crust and bake 20 minutes. Top with mixture of 1/2 cup nuts, 1/2 cup brown sugar and 2 Tbsp. butter and bake 15–20 minutes more.

ID 326 — Old Time Buttermilk Pie Cream 1/2 cup butter and 2 cups sugar, beat in 3 rounded tsp. flour and 3 eggs, stir in 1 cup buttermilk, 1 tsp. vanilla and dash nutmeg, pour into 9-inch unbaked shell and bake at 350°F for 45–50 minutes.

ID 327 — Two Sweet Potato Pies Boil and mash 4 large sweet potatoes, mix with 3 eggs, 1 cup sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla and 3/4 cup milk, pour into 9-inch pastry shell and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes, rest 15 minutes before serving.

ID 328 — Broccoli-Cauliflower Soup Cook 1 lb. broccoli and 1 lb. cauliflower in broth until tender. Sauté 1 diced onion in 1/2 cup butter, add 1/2 cup flour, slowly stir in 1 quart milk and cook gently until thick, combine with vegetables and serve with 1 cup grated sharp Cheddar and black pepper.

ID 329 — Fresh Apple Cake Mix 1 1/2 cups oil, 2 cups sugar, 2 beaten eggs, 3 cups chopped apples, 3 cups cake flour, 1 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. soda and 2 tsp. vanilla and bake in three 9-inch pans at 325°F for 25–30 minutes.

ID 330 — Russian Tea Mix 1 cup Tang, 1 cup sugar, 1/2 cup instant tea with lemon, 1/2 tsp. cloves and 1/2 tsp. cinnamon and use 1 heaping tablespoon per cup of hot water.

ID 331 — Hunter’s Delight Melt 1 Tbsp. butter, sauté 1 Tbsp. onion, add 1 1/2 lb. ground beef, 2 tsp. salt and 1/4 tsp. pepper and brown. Stir in 1 (20 oz.) can cream-style corn and 1/2 cup milk, pour over 1 quart sliced potatoes in casserole and bake uncovered at 375°F for about 1 1/2 hours.

ID 332 — Pie Crust (Never Fail) Cut 1 1/4 cups shortening into 3 cups flour and 1 tsp. salt, mix 1 beaten egg with 5 Tbsp. water and 1 Tbsp. vinegar, add to flour mixture, blend just until moistened and bake at 450°F for 10 minutes.

ID 333 — Burnt Caramel Cake Icing Heat 2 cups sugar, 3/4 cup milk and 1 Tbsp. white Karo syrup in saucepan, caramelize 1/2 cup sugar separately with water, combine and cook to soft-ball stage, beat until spreadable, adding butter and flavoring if desired.

ID 334 — Chicken Sweet-Sour Place cut-up chicken in baking dish, mix 1 jar apricot preserves, 1 bottle Catalina dressing and 1 envelope dry onion soup and pour over chicken, bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 hours.

ID 335 — Microwave Fudge Microwave 2 cups semi-sweet chocolate chips, 1 cup sweet chocolate chips and 1 can condensed milk for 3 minutes, stir in 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla and optional nuts and pour into pan.

ID 336 — Breakfast Rolls Place 1/2 cup chopped nuts in greased Bundt pan, top with 1 bag frozen dinner rolls, sprinkle with 1 (3 5/8 oz.) package butterscotch pudding, boil 1/2 cup butter, 3/4 cup brown sugar and 3/4 tsp. cinnamon and pour over, rest overnight and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 337 — Kentucky Cream Candy Beat 8 oz. cream cheese with 1/4 tsp. salt and 1 tsp. vanilla, gradually add 6 cups confectioners sugar, chill, shape into balls and roll in coconut.

ID 338 — Thousand Island Dressing Mix 4 cups Miracle Whip, 1 can tomato soup, 1 Tbsp. vinegar, 4 Tbsp. sweet relish, 2 Tbsp. chili sauce, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 1 Tbsp. dry mustard, 1 grated onion and 1 grated garlic clove.

ID 339 — Rolls Scald 1 cup milk with 1 stick butter, cool slightly, add 1/3 cup sugar and 1 tsp. salt, then 2 eggs, dissolved yeast cake and 4 1/2 cups flour, mix, refrigerate overnight, shape and bake.

ID 340 — Brownies Mix 1 1/2 cups white sugar, 1 1/2 cups brown sugar, 4 Tbsp. cocoa, 2 cups flour, 6 eggs, 1 1/2 sticks melted oleo, 1/2 cup milk, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1/4 tsp. salt and 1/2 cup nuts, bake at 350°F for 23 minutes.

ID 341 — Diabetic Cookies Mix 1 1/2 cups unsweetened applesauce, 3/4 cup margarine, 2 eggs, 1 Tbsp. vanilla and 1/3 cup brown Sugar Twin, add 2 cups oatmeal, 1 1/2 cups flour, 1 1/2 tsp. soda, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1 Tbsp. cinnamon, 1/2 tsp. allspice, 1 cup raisins and 1/4 cup nuts and bake at 375°F for 15 minutes.

ID 342 — Chocolate-Dipped Strawberries Microwave 2 oz. semi-sweet chocolate with 1/2 Tbsp. whipping cream until melted, stir in dash almond extract, dip 8 strawberries and chill until set.

ID 343 — Working Mother’s “Mess” Brown 1 lb. ground beef and drain, stir in 1–3 Tbsp. tamari, sauté 1 cup chopped onions, 2–3 tomatoes and 1–3 garlic cloves, add 16 oz. chunky spaghetti sauce and 1 (16 oz.) can cooked beans, combine with meat and simmer.

ID 344 — Chicken With Tarragon Lightly brown 4 skinless chicken breasts, place in skillet meat-side down, add bouillon water to cover, top with 1/2 cup finely chopped onion and 1/2 tsp. tarragon, cover and simmer 30–45 minutes.

ID 345 — Lemon Jello Vegetable Salad Dissolve 1 box lemon gelatin in 1 cup hot water, add 3/4 cup cold water, let thicken slightly then stir in 1/2 cup grated cabbage, 1/2 cup chopped celery, 1/4 cup grated carrot, 1/8 cup chopped green pepper and 1/2 cup pineapple tidbits and chill until set.

ID 346 — Shrimp Batter Mix 1 cup flour, 1/2 tsp. cornstarch, 1/2 tsp. soda, 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1 beaten egg, 1/2–1 cup cold water and paprika and use to coat shrimp for deep frying.

ID 347 — Chicken-Cheese Ball Mix 1 small can chicken, 8 oz. softened cream cheese, 1 Tbsp. minced onion, 2 Tbsp. soy sauce, 1 Tbsp. mayonnaise, form into ball, roll in chopped pecans and garnish with cherry if desired.

ID 348 — Salted Nut Squares Spread 1 1/2 cups salted peanuts in 11 x 7-inch pan, melt 3 Tbsp. butter with 2 cups peanut butter chips, add 1 can condensed milk and 2 cups miniature marshmallows, pour over peanuts, top with remaining peanuts and chill.

ID 349 — Date Cake Sprinkle 1 package chopped dates with 1 tsp. baking soda and 1 cup hot water, cool, cream 1/2 cup margarine with 1 cup sugar and 1 egg, add 1 1/2 cups flour, 1/2 tsp. salt and 1/2 cup walnuts, pour into 8 x 8-inch pan and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 350 — Crescent Cake Mix 1 package yellow cake mix, 1 stick margarine, 1 beaten egg and 1/2 cup chopped nuts and press into 9 x 10-inch pan, beat 1 box confectioners sugar with 8 oz. cream cheese and 2 eggs, pour over base and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 351 — Freezer Pie Crust Combine 3 lb. shortening, 5 lb. flour and 2 Tbsp. salt in a very large bowl. Mix 3 cups water with 1 cup white syrup, add to dry ingredients and mix well. Divide into crust-size balls, wrap and freeze; makes about 20–24 crusts.

ID 352 — Basic Graham Cracker Crust Process 1 1/3 cups graham cracker crumbs and 1/4 cup sugar until fine, add 5 Tbsp. melted unsalted butter and mix until moist. Press into a 9-inch pie pan and bake at 375°F for 8 minutes until lightly browned.

ID 353 — Creamy Chicken And Mushrooms Brown 4 skinless boneless chicken breasts in 1 Tbsp. margarine for 10 minutes and remove. In remaining 1 Tbsp. margarine sauté 1 1/2 cups sliced mushrooms, 1 small sliced onion and 1/8 tsp. garlic powder until tender. Add 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1/2 cup milk, 2 Tbsp. dry sherry (optional) and 1/8 tsp. pepper, bring to boil, return chicken, cover and cook on low 5 minutes.

ID 354 — Sweet And Sour Red Cabbage Boil 1 head shredded red cabbage in salted water until just tender, drain and add 1 chopped onion glazed in pan. Stir in 1 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. pepper, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 1/2 cup cider vinegar and caraway seed to taste, stirring until cabbage becomes limp, then serve hot.

ID 355 — Hot Rolls Dissolve 1 pkg. dry yeast in 1/2 cup warm water. Mix remaining 1 cup warm water with 3 1/2 tsp. sugar, 1 tsp. salt and 3 tsp. melted Crisco. Add yeast mixture and knead in 4 cups flour. Let rise until doubled, shape rolls, rise again and bake until browned.

ID 356 — Chicken Casserole Spread 1 1/2 cups uncooked rice in a 9 x 13-inch dish, sprinkle with 1 envelope onion soup mix, top with 8 chicken pieces, spoon over 1 can cream of mushroom soup and pour 1 1/2 cups hot water around chicken. Cover and bake at 325°F for 1 1/2 hours, uncovering last 30 minutes.

ID 357 — Raisin Walnut Shortbread Bars Mix 1 1/4 cups flour and 1/2 cup sugar, cut in 1/2 cup butter until crumbly, press into greased 8-inch pan and bake at 350°F for 20 minutes. Beat 2 eggs with 1/2 cup brown sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla and 1/8 tsp. baking soda, stir in 1 cup walnuts, 1 cup raisins and optional 1/2 cup coconut, spread over crust and bake until set.

ID 358 — Pineapple Parfait Pie Heat 3/4 cup pineapple liquid with water to boiling, remove from heat and dissolve 1 pkg. lemon Jell-O. Add 1 pint vanilla ice cream until melted, chill until thickened, fold in crushed pineapple and pour into baked 9-inch pie shell. Chill until firm and top with Cool Whip.

ID 359 — Cherry Supreme Mix 2 cups graham cracker crumbs with 1/4 cup sugar and 1 stick melted butter, press into pan and cool. Blend 1 pkg. cream cheese, 1/2 cup powdered sugar and 1 small tub Cool Whip, spread over crust and top with 1 can cherry pie filling, refrigerate overnight.

ID 360 — Red Beet Cake Mix 1 1/2 cups sugar, 3 eggs, 1 1/2 cups mashed cooked beets, 1 cup Crisco oil, 2 squares melted unsweetened chocolate, 1 1/3 cups flour, 1 1/3 tsp. soda, 1/2 tsp. salt and 1 tsp. vanilla and bake at 350°F for 25–35 minutes.

ID 361 — Reuben Casserole Spread 1 (7 oz.) can drained sauerkraut in baking dish, top with 1 sliced tomato, 2 Tbsp. Thousand Island dressing and 4 oz. chopped corned beef. Sprinkle with 3/4 cup Swiss cheese and 1/8 tsp. caraway seed, top with 1 cup rye bread crumbs tossed with 1 Tbsp. butter and bake uncovered at 375°F for 20–25 minutes.

ID 362 — Potato Casserole Mix 16 oz. sour cream, 16 oz. Cheez Whiz, 2 Tbsp. minced onions and 1 Tbsp. dried parsley, fold in 4 lb. boiled sliced potatoes and 1 lb. diced precooked sausage. Pour into pan and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 363 — Carrot-Pineapple Bread Mix 3 beaten eggs, 2 cups sugar, 1 cup oil, 1 small can crushed pineapple, 2 tsp. vanilla, 1 cup grated carrots, 1 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. soda, 1/4 tsp. salt, 3 cups flour and 1 cup chopped nuts and bake at 350°F for 1 hour in two loaf pans.

ID 364 — Easy Chicken And Dumplings Layer 1 cooked chopped chicken in casserole and pour over 1/4 stick melted butter. Mix 1 cup self-rising flour with 1 cup milk and pour over chicken. Combine 1 can chicken soup with 2 cups chicken broth, pour over top, smooth gently and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 365 — Delicious Scalloped Potatoes (Without Cheese) Slice 6 peeled potatoes thinly and layer in casserole with 3/4 stick margarine, salt and pepper. Pour 2 cans evaporated milk over potatoes to cover and bake uncovered at 475°F for about 1 hour.

ID 366 — Peanut Butter Oat Cookies Cream 1/2 cup butter and 1 cup brown sugar, add 1/2 cup corn syrup and 1 tsp. salt, mix in 4 cups oats and bake in greased 13 x 9-inch pan at 350°F for 15 minutes. Spread 1/2 cup peanut butter over warm base, melt 1/2 cup chocolate chips with 1 1/2 tsp. butter and drizzle on top, cool and cut.

ID 367 — Cherry Salad Mix 2 cans cherry pie filling, 1 can crushed pineapple with juice, 1/2 cup pecans, 1 cup miniature marshmallows, 1 large container Cool Whip and 1 can sweetened condensed milk and refrigerate 1 hour.

ID 368 — Scalloped Oysters Layer 1 pint oysters with 2 cups cracker crumbs mixed with 1/2 cup melted butter, seasoning with 1/2 tsp. salt and dash pepper. Combine 3/4 cup cream, 1/4 cup oyster liquid and 1/4 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, pour over and bake at 350°F for 40 minutes.

ID 369 — Pie Crust Cut 2/3 cup shortening and 2 Tbsp. butter into 2 cups flour and 1 tsp. salt, add 1/4 cup cold water gradually, form dough, divide for two crusts and bake shells at 475°F for 8 minutes if pre-baking.

ID 370 — Oatmeal Cake Pour 1 1/2 cups boiling water over 1 cup oatmeal and cool 20 minutes. Add 1/2 cup butter, 1 cup white sugar, 1 cup brown sugar, 2 eggs, 1 1/2 cups flour, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. baking powder and 1 tsp. vanilla, bake at 350°F for 35–40 minutes.

ID 371 — Candle Salad Place lettuce leaf on plate, top with pineapple slice, stand 1/2 banana upright in center, spoon on mayonnaise and top with a cherry.

ID 372 — Salmon Croquettes Mix 1 can pink salmon, 1 1/2 cups mashed potatoes, 1 grated onion, 1 egg and 1/2 tsp. pepper, form into 8 patties, coat with 1/4 cup bread crumbs and fry in 3 Tbsp. oil until golden.

ID 373 — Croquettes (Chicken, Fish Or Meat) Mix 2 cups chopped cooked meat, 1 cup croquette sauce, 1 egg, 3/4 cup breadcrumbs, salt and pepper, chill if needed, shape and cook as desired.

ID 374 — Corn Relish Boil 1 large can corn, 6 chopped onions, 1 chopped celery stalk, 1 pint vinegar, 3 chopped red peppers, 3 chopped green peppers, 2 cups sugar, 1 tsp. turmeric, 1 Tbsp. dry mustard, 1 Tbsp. celery salt and 2 Tbsp. salt uncovered for 15 minutes, jar and process.

ID 375 — Flossie’s Gingerbread Mix 1/2 cup sugar, 1/2 cup shortening, 1 egg, 1 1/2 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. ginger, 1/2 tsp. salt, 2 1/2 cups flour, 1 cup hot water and 1 cup molasses and bake at 350°F.

ID 376 — Vanilla Wafer Cake Cream 2 sticks butter and 2 cups sugar, add 6 eggs one at a time, alternate 12 oz. crushed vanilla wafers with 1/2 cup milk, stir in 7 oz. coconut and 1 cup pecans, bake in greased tube pan until done.

ID 377 — Double Baked Potatoes Bake 6 potatoes at 350°F, halve and scoop centers. Mix with 1 diced onion, 1 lb. crumbled bacon, 1 1/2 cups diced ham, 1 1/2 cups cheese, 2 Tbsp. butter and 1/4 cup milk, refill shells and bake until hot.

ID 378 — Crabmeat Au Gratin Mix 1 can cream of shrimp soup, 1/2 can milk, 1 lb. crabmeat, 4 cups chopped celery, 1/2 cup green pepper, 2 chopped pimentos, 2 Tbsp. onion, 1/3 cup almonds and 4 chopped eggs, top with 1 cup Cheddar and buttered crumbs and bake at 350°F for 35 minutes.

ID 379 — Hobo Stew Brown 2 lb. ground beef, drain and add 1/4 cup catsup, 1/4 cup mustard, 1/4 cup barbecue sauce, 2 cans sliced potatoes, 2 cans pork and beans, 1 can corn and 2 Tbsp. onion flakes, simmer 15–20 minutes.

ID 380 — Lemon Crunch Bake crust of 1 stick butter, 1 cup flour and 1/2 cup pecans at 350°F, cool and top with mixture of 8 oz. cream cheese, 1 cup powdered sugar and Cool Whip, then layer lemon pudding made with 3 cups milk.

ID 381 — No Name Cake Beat 1 box butter recipe cake mix, 1 cup milk, 4 eggs and 3/4 cup oil, mix in 1 can coconut pecan icing and 1 cup pecans, bake in Bundt pan at 340°F for 45 minutes then 315°F for 25 minutes.

ID 382 — Gold Rush Brunch Prepare 1 pkg. potatoes O’Brien, make sauce with 1/4 cup butter, 1/4 cup flour and 2 cups milk, stir in 1 cup sour cream and potatoes, pour into pan, top with 8 slices Canadian bacon, bake 20 minutes, add 8 eggs and bake until set.

ID 383 — Pot Roast Season 5 lb. chuck roast with ginger, garlic salt, pepper and paprika, add 1 can tomato paste and cook slowly in iron pot until tender.

ID 384 — Ham Cheese Oven Omelet Beat 8 eggs with 1 cup milk and 1/2 tsp. seasoned salt, stir in 3 oz. chopped ham, 3 Tbsp. onion and 1 cup Cheddar cheese and bake at 325°F for 40–45 minutes.

ID 385 — Never Fail Rolls Mix 1 cup butter, 3/4 cup sugar, 1 cup boiling water, 1 cup lukewarm water, 2 pkgs. yeast, 2 beaten eggs, 1 tsp. salt and about 6 1/2 cups flour, refrigerate 2 hours, shape, rise and bake at 375°F for 18 minutes.

ID 386 — Taco Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground beef and drain, add 1 chopped onion, 1/2 tsp. garlic powder, 1 envelope taco seasoning and 8 oz. tomato sauce. Layer with 1 cup sour cream, 1 cup cottage cheese, 2 cups crushed tortilla chips and 2 cups shredded cheese and bake at 350°F.

ID 387 — Warm Crabmeat Dip Mix 1 can crab, 8 oz. cream cheese, 2 Tbsp. mayonnaise, 3 tsp. lemon juice, 3 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/16 tsp. garlic powder and 1 Tbsp. onion, bake at 400°F for 30 minutes topped with Parmesan.

ID 388 — Herb Butter Blend 2 Tbsp. mixed dried herbs with 1/2 cup margarine and chill overnight.

ID 389 — Good ’N Easy Yeast Rolls Heat 2/3 cup sugar, 1 cup shortening and 1 cup hot water, cool, add 2 pkgs. yeast dissolved in 1 cup warm water, 2 eggs and 6 cups flour with 1 tsp. salt, mix and rise.

ID 390 — Southwestern Skillet Cook 1 lb. ground beef with 1/2 cup onion, add 1 can tomatoes, 3/4 cup rice, 3 Tbsp. green pepper, 1/2 cup olives, chili powder, garlic salt, salt and 1 cup water, simmer 20 minutes and top with 1 cup Cheddar.

ID 391 — Delicious Baked Potato Dish Layer 4 thinly sliced potatoes with 2 Tbsp. butter, salt, 1/2 cup Cheddar cheese and 1 cup whipping cream, sprinkle with chives and bake at 450°F for 45 minutes.

ID 392 — Quick Cream Of Broccoli Soup Boil 3 cups milk with 10 oz. broccoli for 5 minutes, add 1 envelope chicken soup mix and 1 Tbsp. flour blended with remaining milk, simmer 10 minutes.

ID 393 — Cabbage Rolls Wilt 1 head cabbage, mix 1 lb. hamburger, 1 cup cooked rice, 1 egg, 1 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. pepper and onion, roll in leaves, add 1 can tomatoes and cook until tender.

ID 394 — Coconut Custard Pie Blend 4 eggs, 2 cups milk, 1/2 cup Bisquick, 1/3 cup oleo, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1 can coconut and 3/4 cup sugar and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 395 — Zucchini Pizzas Mix 3/4 cup spaghetti sauce with onions, pepper and oregano, top 24 zucchini slices with sauce, mushrooms and mixture of 1/2 cup mozzarella and 2 Tbsp. Parmesan and broil until bubbly.

ID 396 — School Girl Pickles (Sweet Spear) Soak 12 lb. cucumbers in salt water 2 weeks, rinse, soak in alum water 6 hours, heat vinegar to cover, drain, layer with 8 lb. sugar and spices and stand 3 days before jarring.

ID 397 — Earthquake Cake Sprinkle 1 cup coconut and 3/4 cup pecans in 13 x 9-inch pan, pour prepared German chocolate cake batter over, top with mixture of 8 oz. cream cheese, 1 stick butter and 3 cups powdered sugar and bake at 350°F until done.

ID 398 — Mayonnaise Cake Mix 2 cups flour, 4 Tbsp. cocoa, 1 cup sugar, pinch salt, 1 cup water with 2 tsp. soda and 1 cup mayonnaise and bake at 350°F for 20–35 minutes.

ID 399 — White Pear Cake Prepare 1 white cake mix, add 1 can undrained pear halves, 2 egg whites and 1 whole egg and bake as directed, adjusting for altitude if needed.

ID 400 — Party Pink Punch Blend 46 oz. pineapple juice, 1 cup sugar, 6 oz. frozen lemonade and 48 oz. cranberry juice, freeze, thaw to slush and add 2 liters chilled ginger ale before serving.

ID 401 — Country Style Beef And Macaroni Cook and drain 8 oz. macaroni. In a skillet, melt butter (amount not specified in the data) and cook beef (amount not specified in the data) with 2 medium sliced onions until the beef is browned; drain if needed. Stir in the cooked macaroni, 1 package (10 oz.) cooked and drained frozen peas, and salt and pepper to taste; mix well and heat through to serving temperature.

ID 402 — Peanut Butter Cream Pie Beat 3 oz. fat-free cream cheese with 2 Tbsp. skim milk and 1/2 cup reduced-fat peanut butter until smooth, then stir in 1 cup powdered sugar. Fold in 1 large container Cool Whip Lite, spoon into 1 low-fat baked pie shell, and refrigerate several hours until set.

ID 403 — Scalloped Corn Whisk 1 beaten egg with 1/2 cup milk, add 1 (8 3/4 oz.) can cream-style corn, 1 (7 oz.) can drained whole-kernel corn, and a dash of pepper; pour into a 1-quart casserole and bake at 350°F for about 35 minutes, until a knife inserted near the center comes out clean (makes about 4 servings).

ID 404 — Waldrop Banana Pudding Whisk 2 cups milk, 1 cup sugar, 1/2 cup flour, 2 eggs, 1 tsp. vanilla, and a pinch of salt until smooth; cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until thickened, then remove from heat and layer the warm pudding with sliced bananas (amount not specified) and vanilla wafers (amount not specified); serve warm or chilled.

ID 405 — Hungarian Goulash Brown 2 lb. cubed stew beef with 1 medium sliced onion and 1 small clove garlic in 1/4 cup shortening; drain. Stir in 1 1/2 cups water, 3/4 cup catsup, 2 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 Tbsp. packed brown sugar, 2 tsp. salt, 2 tsp. paprika, 1/2 tsp. dry mustard, and a dash of cayenne; bring to a boil, reduce heat, cover, and simmer 2 to 2 1/2 hours until tender (or cook on low in a slow cooker 8 to 9 hours). Shake together 1/4 cup cold water and 2 Tbsp. flour, stir gradually into the stew, bring to a boil stirring constantly, boil 1 minute, and serve over hot noodles.

ID 406 — Plain Pound Cake Mix 3 cups sugar, 3 cups Swans Down cake flour, 7 medium eggs, 1 cup milk, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. vanilla flavoring, 1 tsp. butternut flavoring, and 1 1/2 cups Crisco until well combined; pour into a pound-cake pan and bake at 300°F for about 1 1/2 hours.

ID 407 — Ham And Country Dumplings Boil a ham bone (amount not specified) in a large pot of water until flavorful; remove the bone, return any picked meat to the broth, and season with ham bouillon (amount not specified). Make dumplings by mixing flour (amount not specified) with 2 eggs and 1 cup cold water to form a dumpling dough/batter, then cook dumplings in the simmering ham broth until done (exact proportions and timing not specified in the data).

ID 408 — Broccoli Rice Casserole Sauté 1 chopped onion and 1 chopped celery rib in 1/2 stick butter until tender. Combine with 1 (10 oz.) package cooked, well-drained frozen broccoli, 2 1/2 cups cooked rice, 1 (10 3/4 oz.) can condensed cream of chicken soup, 4 oz. Cheez Whiz, a dash of Tabasco, and pepper to taste; pour into a greased 1 1/2-quart dish and bake at 350°F until hot and bubbly (time not specified); this is best made a day ahead and freezes well.

ID 409 — Buckeyes (Cookies) Melt 1 stick oleo and mix with 1 (18 oz.) jar crunchy peanut butter, 3 cups Rice Krispies, and 1 lb. powdered sugar; roll into small balls and place on wax paper. Melt 1 (12 oz.) bag chocolate chips with 1/2 stick paraffin wax, dip the balls, return to wax paper, and cool until set (makes about 120 pieces).

ID 410 — Broccoli-Raisin Salad Combine 1 bunch broccoli heads (chopped), 2 green onion stems (or 1/2 medium onion), 1/4 cup sunflower seeds, 1/2 cup raisins, and 6 fried-and-cooled bacon slices (crumbled). Mix 1/2 cup mayonnaise with 2 Tbsp. vinegar and 1/8 cup sugar, toss with the salad (dressing step implied by ingredients; the data’s instruction line is truncated).

ID 411 — Low-Fat “French Fries” Heat oven to 425°F. Cut 1 1/2 to 2 lb. baking potatoes into 2-inch strips (peeled or unpeeled). Toss in a container with 1 to 1 1/2 Tbsp. olive oil and 1/8 to 1/4 tsp. cayenne, then season with 1/3 to 1/2 tsp. garlic powder and 1/4 to 1/2 tsp. salt; coat a baking sheet with nonstick cooking spray, spread potatoes out, and bake until crisp and browned (baking time not specified in the data).

ID 412 — Chicken Pot Pie Grease a shallow 2-quart dish and add 3 cups cooked diced chicken plus 1 small package frozen Veg-All. Mix 1 cup chicken broth with 1 cup cream of celery soup, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. pepper; pour over chicken. Stir 1 cup self-rising flour with 1 cup milk and 1/2 cup melted margarine until smooth, pour over the filling, and bake at 400°F for 40 to 50 minutes.

ID 413 — Old-Time Bread Pudding Grease a 1 1/2-quart baking dish and place 4 slices buttered toast cut into quarters inside; sprinkle with 1/3 cup seedless raisins. Mix 2 slightly beaten eggs with 1/4 cup sugar, 1/8 tsp. salt, 1 cup Pet milk, 1 cup boiling water, and 1 tsp. vanilla; pour over toast and let stand 10 minutes. Sprinkle with 4 tsp. sugar mixed with 1/4 tsp. cinnamon and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes, until a knife inserted in the center comes out clean (about 4 servings).

ID 414 — Original Mayfair Dressing In a blender, blend 1 (2 oz.) can anchovies, 1 Tbsp. black pepper, 1 Tbsp. Accent, 2 celery stalks, 1 medium onion, 1/4 cup mustard, 1 1/2 cloves garlic, and 1 tsp. lemon juice until smooth. Add 3 eggs one at a time, blending after each, then slowly blend in 2 cups Mazola oil a little at a time until thick and creamy (makes about 1 quart).

ID 415 — Apple Cake Beat 3 eggs with 2 cups sugar and 1 1/4 cups oil. Add 3 cups flour, 1 tsp. soda, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/2 tsp. cinnamon; stir in 2 cups chopped apples, 1 cup pecans, and 1 cup coconut. Bake at 375°F for 25 to 35 minutes.

ID 416 — Cheeseburger Pie Brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1 Tbsp. onions, 1 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, and 3/4 tsp. Italian seasoning; drain. Stir in 1 (6 oz.) can tomato paste, spread over 1 pizza crust, top with 8 oz. shredded mozzarella, and bake at 375°F for 10 to 15 minutes.

ID 417 — Fried Cabbage Chop 1 head cabbage, 1 onion, 1 bell pepper, and 1 ripe tomato, then mix with 2 Tbsp. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 tsp. pepper and let stand at least 1 hour. Heat 3 Tbsp. oil (amount appears in directions, not ingredients list) in a skillet, drain vegetables, add to skillet with 1/2 cup water (amount appears in directions, not ingredients list), and cook 20 to 30 minutes.

ID 418 — Jello Salad (Almost Like a Dessert) Heat 1 cup water with pineapple juice (from 1 No. 2 can crushed pineapple, drained) and 12 large marshmallows until dissolved. Stir in 1 package lemon gelatin and 1 package orange gelatin until dissolved; cool at room temperature until almost set. Fold in drained crushed pineapple, 1 cup grated carrots, 1 cup diced celery, 1 lb. cottage cheese, 1/2 cup mayonnaise, and 3/4 cup chopped nuts, then fold in 1 prepared package Dream Whip (or other whipped topping) and chill in a mold until firm.

ID 419 — Wedding Cookies Heat oven to 300°F and line 2 cookie sheets with parchment (or leave ungreased). Cream 1 stick unsalted butter (room temp) with 2 Tbsp. granulated sugar and 1 tsp. vanilla until light; mix in 1 cup sifted all-purpose flour, then 1 cup finely chopped walnuts. Roll rounded teaspoonfuls into balls, space about 2 inches apart, bake about 30 minutes until just turning golden, then roll hot cookies in 1 cup sifted powdered sugar and cool on sheets before serving.

ID 420 — Jezebel Sauce Blend together 1 (18 oz.) jar pineapple preserves, 1 (18 oz.) jar apple jelly, 1 (5 oz.) jar horseradish, 1 1/4 oz. dry mustard, and 1 Tbsp. coarse black pepper; serve over cream cheese with crackers.

ID 421 — Banana Bread Mix 1 cup sugar, 2 eggs, 1/2 cup shortening, 3 mashed bananas, vanilla to taste, a pinch of salt, and optional 1/2 cup chopped nuts. Stir in 2 cups flour sifted with 1 tsp. soda and bake at 350°F for about 45 minutes.

ID 422 — Mexicali Chicken And Cheese Bake Heat oven to 350°F and grease a 13 x 9-inch dish. Mix 3 cups cooked cubed chicken with 1 cup (of the 2 cups) shredded Monterey Jack, 1 (12 oz.) can drained corn, and 1 (10 3/4 oz.) can condensed cream of chicken soup; spoon into dish. Stir together 1 cup flour, 1/4 cup cornmeal, 1 3/4 tsp. baking powder, chili powder or seasoned salt to taste, 1 1/2 cups milk, 1/2 cup melted margarine, 3 beaten eggs, 1/4 cup chopped onion, 1 (4 oz.) can chopped green chiles, and 2 oz. chopped drained pimento just until moistened (batter will be lumpy); pour over chicken mixture and bake 50 to 60 minutes, sprinkle with remaining cheese (about 1 cup) and return to oven just to melt, then let stand 10 minutes (serves about 8).

ID 423 — Ripe Tomato Ketchup Chop 1 gallon chopped cabbage, 1 gallon tomatoes, 6 to 8 onions, and 6 small bell peppers; add 1 quart vinegar, 1 hot pepper, 5 lb. sugar (or to taste), 1 Tbsp. allspice, 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, and 1 Tbsp. salt. Cook about 40 minutes, then can and seal.

ID 424 — Fresh Broccoli Salad Cut 2 bunches fresh broccoli into bite-size pieces and combine with 10 cooked crumbled bacon slices, 2/3 cup raisins, 1/2 cup chopped onion, and optional 1/2 cup slivered almonds and/or 1/2 cup sharp cheese. Mix 1 cup Miracle Whip with 1/2 cup sugar and 2 Tbsp. vinegar, toss with broccoli mixture, and refrigerate about 2 hours before serving.

ID 425 — Lemon Chicken Heat oven to 400°F. Place 1 whole cut-up chicken in a pan, melt 1 stick butter and mix in juice from 3 large lemons, baste chicken, sprinkle with oregano to taste, and bake about 1 hour at 400°F.

ID 426 — Cherry Topsy-Turvy Pudding Cream 2 Tbsp. butter with 1 cup (of the 1 1/4 cups) sugar. Sift 1 cup flour with 1 tsp. baking powder and 1/8 tsp. salt, then add alternately with 3/4 cup milk to the creamed mixture; spread in a greased casserole. Heat 1 1/2 cups canned tart cherries with the remaining 1/4 cup sugar and 1/4 cup reserved cherry juice, pour hot cherry mixture over batter, and bake at 350°F for 35 to 40 minutes (serves about 6).

ID 427 — Strawberry Pan Pie Cook 1 cup sugar with 1 cup water and 3 level Tbsp. cornstarch until thick and clear (add red food coloring if desired; amount not specified), cool, stir in 1 pint raw strawberries, and pour into 1 baked 9-inch pie crust.

ID 428 — Chicken Casserole Cook 1 large package spinach noodles in broth (amount not specified), then combine with 6 boiled chicken breasts (boned; reserve 1 cup broth), sautéed 1 cup chopped celery plus 1 large chopped green pepper and 1 large chopped onion, 1/2 lb. Velveeta, optional mushrooms, and 1 can mushroom soup plus 1 cup chicken broth; bake uncovered at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 429 — Cream Tacos Brown 1 lb. hamburger with onion (amount not specified). In a pan, layer 1 dozen corn tortillas (cut into quarters), topping each piece with about 1 tsp. meat, about 1 tsp. green chili (amount not specified), about 1 tsp. tomato sauce from 2 small cans, and grated Cheddar cheese (amount not specified); repeat layers, pour 1 can evaporated milk over all, cover with foil, and bake at 350°F for 30 to 35 minutes until milk has mostly evaporated.

ID 430 — Scottish Shortbread Let 1/2 cup (1 stick) unsalted butter come to room temperature. Grease an 8 x 8-inch metal pan; sift 2 cups all-purpose flour with 1/4 cup sugar and a pinch of salt, rub in the butter with fingers, knead gently into a soft dough, press evenly into pan, prick with a fork, bake at 325°F for 30 to 35 minutes until pale golden, cool slightly, sprinkle with a little granulated sugar (amount not specified), cut into fingers, and cool completely before storing airtight.

ID 431 — Slaw Whisk 1/3 cup sugar, 3/4 tsp. salt, 3/4 tsp. pepper, 1 Tbsp. celery seed, 1 Tbsp. prepared mustard, and 1/4 cup apple cider vinegar; slowly stir in 1 cup mayonnaise. Rub a bowl with 1 clove garlic (cut), add shredded cabbage (amount not specified), toss with desired amount of dressing, and chill.

ID 432 — Hot Cheese Balls With ingredients at room temperature, mix 1/2 lb. shredded Cheddar with 1 stick oleo, then add 1 cup flour, 1/4 tsp. paprika, 1/4 tsp. salt, and optional dash cayenne; roll into 1-inch balls and bake at 400°F for 15 to 20 minutes on an ungreased cookie sheet.

ID 433 — Pizza Cups Brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1/4 cup minced onion and optional 1/2 tsp. salt; drain. Stir in 8 oz. tomato sauce and 1 tsp. Italian seasoning and cook 5 minutes. Press 2 cans refrigerated biscuits (10-count each) into greased muffin tins, fill with meat mixture, top with 1/2 to 3/4 cup grated cheese, and bake at 400°F for about 12 minutes (makes about 20 cups).

ID 434 — All-American Apple Pie Fill a pastry-lined pie plate (pastry for a double crust) with 6 cups thinly sliced cooking apples, optionally tossed with 1 Tbsp. lemon juice. Mix 1 cup sugar with 2 Tbsp. flour, 1 tsp. cinnamon, and a dash nutmeg; toss with apples, mound into crust, dot with 1 Tbsp. butter, cover with top crust, cut slits, seal and flute edges, and optionally sprinkle with sugar (amount not specified).

ID 435 — Strawberry Cake With Icing Mix 1 box Duncan Hines Strawberry Supreme cake mix with juice from 1 box frozen strawberries, 4 eggs, 1 cup Crisco, 1/2 cup water, and 1 (3 oz.) box strawberry gelatin; beat well and bake in layers or a long pan until done (time depends on pan size; not specified).

ID 436 — Swedish Meat Balls Combine 1 1/2 lb. ground beef with 1 box garlic-and-onion croutons, 1/4 cup chopped onion, 2 eggs, and salt and pepper to taste; form balls and brown. Mix 1 (10 oz.) jar grape jelly with 1 (10 oz.) bottle chili sauce, pour over meatballs, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes (or simmer on stovetop about 20 minutes).

ID 437 — Calf Liver Braised In Wine Dredge 1 lb. thin-sliced calf liver in 1/4 cup flour mixed with 1/2 tsp. salt and 1/8 tsp. pepper. Sauté 1/2 cup chopped onion in 3 Tbsp. butter until tender, add liver and brown lightly. Dissolve 1 bouillon cube in 1/2 cup boiling water, add 1 cup sliced mushrooms, the bouillon, 1/2 cup dry red wine, and 1/4 tsp. basil; cover and simmer about 15 minutes until liver is tender (serves about 4).

ID 438 — Sour Cream Pound Cake Cream 1 cup oleo with 3 cups sugar, blend in 1 cup sour cream, add 5 eggs in stages (3 then 2), then alternately add 3 cups flour mixed with 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/4 tsp. baking soda, and 1/4 tsp. salt with 1/2 cup milk stirred with 2 tsp. vanilla, blending after each addition without overbeating; bake time/temperature not specified in the data.

ID 439 — Baked Beans Mix 4 (15 oz.) cans Great Northern beans with 3/4 lb. cooked bacon pieces, 3/4 to 1 cup ketchup, and 1 cup white sugar; bake in a casserole at 325°F for 1 hour.

ID 440 — Vanilla Ice Cream In a large bowl, mix 6 eggs, 1 1/2 cups sugar, 1 can evaporated milk, 1 Tbsp. milk, and vanilla (amount not specified in the data); add enough additional milk (amount not specified) to fill an ice-cream freezer about 3/4 full, then freeze according to your machine’s directions.

ID 441 — Sparkle Cutout Cookies Cream 1 (8 oz.) softened cream cheese with 1 cup margarine, 2/3 cup sugar, and 1/2 tsp. vanilla; add 2 1/2 cups flour and a dash of salt, mix well, chill, roll to 1/4-inch thick, cut shapes, place on ungreased sheets, decorate with colored sugar or icing (amounts not specified), and bake at 375°F for 8 to 10 minutes until edges just start to brown.

ID 442 — Taco Soup Put 2 lb. browned hamburger meat and 1 chopped medium onion in a crock-pot with 1 packet dry Ranch dressing mix, 1 packet taco seasoning, 1 can whole-kernel corn, 1 can red kidney beans, 1 can pinto beans, 1 small can chopped chiles, and 3 cans stewed tomatoes; cook all day on low (or simmer on stovetop 2 to 3 hours).

ID 443 — Fruit Cocktail Cake Mix 1 can (No. 303) fruit cocktail with juice, 1 1/2 cups sugar, 2 eggs, 1 tsp. vanilla, 2 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, and 2 cups flour all at once and beat 3 minutes. Pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, top with 1/2 cup brown sugar and 1 cup chopped pecans, and bake at 350°F for about 45 minutes.

ID 444 — Fa-La-La-La-Las Cream 1 cup butter-flavor Crisco with 1/2 cup sugar; beat in 1 egg, 3/4 tsp. salt, 3/4 tsp. vanilla, and 1/2 tsp. almond extract. Stir in 2 1/4 cups all-purpose flour, press dough through a cookie press onto ungreased sheets, and bake at 400°F for 5 to 7 minutes until set but not browned (makes about 4 to 4 1/2 dozen).

ID 445 — Orange-Coconut Pie Cream 1/4 cup softened butter with 1 cup sugar, beat in 3 beaten eggs, then stir in 1/2 cup orange juice, 1 tsp. lemon extract, a dash of salt, and 1 cup flaked coconut. Pour into 1 unbaked 9-inch pie crust and bake at 350°F for 45 to 50 minutes until a knife inserted in the center comes out clean.

ID 446 — Sour Cream Pound Cake Cream 2 sticks real butter with 3 cups sugar, beat in 6 eggs one at a time, add 3 cups flour mixed with 1/4 tsp. baking soda, beat well, then blend in 1/2 pint sour cream and 1 tsp. vanilla. Pour into a greased and floured tube pan and bake at 325°F for about 1 hour or a bit longer.

ID 447 — Company Chicken Mix 1 cup instant rice with 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, and 1 can cream of celery soup; place 4 chicken breasts on top, add a pat of butter to each (amount not specified) and season to taste, then bake at 375°F for 1 hour.

ID 448 — Minestrone Soup Sauté 1 cup thinly sliced carrots, 1 cup sliced celery, 1/2 cup chopped onions, and 1 minced garlic clove in 2 Tbsp. margarine. Add 2 cans (15 oz. each) Chef Boyardee Beefogetti, 1 drained can chickpeas, 2 cups water, 2 beef bouillon cubes, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. crushed basil, and 1/4 tsp. pepper; simmer covered about 15 minutes and top servings with Parmesan cheese (amount not specified) (serves about 6).

ID 449 — Cherry Topped Cheesecake Heat oven to 300°F. Reserve 1 cup dry cake mix from 1 package yellow cake mix; combine remaining cake mix with 2 Tbsp. oil and 1 egg, press crumb mixture into a 13 x 9-inch pan bottom and slightly up sides. Beat 2 (8 oz.) packages cream cheese with 1/2 cup sugar, then beat in remaining 3 eggs, 1 1/2 cups milk, 3 Tbsp. lemon juice, and 3 Tbsp. vanilla; pour over crust and bake at 300°F until set (time not specified in the provided lines), cool, then top with 1 can cherry pie filling.

ID 450 — Sweet ’N’ Sour Sauce Whisk together 1/2 cup vinegar, 1/2 cup sugar, and 1/3 cup oil until well blended; use for bean salad or cucumbers.

ID 451 — Easy Taco Dip In a glass pie plate, layer 1 large package cream cheese, 1 can Hormel chili, and 2 cups shredded Cheddar; microwave on High about 5 to 6 minutes and serve with nacho chips.

ID 452 — Monkey Bread Separate 2 packages refrigerator rolls, dip each in 1/2 cup melted margarine or butter, then in a mixture of 3/4 cup sugar and 1 tsp. cinnamon. Stack unevenly in a casserole or ring pan, bake at 425°F for 20 to 25 minutes, invert onto a plate, and optionally drizzle with powdered-sugar icing (amount not specified).

ID 453 — Coconut Cream Pie Or Lemon Meringue Pie For coconut version, cook a custard using 3 separated eggs (use yolks for filling), 4 Tbsp. cornstarch, 2 cups milk, 2 Tbsp. butter, 1 1/2 cups sugar, and 1 Tbsp. coconut flavoring, then pour into 1 unbaked pie shell and top with meringue made from the egg whites (method details not fully specified in the data). Note from data: for lemon pie, use 1 1/2 cups milk plus 1/2 cup ReaLemon instead of the 2 cups milk and omit coconut flavoring.

ID 454 — Death By Chocolate Bake 1 chocolate cake mix as directed, cool completely, and break into pieces. Beat together 2 packages chocolate instant pudding, 2 envelopes Dream Whip, and 3 cups cold milk; refrigerate 1 hour. Layer cake pieces with 2 (8 oz.) containers Cool Whip and the pudding mixture, and top with 4 crushed Heath bars if desired (assembly details beyond the provided lines are implied by ingredients).

ID 455 — Corn Meal Muffins Sift 1 cup flour and sift with 3/4 tsp. baking soda, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 tsp. baking powder; mix with 1 cup corn meal. Combine 1/4 cup melted bacon fat with 2 Tbsp. brown sugar and 2 well-beaten eggs, add 1 1/2 cups sour milk, then stir into dry ingredients just until smooth. Fill a well-oiled muffin pan 2/3 full and bake at 435°F for 15 to 20 minutes.
ID 456 — Hot Taco Rice Brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1 chopped onion; drain. Add 1 1/2 cups salsa, 1 can tomato sauce, and 1 chicken bouillon cube, bring to a boil, then stir in 1 1/2 cups Minute rice, cover, and simmer about 5 minutes.

ID 457 — Moist Devil’s Food Cake Beat 1 devil’s food cake mix with 1 can cherry pie filling, 1/4 cup oil, and 3 eggs on medium speed about 3 minutes; bake in a greased and floured tube pan at 350°F for about 40 minutes.

ID 458 — Peanut Butter Twinkies Bring 1 cup sugar and 1 cup light Karo syrup to a full boil, remove from heat, stir in 1 cup peanut butter, 1/4 stick oleo, and 1 Tbsp. vanilla. Add 6 to 8 cups cornflakes (enough to press) and press into a well-buttered 13 x 9-inch pan; cut into squares while warm.

ID 459 — Low-Calorie Pumpkin Pie Heat oven to 350°F and lightly grease or spray a 9-inch pie pan. Blend 1 (16 oz.) can solid-pack pumpkin, 1 (13 oz.) can evaporated skim milk, 1 egg, 2 egg whites, 1/2 cup biscuit mix, 2 Tbsp. sugar, 6 packets sugar substitute, 2 tsp. pumpkin pie spice, and 2 tsp. vanilla for about 1 minute (or beat 2 minutes). Pour into pan and bake about 50 minutes until center is puffed (about 8 servings).

ID 460 — Zucchini Squares Mix 2 cups shredded zucchini with 1/2 cup chopped onion, 1 clove garlic (minced), 1/2 cup grated Parmesan, 1/2 cup oil, 2 Tbsp. dried parsley, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. seasoned salt, 1/2 tsp. oregano, and 2 slightly beaten eggs; bake in a greased 9 x 13-inch pan at 350°F for about 30 minutes until lightly browned on top.

ID 461 — Pound Cake Cream 1 stick butter with 1 cup Crisco and 3 cups sugar, add 6 eggs one at a time, add 3 cups plain flour one cup at a time plus 1/2 tsp. baking powder, then add 1 cup sweet milk in thirds and 1 tsp. vanilla; beat 3 minutes. Pour into a greased and floured tube pan, place in a cold oven, set to 350°F, and bake about 1 hour 15 minutes.

ID 462 — Chocolate Eclair Dessert Line a buttered 9 x 13-inch dish with about 10 graham crackers (half of ~20). Beat 2 (4 oz.) packages vanilla instant pudding with 3 1/2 cups milk for 2 minutes, fold in 8 oz. whipped topping, spread half over crackers, add remaining crackers, then remaining pudding mixture, and chill 2 hours. Beat 2 packages Choco-bake with 2 tsp. light corn syrup, 2 tsp. vanilla, and 3 Tbsp. softened margarine, then beat in 1 1/2 cups confectioners sugar alternating with 3 Tbsp. milk, and spread icing over the top.

ID 463 — Butternut Cookies Cream 2 cups butter with 1 cup sugar and 4 tsp. vanilla until fluffy, add 4 cups flour and 1 tsp. salt, then mix in 4 cups finely chopped walnuts. Shape into 1-inch balls, bake at 325°F for about 20 minutes without browning, cool, and roll in confectioners sugar (amount not specified).

ID 464 — Hattie Coffer’s Kool-Aid Punch Make a syrup by heating 1 cup water with 2 cups sugar until dissolved; stir in 1 package Kool-Aid (any flavor), 1/2 cup lemon juice, 2 cups pineapple juice, 1 quart ginger ale, and 10 cups water (makes about 30 cups).

ID 465 — Scalloped Corn Heat oven to 350°F. Sauté 1/2 cup chopped onion in 2 Tbsp. butter until golden, blend in 2 Tbsp. flour, 1 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. paprika, and a dash black pepper and cook until bubbly. Remove from heat, whisk in 3/4 cup milk, bring to a boil and cook 1 minute stirring constantly, then stir in 1 can whole-kernel corn and 1 slightly beaten egg. Pour into a baking dish, top with breadcrumbs (amount not specified), and bake 30 minutes.

ID 466 — Becky’s Punch Mix 1 packet black cherry (or cherry) Kool-Aid with 1 small box same-flavor Jell-O in 2 quarts warm water, then add 1 cup sugar, 1 can frozen lemonade, and 1 can pineapple juice; freeze. Thaw about 1 hour before serving and add 2 liters 7-Up.
ID 467 — Chicken Saltimbocca Pound 3 large chicken breasts (skinned, boned, halved lengthwise) into 6 cutlets; top each with 1 thin ham slice and 1 slice process Swiss cheese, add some of 1 chopped medium tomato, and sprinkle lightly with crushed dried sage (amount not specified). Fold sides and roll; mix 1/3 cup fine dry bread crumbs with 2 Tbsp. grated Parmesan and 2 Tbsp. snipped parsley, dip rolls in 1/4 cup melted butter and coat with crumbs, then bake in a shallow pan at 350°F for 40 to 45 minutes (serves about 6).

ID 468 — Toll House Cookies (Oatmeal Version) Cream 1 cup shortening with 3/4 cup brown sugar and 3/4 cup white sugar. Add 1 1/2 cups sifted flour, 1 tsp. soda, 2 beaten eggs, 1 tsp. hot water, 1 tsp. vanilla, and 1 tsp. salt; stir in 2 cups oatmeal, 1 cup chopped nuts, and 1 package Toll House chocolate chips (or butterscotch chips). Drop by teaspoonfuls onto a cookie sheet and bake at 350°F for 10 to 15 minutes.

ID 469 — Chicken Tortilla Casserole Mix 1 can cream of chicken soup with 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 cup sour cream, 1 cup picante sauce, and onion to taste; heat until nearly boiling. Grease a 9 x 9-inch pan, break 12 tortillas into pieces and layer half in the pan, add half of 1 cooked boned chicken, pour on half the hot sauce mixture, repeat layers, top with Cheddar cheese (amount not specified), and bake at 350°F for 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 470 — Chop Suey Brown 1 to 1 1/2 lb. stew meat and cook until tender (about 2 to 2 1/2 hours). Add 1 can mushrooms and 1 medium onion and cook until onion is done. Add 6 to 8 cups water plus 1 cup soy sauce and 1 large can chop suey vegetables; thicken with cornstarch stirred into a half-water/half-soy mixture (amounts not specified) and serve over rice or noodles.

ID 471 — Vegetable Pizza Press 1 (8 oz.) package crescent-roll dough onto a baking sheet (do not separate), bake as package directs until golden, and cool. Mix 2 (8 oz.) packages softened cream cheese with 1 cup mayonnaise and 1/2 packet (of a 10 oz. packet) Ranch mix, spread over crust, top with 4 cups finely chopped raw vegetables, and chill until firm (best made a day ahead; serves about 12–15).

ID 472 — Log Cabin Toast Mix 1/4 cup sugar with 2 tsp. cinnamon. Toast 2 slices bread, spread with soft margarine or butter (amount not specified), sprinkle with cinnamon sugar, cut each slice into 4 strips, and stack like “logs.”

ID 473 — Yum Yum Salad Mix 1 can cherry pie filling with 1 large can drained crushed pineapple, 1 can Borden milk (sweetened condensed; amount as “1 can”), 3/4 cup chopped pecans, and 1 (8 oz.) Cool Whip; refrigerate overnight.

ID 474 — My Caramel Rolls Beat together 3 packages yeast, 1/2 cup sugar, 2 cups warm water, and 2 eggs until light and fluffy; stir in 3 Tbsp. oleo, 1 tsp. salt, and 6 to 7 cups flour, let rise once, and meanwhile prepare caramel (caramel ingredients/amounts not provided in the data).

ID 475 — Spanish Hamburger #1 Brown 6 lb. hamburger about halfway, add finely chopped 1 medium white onion, 1/2 green pepper, and 1 stalk celery, simmer 30 minutes, season with salt and pepper to taste, stir in 1 (20 oz.) can tomato soup, cover to keep steam in, and simmer about 2 hours.

ID 476 — Turkey Vegetable Stir-Fry Whisk 1 Tbsp. cornstarch with 2 Tbsp. soy sauce, 1/4 tsp. ground ginger, and 1 (10 1/2 oz.) can chicken broth; microwave uncovered 2 to 3 minutes, stirring every 30 seconds, until thickened to make sauce. In a skillet, heat 2 Tbsp. vegetable oil and stir-fry 1 julienned carrot, 2 cups sliced mushrooms, 4 minced green onions, 1 diagonally sliced celery stalk, and 1 (6 oz.) package thawed snow peas until crisp-tender; add 2 cups chopped cooked turkey, pour in sauce, heat through, and serve over 2 cups cooked brown rice topped with 2 Tbsp. toasted slivered almonds.

ID 477 — Mango With Tomatoes And Scallions Or Leeks Toss 1 large (or 2 small) sliced mango with 2 medium tomatoes and 1 large leek (or 2 scallions). Whisk lemon juice with pulp (amount not specified) with 2 tsp. safflower oil and a pinch of dry mustard, pour over, toss, and serve chilled or at room temperature.

ID 478 — Vegetable Pizza Press and bake 2 cans crescent rolls as a crust (bake time per package; not specified), then spread with a mixture of 2 large packages softened cream cheese, 1/2 cup mayonnaise (not Miracle Whip), and 1/2 cup Ranch dressing; cut and serve (vegetable topping not listed in the provided lines).

ID 479 — Luau Brown 2 lb. pork sausage, remove, and cook 1 chopped green pepper, 2 chopped large onions, and 1 chopped bunch celery in as little grease as possible. Bring 7 cups water to a boil, stir in 2 packets Lipton noodle soup, 2 cups white Minute rice, and 3 1/2 oz. chopped almonds, then immediately stir in the sausage and vegetables, cover, and bake at 350°F for 40 to 45 minutes, stirring once or twice (serves about 10–12).

ID 480 — Ma’s Dill Pickles Pack cucumbers/dills (amounts not specified) into jars. Boil a brine of 7 cups water, 3 cups vinegar, 1/2 cup salt, and 1/2 cup sugar; pour hot brine over, seal.

ID 481 — Stir-Fried Gumbo Toss 3 to 4 cups okra with flour (amount not specified) plus salt and pepper; fry in oil (amount not specified) as needed. In a large skillet, melt 3/4 stick butter and sauté 3/4 cup sliced green bell pepper, 1 chopped small jalapeño (optional), 1 thinly sliced medium onion, and 1 medium carrot (or 3/4 cup thin slices) until onion is clear; add 1 can stewed tomatoes and cook about 5 minutes, stir in 3/4 cup water, bring to a boil, add 2 cups cooked ground beef or chicken breast or ham, and season with salt and pepper to taste.

ID 482 — No Bake Chocolate Cookies In a saucepan, stir together 2 cups sugar, 1/3 cup cocoa, 1/2 cup milk, and 1 stick oleo; bring to a boil and boil 1 minute. Remove from heat and stir in 1 tsp. vanilla, 1/2 cup peanut butter, and 3 cups quick oats; drop by teaspoonfuls onto wax paper and cool (makes about 4 to 5 dozen).

ID 483 — Carrot Cake Mix 2 cups sifted flour with 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, 2 cups sugar, and 1 tsp. cinnamon. Add 1 1/2 cups oil, 4 eggs, 2 cups grated carrots, and 1 cup nuts, mix well, pour into greased and floured pans, and bake at 350°F for about 30 minutes (makes 2 nine-inch or 3 eight-inch layers).

ID 484 — No Fat Rice And Vegetable Dish In a skillet sprayed with vegetable spray (amount not specified), sauté 1/2 cup sliced summer squash and 1/4 cup chopped onions until tender. Add 1/2 cup sliced mushrooms, 1/2 cup chopped fresh tomato, 1 tsp. chopped garlic, 1/2 tsp. basil, and lemon pepper and salt to taste; cook 5 minutes, then toss with 1 cup cooked rice.

ID 485 — Oyster Fritters Sift 2 cups flour with 2 tsp. baking powder and 1/2 tsp. baking soda. Beat 3 eggs, add 1/4 cup buttermilk and salt to taste, then stir in dry ingredients plus reserved oyster juice from 1 pint oysters; add oysters, stir to coat, and deep-fry at 350°F until golden.

ID 486 — Quick Coffee Cake (Double Recipe) Mix 2 cups flour, 6 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 cup sugar, 1 tsp. salt, 2 beaten eggs, 1 cup milk, and 1/2 cup melted oleo or butter; spread in a 13 x 9-inch pan (or two 8-inch pans), sprinkle thickly with sugar and cinnamon (optional chopped nuts; amounts not specified), and bake at 375°F for 15 to 21 minutes.

ID 487 — Belly Buttons Prepare 1 box crust mix according to package directions (additional flour as needed; amounts not specified), roll dough out on a floured surface, spread with softened butter or margarine (amount not specified), cover with brown sugar (amount not specified) and cinnamon (amount not specified), roll up like a long thin cinnamon roll, slice into 1-inch pieces, set upright in a buttered 13 x 9-inch dish, and bake at 400°F for about 15 minutes.

ID 488 — Tater Tot Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground lean beef with 1 large chopped onion; stir in 1 can cream of mushroom soup and 1 can mixed vegetables (partially drained), spread in a buttered casserole, top with Tater Tots as needed, and bake at 350°F for about 45 minutes.

ID 489 — Cheesy Cornbread Cook 4 slices bacon in an 8-inch cast-iron skillet, remove bacon and reserve 2 Tbsp. drippings, then heat skillet with drippings at 425°F for 5 minutes. Stir together crumbled bacon, 1 (16 oz.) cornbread mix, 2 beaten eggs, 1 (15 oz.) can cream-style corn, 3/4 cup mayonnaise, and 1 cup shredded Swiss or Cheddar; pour into hot skillet and bake at 425°F for 30 to 35 minutes until golden.

ID 490 — Rice Crispy Chicken Crush 4 cups Rice Krispies to make 2 cups crumbs and mix with 1 tsp. paprika in a shallow dish. Beat 1 egg with 3/4 cup milk; in another dish mix 3/4 cup flour with 1 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, and 1 tsp. poultry seasoning. Dip 3 lb. frying chicken pieces in flour mixture, then egg mixture, then cereal crumbs; place in pan, drizzle with 3 Tbsp. melted margarine, and bake until chicken is done (baking time/temperature not included in the provided lines).

ID 491 — No-Fat Added Oven Fried Chicken Heat oven to 350°F. Coat a baking sheet with vegetable cooking spray. Mix 1/2 cup dry bread crumbs with 3 Tbsp. grated Parmesan, 1 tsp. dried thyme, 1/4 tsp. garlic powder, 1/4 tsp. onion powder, 1/4 tsp. black pepper, and optional 1/4 tsp. salt. Dip 4 skinless boneless chicken breast halves (about 3 oz. each) in 3/4 cup nonfat buttermilk, coat with crumb mixture, place on sheet, and bake until cooked through (baking time not provided in the given lines).

ID 492 — Sauerkraut Salad Toss 1 quart drained sauerkraut with 1 cup chopped green bell pepper, 1 cup chopped celery, 1 (4 oz.) jar pimento, and 1 chopped medium onion. Mix in a dressing of 1/2 cup vinegar, 1 1/2 cups sugar, and 2 Tbsp. oil (directions line is truncated in the data).

ID 493 — Sour Cream Meat Loaf Combine 2 lb. ground lean beef with 1 1/2 cups grated raw carrot, 1/4 cup grated unpeeled apple, 1 1/2 cups grated raw potato, 1 onion quartered and studded with 4 cloves, 6 crumbled fried bacon slices, 2 beaten eggs, 2 1/4 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. pepper, 1/8 tsp. nutmeg, 1/8 tsp. dry mustard, and 2 cups sour cream. Pack into a 9 x 5 x 3-inch loaf pan and bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 to 1 3/4 hours (serves about 6).

ID 494 — Stuffed Chicken Breast Heat oven to 375°F. Prepare 1 box Stove Top stuffing as directed; optionally slice 1 medium green pepper into short strips. Mix 1/4 cup hot water with 1 can cream of mushroom soup. Stuff 8 boneless chicken breasts with stuffing, place in a baking dish, season with garlic salt, pepper, and paprika to taste, and spoon soup mixture over/around chicken (remaining baking details are truncated in the data).

ID 495 — Meg’s Power Peanut Butter Balls Melt 2 sticks butter or margarine and pour over 1/2 cup graham cracker crumbs, 1 box confectioners sugar, and 1 cup crunchy peanut butter; mix well and form bite-size balls. Melt chocolate chips (amount not specified) with 2 oz. paraffin in a double boiler, dip balls, and set on a greased cookie sheet to harden.

ID 496 — Indian Meat Loaf Mix 1 lb. ground beef with 1/2 lb. ground pork, 1 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, 1/2 tsp. sage, and 1 beaten egg; stir in 1/2 cup corn meal, 1/2 cup chopped onion, 1/4 cup diced green pepper, 1/2 cup cream-style corn, and 1 1/4 cups canned tomatoes. Pack into a loaf pan and bake at 350°F for about 1 1/2 hours.

ID 497 — Creamy Cheese Crab Dip Mix 1 (8 oz.) package plus 1 (3 oz.) package cream cheese with 1/2 cup white wine and 1/8 tsp. garlic powder, fold in 1 lb. crabmeat, bake at 350°F for about 20 minutes, and serve with crackers or toast rounds.

ID 498 — Skillet Beef and Macaroni In a skillet, cook 1 to 1 1/2 lb. ground beef with 1/2 c. chopped onion until the meat is browned and the onion is tender, then drain. Stir in 2 cans (8 oz.) tomato sauce, 1 c. water, 1 (7 oz.) pkg. macaroni, 1/2 c. chopped green pepper, 2 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, and 1 1/2 Tbsp. chili powder, bring to a boil, reduce heat, cover and simmer until the macaroni is tender, about 20 minutes, stirring occasionally and adding additional water if needed (yields 4 to 6 servings).

ID 499 — Jiffy Beef Stroganoff Brown 1 lb. ground beef, sprinkle with 1 pkg. dry onion soup mix and 1/2 tsp. ginger, arrange 3 c. medium noodles over the meat, add 1 (3 oz.) can sliced mushrooms, pour 3 c. hot water over the noodles, and cook on low for 20 minutes. Blend 2 Tbsp. flour into 1 c. sour cream, stir into the stroganoff, and cook 3 minutes longer.

ID 500 — Baked Cheese Sandwiches Make 4 cheese sandwiches using 2 slices of American cheese in each, remove crusts and arrange in a baking dish. Mix 5 eggs with 3 c. milk and 1 tsp. mustard, pour over the sandwiches, and bake at 400°F for about 20 minutes or until browned on top.

ID 501 — Teresa’s Brisket Cover the brisket with garlic, onion, celery powder, minced onion, and a bottle of liquid smoke and refrigerate overnight in a 13 x 9-inch pan. The next morning add 1 bottle Worcestershire sauce and black pepper, bake at 275°F for 6 to 8 hours, and cover with barbecue sauce.

ID 502 — Heavenly Rice Cook 3/4 c. rice without salt and drain off excess water, then while hot mix in 1 small can drained pineapple and sugar to taste. Let set until cold, fold in 1 c. whipped cream, and add miniature marshmallows if desired.

ID 503 — Baked Salmon Loaf Combine 1 (1 lb.) can salmon with 1/2 c. chopped celery, 1/4 c. chopped onion, 1/4 lb. chopped fresh mushrooms, 1/4 c. evaporated skim milk, 2 egg whites or egg substitute equal to 1 egg, and 1 c. bread crumbs or oat bran cereal; optionally add 1 1/2 Tbsp. dill weed.

ID 504 — Favorite Vegetable Soup (Low-Fat) In a 1 1/2-quart nonstick saucepan cook 1/4 c. diced onion with 2 packets instant chicken broth mix and 2 minced garlic cloves until translucent. Add 1 1/2 c. sliced zucchini, 1/2 c. sliced carrots, 1/2 c. chopped seeded tomato, 1 tsp. chopped parsley, 1/4 tsp. basil, and 1/8 tsp. pepper, cover and cook about 10 minutes. Add 2 c. water, bring to a boil, reduce heat and cook about 20 minutes, puree most of the soup, return to the pan, add reserved vegetables and heat (makes 2 servings).

ID 505 — Sour Cream Lasagna Cook 1 (8 oz.) pkg. egg dumpling noodles, rinse and drain. Brown 1 1/2 lb. ground beef and mix in 1 tsp. salt, a dash of pepper, 1/4 tsp. garlic salt, 1/4 tsp. liquid smoke, 1 (8 oz.) can tomato sauce, and 1 Tbsp. brown sugar, cook 5 minutes and remove from heat. Combine noodles with 1 c. cottage cheese, 1 (12 oz.) carton sour cream, and 6 chopped green onions. Layer noodle and meat mixtures in a 2-quart dish, top with 3/4 c. grated Cheddar cheese, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 506 — Tater Tot Casserole Lightly brown 3/4 to 1 lb. ground beef or turkey with 1 small chopped onion if desired, drain, and spread in a casserole dish. Mix 1 can cream soup with 1/2 can milk, spread over 1 can drained whole kernel corn, sprinkle with 1 c. shredded Cheddar cheese, top with frozen Tater Tots, and bake covered at 325°F for 30 to 40 minutes or until done.

ID 507 — Earthquake Cake Prepare 1 box German chocolate cake mix as directed. Grease a 9 x 13-inch pan, sprinkle 1 1/2 c. chopped pecans and 1 1/2 c. shredded coconut over the bottom, and pour cake batter over the top.

ID 508 — Raw Gluten Mix 2 lb. whole wheat flour with 1 qt. water into a firm dough and let stand 45 minutes. Rinse and squeeze under cold running water until starch is removed and water runs clear, keeping dough together, then cover with water until ready to use (yields 1 lb.).

ID 509 — Lemon Chicken and Zucchini Cut 1 1/2 lb. chicken breasts and thighs into 1-inch pieces. Blend 1/4 c. chicken broth with 1 Tbsp. cornstarch, then stir in 2 Tbsp. soy sauce and 1 tsp. sugar and set aside.

ID 510 — Meat Balls Mix 2 lb. ground beef with a 10 oz. jar sweet relish, 2 tsp. garlic powder, 1/2 c. minced onions, 1/2 tsp. onion salt, and 1 egg. Form into balls, coat with 1 box barbecue Shake ’N Bake, and bake at 350°F for 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 511 — Butternut Chewies Beat 2 eggs until foamy, add 2 c. light brown sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla, and 1/2 c. melted margarine. Mix in 1 1/2 c. flour combined with 2 tsp. baking powder and 1/2 tsp. salt, stir in 1 c. chopped nuts, spread in a greased 13 x 9-inch pan, and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes (makes 2 dozen).

ID 512 — Tennessee Tea Combine 1 c. sugar, 1 c. Country Time Lemonade, 1/2 c. instant tea, and 1 c. white grape juice in a gallon pitcher, fill with water, stir, and chill or serve over ice.

ID 513 — Apple Waldorf Salad Chop 1 Granny Smith apple and 1 red Delicious apple without peeling, sprinkle with 1 Tbsp. lemon juice, add 1/2 c. chopped celery, 1 Tbsp. pecans, a dash of cinnamon and nutmeg, and 1/4 c. nonfat yogurt, then serve chilled.

ID 514 — Jackie’s Coconut Pie Melt 1 1/2 sticks butter, beat with 8 eggs and 3 c. sugar, mix in 1 c. buttermilk, then add 2 tsp. vanilla and a 7 oz. can coconut. Pour into 2 deep dish pie shells and bake at 300°F for 1 hour.

ID 515 — Navy Bean Soup Combine 2 (16 oz.) cans navy beans undrained, 1/2 c. diced salt pork if desired, 2 (14 1/2 oz.) cans stewed tomatoes, 2 diced potatoes, 2 diced onions, 2 diced carrots, 1 Tbsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. pepper, and celery salt to taste. Add water if needed and cook until vegetables are tender (makes 6 servings).

ID 516 — Layered Banana Pineapple Dessert Mix 1 1/2 c. graham cracker crumbs with 1/4 c. sugar and 1/3 c. melted margarine and press into a 13 x 9-inch pan. Layer 3 sliced bananas on top. Beat 1 (8 oz.) cream cheese with 3 1/2 c. cold milk and 2 pkg. vanilla instant pudding, spread over bananas, top with 1 (20 oz.) can crushed pineapple drained and 1 (8 oz.) Cool Whip, and refrigerate 3 hours.

ID 517 — Scalloped Potatoes Sauté 1 thinly sliced large onion in 1 Tbsp. butter until translucent, add 2 thinly sliced large potatoes, then mix in 2 Tbsp. lemon juice, 1 tsp. thyme, and 1/2 tsp. salt.

ID 518 — Herb Butter Cream 1/4 lb. Heritage butter at room temperature with 1 Tbsp. lemon juice, then beat in 3 Tbsp. fresh parsley, 3 Tbsp. tarragon basil, and salt and pepper to taste; chill and use on corn or vegetables.

ID 519 — Turnip Greens Wash 1 bucket turnip greens thoroughly. In a large pot 3/4 full of water add 1 c. bacon grease and 1 Tbsp. salt and bring to a boil. Add greens by the handful, letting them cook down, poking them under as needed. Add 1/4 tsp. baking soda, boil until tender about 30 minutes, drain well, and chop.

ID 520 — Bourbon Balls Beat 1/2 c. butter until fluffy, gradually beat in 1 lb. confectioners sugar, then slowly add 4 1/2 tsp. 100-proof bourbon. Chill 1 hour, roll into 1-inch balls, chill again, melt 8 oz. semisweet chocolate in a double boiler, dip balls halfway, place on wax paper, top each with a pecan half, and chill until firm (about 3 dozen).

ID 521 — Pinto Beans Sort and rinse 1 1/2 c. dry beans, place in saucepan with water and 3/4 tsp. ground ginger, bring to a boil, cover and cook about 1 hour. Add 3 Tbsp. melted meat drippings and 1 1/2 tsp. salt, continue cooking, then add 1 heaping Tbsp. sugar and cook until very tender.

ID 522 — Cook While You Sleep Cookies Preheat oven to 350°F. Beat 2 egg whites until foamy, add a pinch of salt and 1/4 tsp. cream of tartar, beat until stiff, then add 2/3 c. sugar gradually. Stir in vanilla, 1 c. chocolate chips, 1 c. chopped nuts, and coconut if desired. Drop by teaspoon onto foil-lined sheets, put in oven, turn oven off immediately, do not open for 8 hours, then remove cookies (makes 40–50).

ID 523 — Chili Spaghetti Fry chopped mango (green pepper) and 1 chopped onion in butter, then brown 1 1/2 lb. hamburger in the same skillet. Add 3 cans tomato sauce and a dash of chili powder and simmer about 20 minutes.

ID 524 — Cherry Delight Mix 1 small can drained crushed pineapple with 1 small pkg. dry cherry Jell-O, stir in 1 small container cottage cheese, fold in 1 small container Cool Whip, and refrigerate.
