ID 525 — Banana Split Dessert Mix 2 c. crushed graham crackers with 6 Tbsp. melted butter and press into a 13 x 9-inch pan. Beat 1/2 c. butter with 2 c. powdered sugar, 2 eggs, and 1 tsp. vanilla until fluffy and spread over crust. Arrange sliced bananas, top with crushed pineapple, spread with 2 c. whipped cream, sprinkle with 1/4 c. crushed nuts, garnish with maraschino cherries, and chill 6 hours.

ID 526 — Strawberry Salad Dissolve 2 pkg. strawberry Jell-O in 1 c. boiling water, add 1 small pkg. strawberries, 2 crushed bananas, and 1 can crushed pineapple. Pour half into a pan, let set, spread with sour cream, add remaining mixture, and chill until firm.

ID 527 — Peanut Butter Pie Beat 2 eggs and mix with 1 c. corn syrup, sugar, 1/2 c. peanut butter, and 1 tsp. vanilla. Pour into ̀1 unbaked 8-inch pie crust and bake at 350°F for 45 to 60 minutes until browned.

ID 528 — Foolproof Fudge Melt 3 (6 oz.) pkg. chocolate chips with 1 (14 oz.) can Eagle Brand milk over low heat, remove from heat, stir in a dash of salt, 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, and 1/2 c. chopped nuts. Spread in an 8-inch square dish and chill 2 hours.

ID 529 — Hamburger Party Balls Mix 1 1/2 lb. hamburger with 1/2 c. chopped dill pickles, 1/4 c. Carnation cream, 2 Tbsp. Shake ’n Bake for chicken, and chopped onion if desired. Shape into balls, roll in remaining Shake ’n Bake, and bake at 350°F for 20 to 30 minutes.

ID 530 — Pigs in Blanket Wrap cocktail hot dogs in crescent roll dough and bake as directed on the package. Serve warm with mustard.

ID 531 — Fresh Tomato Salsa Combine 5 diced tomatoes with 1/3 c. tomato sauce, 1/4 c. finely chopped purple onion, 3 minced garlic cloves, 1–2 minced jalapeños, 2 Tbsp. cilantro, 1 tsp. oregano, 2 Tbsp. lime juice, and 1 tsp. salt, then chill.

ID 532 — Fresh Apple Cake #2 Beat 1 c. oil with 1 3/4 c. sugar and 2 eggs until creamy. Add 2 1/2 c. flour, 1 tsp. soda, 2 tsp. baking powder, and 1 tsp. salt gradually, then stir in 3 c. chopped apples, 1 c. nuts, 1 c. coconut, and 1 tsp. vanilla. Bake in an angel food pan at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 533 — Pumpkin Pie Dessert Mix 2 1/4 c. crushed butter crackers with 1/2 c. sugar and 3/4 c. melted margarine and press into a 9 x 13 pan. Whisk 2 c. cold milk with 2 pkg. instant vanilla pudding, stir in 1 can pumpkin and spices, spread over crust, refrigerate 3 hours, and garnish with whipped topping and nuts.

ID 534 — Vermicelli Salad Combine cooked and cooled 1 (12 oz.) pkg. vermicelli with chopped black olives, green onions, pimentos, oil, Tex Joy seasoning, lemon juice, and 1/2 to 1 c. mayonnaise. Refrigerate overnight.

ID 535 — Two Potato Bake Layer 4 c. sliced sweet potatoes on one side of a greased baking dish and 4 c. sliced red potatoes on the other. Sprinkle with onion, drizzle with melted oleo, season with salt and pepper, repeat layers, add 3/4 c. skim milk, parsley, and Parmesan, and bake until tender.

ID 536 — Spinach Dip Mix thawed, drained spinach with 1 c. sour cream, 1 c. mayonnaise, 1 c. chopped green onions, and 1 pkg. vegetable soup mix. Serve in hollowed sourdough bread with bread chunks.

ID 537 — Scalloped Potatoes Mix 2 cans cream of chicken soup with 1 c. sour cream and 2 Tbsp. chives. Layer with 6 c. frozen hash browns and 2 c. Cheddar cheese in a greased pan and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 538 — Pork Chop Dinner Layer pork chops, sliced potatoes, and mushrooms in a baking pan, pour onion soup mix with water over top, cover with foil, and bake at 350°F for 2 hours.

ID 539 — Chicken Casserole Mix 4 c. cooked chicken, 1 c. celery, 1 c. rice, 3/4 c. mayonnaise, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 Tbsp. lemon juice, 3 Tbsp. onion, 3 chopped hard-boiled eggs, and optional water chestnuts. Sauté butter with almonds and corn flakes, sprinkle on top, and bake at 350°F for 35 minutes.

ID 540 — Cabbage and Noodles Boil chopped cabbage and egg noodles until tender. Sauté sliced onions in butter, add cabbage and noodles, stir well, and season with salt and pepper.

ID 541 — Scalloped Tomatoes Preheat oven to 375°F. Combine tomatoes, green pepper, onion, garlic, basil, and pepper in a sprayed casserole. Toss bread cubes with melted margarine, sprinkle on top, and bake 30 minutes.

ID 542 — Hobo Dinner Place 1/4 lb. hamburger patty on foil, top with sliced potato, carrot, onion, salt, pepper, and butter, wrap tightly, and bake at 400°F for 1 hour (serves 1).

ID 543 — Monkey Bread Coat biscuit quarters in sugar and cinnamon, layer with pecans and cherries in a Bundt pan, pour melted butter mixed with brown sugar and cinnamon over top, bake at 350°F for 35 minutes, cool briefly, and invert.

ID 544 — Mixed Up Marinade Stir together 1/4 c. A.1. sauce, 1/4 c. red wine vinegar, 2 Tbsp. soy sauce, 2 Tbsp. ketchup, 1 tsp. garlic salt, pepper, and onion powder, pour over steaks, marinate 2 hours, then grill.

ID 545 — Banana Nut Muffins Mix dry ingredients, add mashed bananas, milk, butter, and egg, fill muffin cups, sprinkle with cinnamon sugar if desired, and bake at 400°F for 20–22 minutes (1 dozen).

ID 546 — Fudge Pie Mix 2 well-beaten eggs with 1 c. sugar, 1 stick butter, 1/2 c. self-rising flour, 2 Tbsp. cocoa, and a pinch of salt, pour into a greased and floured pie pan, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 547 — Brazilian Coffee Cookies Cream 1/3 c. shortening with 1/2 c. granulated sugar and 1/2 c. packed brown sugar, then beat in 1 egg, 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, and 1 Tbsp. milk. Sift together 2 c. flour, 2 Tbsp. powdered instant coffee, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. baking soda, and 1/4 tsp. baking powder, add to the creamed mixture, mix well, shape into 1-inch balls, place on ungreased cookie sheets, flatten to about 1/8 inch, and bake at 400°F for 8 to 10 minutes.

ID 548 — Quick-Energy Pickups Crush 3 or 4 squares of graham crackers and mix with 1 c. powdered sugar, 1 c. crunchy peanut butter, 1 c. semi-sweet chocolate chips, and 1/2 c. instant nonfat dry milk or 3 Tbsp. milk. Shape teaspoonfuls into 1-inch balls, roll in graham cracker crumbs, and refrigerate until firm.

ID 549 — Chicken with Rice (Arroz con Pollo) Mix 2 tsp. salt, chopped garlic, 1/2 tsp. oregano, 1 can tomato sauce, chopped tomatoes, chopped green pepper, chopped onion, 1 Tbsp. achiote coloring, olives, and capers. Add 1 (2 1/2 lb.) cut-up chicken and cook a few minutes, then add 1 lb. rice and 2 c. water or broth, stir and cook until the liquid is absorbed, cover and finish cooking until rice is tender, then garnish with peas and strips of pimentos and serve hot.

ID 550 — Puff Pancakes Preheat oven to 425°F and grease a 10-inch ovenproof skillet. Beat 2 eggs with 1/2 c. flour, 1/2 c. milk, 2 Tbsp. melted butter, 1 Tbsp. sugar, and 1/4 tsp. salt until smooth, pour into skillet, bake 15 minutes, reduce heat to 350°F, and bake 10 to 15 minutes more until puffed and golden (serves 6).

ID 551 — Easy Hot Dish Brown 1 lb. hamburger with chopped onion and celery, mix with 1 can Franco-American spaghetti, 1 can Veg-All mixed vegetables, and 1 can undiluted cream of chicken soup, then bake uncovered until thoroughly heated or keep warm on the stovetop.

ID 552 — Hot Spiced Tea Mix 1 1/3 c. Tang, 1/2 c. sugar, 1/2 c. instant tea, 1 tsp. cinnamon, and 1/2 tsp. cloves; use as needed (makes about 2 cups mix).

ID 553 — Easy Spaghetti Sauté 1 chopped medium onion, 1 chopped garlic clove, and 2 Tbsp. chopped parsley in 4 Tbsp. olive oil until soft, add 1 lb. ground beef, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/8 tsp. pepper and brown lightly, then stir in 2 1/4 c. tomato juice, 1 can tomato paste, 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 tsp. oregano, 1 pkg. spatini, and 1 Tbsp. brown sugar, and simmer about 1 hour (serves 4 to 6).

ID 554 — Cashew Chicken Cut 1 chicken breast into thumb-size cubes and marinate in a soy sauce and sherry mixture for 4 to 6 hours or overnight before cooking with green pepper, blanched cashews, pineapple, snow peas, and seasonings.

ID 555 — Corn Casserole Sauté 1 chopped red or green pepper and 1 chopped medium onion in 1/2 c. margarine, then combine with 1 (17 oz.) can corn with liquid, 1 (17 oz.) can creamed corn, 3 slightly beaten eggs, and 1 pkg. corn muffin mix, pour into a well-greased 2-quart casserole, top with 1 c. shredded Cheddar cheese, and bake at 350°F for 55 to 65 minutes.

ID 556 — Rhubarb Crumble Mix 1 c. brown sugar, 3/4 c. quick oats, 1 c. flour, 1/2 c. melted butter, and 1 tsp. cinnamon. Press half into a 9-inch square pan, cover with 4 c. diced rhubarb, cook together 1 c. sugar, 2 tsp. cornstarch, 1 c. water, and 1 tsp. vanilla until thick and clear, pour over rhubarb, sprinkle with remaining crumb mixture, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 557 — Skillet Pineapple Upside-Down Cake Melt 1/4 c. butter in a skillet, spread 1 c. brown sugar evenly over it, arrange 8 pineapple slices and 8 maraschino cherries on top, cover with batter made from 3 beaten eggs, 1 1/2 c. sugar, 1 1/2 c. sifted cake flour, 1 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. salt, 3/4 c. scalded milk, 1 tsp. vanilla, and 2 Tbsp. butter, and bake until done.

ID 558 — Kim’s Chicken Alfredo Pizza Prepare pizza crust and sprinkle with cornmeal if using a stone. Spread 1 c. light Alfredo sauce over crust, add green pepper, chopped onion, jalapeños, cooked chicken breasts, season with garlic salt, coarse pepper, jerk spice, and parsley flakes, top with Mozzarella cheese, and bake at 450°F for 15 minutes.

ID 559 — Don Hill’s Lasagna Cook 1 1/2 lb. hamburger with chopped onion and bell pepper until meat is no longer pink, add garlic, 1 jar spaghetti sauce, salt, and pepper. Cook egg noodles until almost tender, then layer noodles, sauce, Mozzarella, Cheddar, and Parmesan cheeses in a casserole dish and bake until browned.

ID 560 — Layered Salad Layer chopped lettuce, sliced red onion, 1/2 lb. fried and crumbled bacon, and 1/2 head cauliflower in a bowl. Mix 1/4 c. sugar with 2 c. mayonnaise and 1/2 c. Parmesan cheese, spread on top, refrigerate several hours, then toss before serving.

ID 561 — Apple Cream Coffee Cake Heat oven to 375°F. Mix 1/2 c. sugar with 2 tsp. cinnamon and 1/2 c. chopped walnuts. Cream 1/2 c. softened butter with remaining sugar, beat in 2 eggs and 1 tsp. vanilla, add 2 c. flour sifted with baking powder, baking soda, and salt alternately with 1 c. sour cream, spread half the batter in a greased tube pan, top with sliced apple and half the cinnamon mixture, add remaining batter, sprinkle with remaining topping, and bake 45 minutes.

ID 562 — Apple Crunch Mix 3 sliced apples with 1/4 c. packed brown sugar in a baking pan. Combine 3/4 c. flour, 3/4 c. white sugar, 1/4 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. cinnamon, mix in 1 beaten egg, spread over apples, drizzle with 1/3 c. melted margarine, and bake at 375°F for about 45 minutes until lightly browned.

ID 563 — Ambrosia Combine 1 can drained pineapple chunks, 1 can drained mandarin oranges, 1 1/2 c. seedless grapes, 1 c. miniature marshmallows, 1 c. flaked coconut, and 1/2 c. nuts. Mix 3/4 c. sour cream or vanilla yogurt with 1 Tbsp. sugar, stir into fruit mixture, and chill.

ID 564 — Chocolate Covered Cherries Cream 1/3 c. butter, beat in 2 c. marshmallow cream, a dash of salt, and 1 tsp. almond flavoring, then gradually add 4 c. sifted confectioners sugar. Chill the fondant, wrap around 36 drained maraschino cherries, chill again, melt 12 oz. chocolate chips with optional paraffin, dip cherries, and let set on waxed paper.

ID 565 — Pork Medallions Blend 1 1/2 Tbsp. olive oil with garlic and 1/4 tsp. rosemary, then season 1 lb. thinly sliced pork tenderloin with the mixture, 2 1/2 Tbsp. lemon juice, 1/4 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. black pepper.

ID 566 — Coconut Kisses Preheat oven to 350°F. Beat 2 egg whites until foamy, gradually add 2/3 c. sugar until stiff peaks form, fold in 1/2 tsp. vanilla, 2 c. cornflakes, 1 (3 1/2 oz.) can flaked coconut, and 1/2 c. chopped pecans, drop by tablespoon onto foil-lined cookie sheets, place in oven and immediately turn it off, and do not open the door for 8 hours (yields about 3 dozen).

ID 567 — Lemon Chess Pie Combine 2 c. sugar and 4 eggs, mix together 1 Tbsp. flour and 1 Tbsp. cornmeal and add, then stir in 1/2 c. milk, 1/4 c. melted butter, and 1/2 c. lemon juice, pour into an unbaked pie shell, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 568 — Oatmeal Chocolate Chip Cookies Cream 1 c. butter-flavored shortening with 1 1/4 c. brown sugar and 1/2 c. sugar, beat in 2 eggs, 2 Tbsp. milk, and 2 tsp. vanilla, add 1 3/4 c. flour, 1 tsp. baking soda, then stir in 2 1/2 c. oatmeal, 2 c. chocolate chips, and 1 c. chopped nuts, drop by tablespoon on ungreased sheets, and bake at 375°F for 10 to 12 minutes.

ID 569 — Dirty Pudding Crush 1 small pkg. Oreo cookies and spread half in a 9 x 13-inch pan. Mix 1 large Cool Whip with 1 (8 oz.) cream cheese and 1 c. powdered sugar. In another bowl mix 2 (3 oz.) pkg. French vanilla instant pudding with 3 c. milk, combine mixtures, pour over crumbs, top with remaining crumbs, and refrigerate.

ID 570 — Pickled Bologna Boil together 1 1/2 qt. white vinegar, 1/2 c. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 tsp. pickling spice for 10 minutes, pour hot syrup over sliced bologna packed in a glass jar, cover, refrigerate, and use the next day.

ID 571 — Nutty Oven Fried Chicken Mix 1 c. biscuit mix with 1/3 c. finely chopped pecans, 2 tsp. paprika, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. poultry seasoning, and 1/2 tsp. dried sage. Dip chicken in 1/2 c. evaporated milk, coat with pecan mixture, drizzle with 1/3 c. melted margarine, and bake until done.

ID 572 — Wayne’s Cajun Bean Soup Cook chopped potatoes, onion, and celery until tender, add 3 cans Northern beans, 1 qt. tomatoes, 1 or 2 cans tomato soup, 1 1/2 tsp. chili powder, and 1 lb. sliced smoked sausage, simmer, and serve.

ID 573 — Grandma’s Cheesecake Melt 1 stick butter, mix with 1 1/2 c. graham cracker crumbs and 4 Tbsp. sugar, press into a springform pan, beat 3 (8 oz.) cream cheese bars with 1 c. sugar, egg yolks from 5 eggs, 1 pt. sour cream, and 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, pour into crust, and bake at 350°F.

ID 574 — Preacher Cookies Bring 2 c. sugar, 1 stick butter, and 1/2 c. milk to a boil and cook 3 minutes, remove from heat, stir in 1/2 c. powdered cocoa, 2 c. quick oats, and 1 tsp. vanilla, drop by teaspoon onto waxed paper, and cool (yields about 3 dozen).

ID 575 — Punch Bowl Cake Bake an 18.5 oz. yellow cake mix in two layers as directed, prepare 1 large box instant vanilla pudding, then layer cake, pudding, cherry pie filling, crushed pineapple, Cool Whip, frozen coconut, and chopped pecans in a punch bowl.

ID 576 — Sour Cream Apple Pie Line an unbaked 9-inch pie shell with sliced apples made from 3 to 4 tart green apples, mix 3/4 c. sugar, 1/3 c. flour, spices, and 1/4 c. butter, sprinkle over apples, bake at 350°F for 25 minutes, spread 1 c. sour cream on top, and bake 15 minutes more.

ID 577 — Meat Loaf Mix 1 1/2 lb. ground round with bread soaked in 1 c. milk, 1 beaten egg, 1/4 c. chopped onion, 1 1/4 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, and 1 Tbsp. catsup, pack into a loaf pan, and bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 hours.

ID 578 — Cumin Rice Dish Sauté 1 c. uncooked rice with chopped onion and bell pepper in 2 Tbsp. bacon fat until browned, add 2 cans consommé, 3/4 Tbsp. cumin, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, bring to a boil, cover, and simmer 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 579 — Prune Punch Cake Mix 1/2 c. Crisco, 1 c. sugar, 2 eggs, 1 c. prune juice, 1 c. cooked prunes, 2 c. flour, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 3/4 tsp. salt, and 1 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, bake at 350°F until done, then top warm cake with sugar mixed with orange juice.

ID 580 — Danish Cake Mix 1 c. shortening, 1 3/4 c. sugar, 3 eggs, 3 c. sifted flour, 1 1/2 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, 1 c. buttermilk, 1 Tbsp. orange juice, 1 c. nuts, 2 c. chopped dates, grated orange rind, and 1 tsp. vanilla, bake in a tube pan at 350°F for 1 1/4 hours, and pour sauce over cake while hot.

ID 546 — Fudge Pie Mix 2 well-beaten eggs with 1 c. sugar, 1 stick butter, 1/2 c. self-rising flour, 2 Tbsp. cocoa, and a pinch of salt, pour into a greased and floured pie pan, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 547 — Brazilian Coffee Cookies Cream 1/3 c. shortening with 1/2 c. granulated sugar and 1/2 c. packed brown sugar, then beat in 1 egg, 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, and 1 Tbsp. milk. Sift together 2 c. flour, 2 Tbsp. powdered instant coffee, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. baking soda, and 1/4 tsp. baking powder, add to the creamed mixture, mix well, shape into 1-inch balls, place on ungreased cookie sheets, flatten to about 1/8 inch, and bake at 400°F for 8 to 10 minutes.

ID 548 — Quick-Energy Pickups Crush 3 or 4 squares of graham crackers and mix with 1 c. powdered sugar, 1 c. crunchy peanut butter, 1 c. semi-sweet chocolate chips, and 1/2 c. instant nonfat dry milk or 3 Tbsp. milk. Shape teaspoonfuls into 1-inch balls, roll in graham cracker crumbs, and refrigerate until firm.

ID 549 — Chicken with Rice (Arroz con Pollo) Mix 2 tsp. salt, chopped garlic, 1/2 tsp. oregano, 1 can tomato sauce, chopped tomatoes, chopped green pepper, chopped onion, 1 Tbsp. achiote coloring, olives, and capers. Add 1 (2 1/2 lb.) cut-up chicken and cook a few minutes, then add 1 lb. rice and 2 c. water or broth, stir and cook until the liquid is absorbed, cover and finish cooking until rice is tender, then garnish with peas and strips of pimentos and serve hot.

ID 550 — Puff Pancakes Preheat oven to 425°F and grease a 10-inch ovenproof skillet. Beat 2 eggs with 1/2 c. flour, 1/2 c. milk, 2 Tbsp. melted butter, 1 Tbsp. sugar, and 1/4 tsp. salt until smooth, pour into skillet, bake 15 minutes, reduce heat to 350°F, and bake 10 to 15 minutes more until puffed and golden (serves 6).

ID 551 — Easy Hot Dish Brown 1 lb. hamburger with chopped onion and celery, mix with 1 can Franco-American spaghetti, 1 can Veg-All mixed vegetables, and 1 can undiluted cream of chicken soup, then bake uncovered until thoroughly heated or keep warm on the stovetop.

ID 552 — Hot Spiced Tea Mix 1 1/3 c. Tang, 1/2 c. sugar, 1/2 c. instant tea, 1 tsp. cinnamon, and 1/2 tsp. cloves; use as needed (makes about 2 cups mix).

ID 553 — Easy Spaghetti Sauté 1 chopped medium onion, 1 chopped garlic clove, and 2 Tbsp. chopped parsley in 4 Tbsp. olive oil until soft, add 1 lb. ground beef, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/8 tsp. pepper and brown lightly, then stir in 2 1/4 c. tomato juice, 1 can tomato paste, 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 tsp. oregano, 1 pkg. spatini, and 1 Tbsp. brown sugar, and simmer about 1 hour (serves 4 to 6).

ID 554 — Cashew Chicken Cut 1 chicken breast into thumb-size cubes and marinate in a soy sauce and sherry mixture for 4 to 6 hours or overnight before cooking with green pepper, blanched cashews, pineapple, snow peas, and seasonings.

ID 555 — Corn Casserole Sauté 1 chopped red or green pepper and 1 chopped medium onion in 1/2 c. margarine, then combine with 1 (17 oz.) can corn with liquid, 1 (17 oz.) can creamed corn, 3 slightly beaten eggs, and 1 pkg. corn muffin mix, pour into a well-greased 2-quart casserole, top with 1 c. shredded Cheddar cheese, and bake at 350°F for 55 to 65 minutes.

ID 556 — Rhubarb Crumble Mix 1 c. brown sugar, 3/4 c. quick oats, 1 c. flour, 1/2 c. melted butter, and 1 tsp. cinnamon. Press half into a 9-inch square pan, cover with 4 c. diced rhubarb, cook together 1 c. sugar, 2 tsp. cornstarch, 1 c. water, and 1 tsp. vanilla until thick and clear, pour over rhubarb, sprinkle with remaining crumb mixture, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 557 — Skillet Pineapple Upside-Down Cake Melt 1/4 c. butter in a skillet, spread 1 c. brown sugar evenly over it, arrange 8 pineapple slices and 8 maraschino cherries on top, cover with batter made from 3 beaten eggs, 1 1/2 c. sugar, 1 1/2 c. sifted cake flour, 1 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. salt, 3/4 c. scalded milk, 1 tsp. vanilla, and 2 Tbsp. butter, and bake until done.

ID 558 — Kim’s Chicken Alfredo Pizza Prepare pizza crust and sprinkle with cornmeal if using a stone. Spread 1 c. light Alfredo sauce over crust, add green pepper, chopped onion, jalapeños, cooked chicken breasts, season with garlic salt, coarse pepper, jerk spice, and parsley flakes, top with Mozzarella cheese, and bake at 450°F for 15 minutes.

ID 559 — Don Hill’s Lasagna Cook 1 1/2 lb. hamburger with chopped onion and bell pepper until meat is no longer pink, add garlic, 1 jar spaghetti sauce, salt, and pepper. Cook egg noodles until almost tender, then layer noodles, sauce, Mozzarella, Cheddar, and Parmesan cheeses in a casserole dish and bake until browned.

ID 560 — Layered Salad Layer chopped lettuce, sliced red onion, 1/2 lb. fried and crumbled bacon, and 1/2 head cauliflower in a bowl. Mix 1/4 c. sugar with 2 c. mayonnaise and 1/2 c. Parmesan cheese, spread on top, refrigerate several hours, then toss before serving.

ID 561 — Apple Cream Coffee Cake Heat oven to 375°F. Mix 1/2 c. sugar with 2 tsp. cinnamon and 1/2 c. chopped walnuts. Cream 1/2 c. softened butter with remaining sugar, beat in 2 eggs and 1 tsp. vanilla, add 2 c. flour sifted with baking powder, baking soda, and salt alternately with 1 c. sour cream, spread half the batter in a greased tube pan, top with sliced apple and half the cinnamon mixture, add remaining batter, sprinkle with remaining topping, and bake 45 minutes.

ID 562 — Apple Crunch Mix 3 sliced apples with 1/4 c. packed brown sugar in a baking pan. Combine 3/4 c. flour, 3/4 c. white sugar, 1/4 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. cinnamon, mix in 1 beaten egg, spread over apples, drizzle with 1/3 c. melted margarine, and bake at 375°F for about 45 minutes until lightly browned.

ID 563 — Ambrosia Combine 1 can drained pineapple chunks, 1 can drained mandarin oranges, 1 1/2 c. seedless grapes, 1 c. miniature marshmallows, 1 c. flaked coconut, and 1/2 c. nuts. Mix 3/4 c. sour cream or vanilla yogurt with 1 Tbsp. sugar, stir into fruit mixture, and chill.

ID 564 — Chocolate Covered Cherries Cream 1/3 c. butter, beat in 2 c. marshmallow cream, a dash of salt, and 1 tsp. almond flavoring, then gradually add 4 c. sifted confectioners sugar. Chill the fondant, wrap around 36 drained maraschino cherries, chill again, melt 12 oz. chocolate chips with optional paraffin, dip cherries, and let set on waxed paper.

ID 565 — Pork Medallions Blend 1 1/2 Tbsp. olive oil with garlic and 1/4 tsp. rosemary, then season 1 lb. thinly sliced pork tenderloin with the mixture, 2 1/2 Tbsp. lemon juice, 1/4 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. black pepper.

ID 566 — Coconut Kisses Preheat oven to 350°F. Beat 2 egg whites until foamy, gradually add 2/3 c. sugar until stiff peaks form, fold in 1/2 tsp. vanilla, 2 c. cornflakes, 1 (3 1/2 oz.) can flaked coconut, and 1/2 c. chopped pecans, drop by tablespoon onto foil-lined cookie sheets, place in oven and immediately turn it off, and do not open the door for 8 hours (yields about 3 dozen).

ID 567 — Lemon Chess Pie Combine 2 c. sugar and 4 eggs, mix together 1 Tbsp. flour and 1 Tbsp. cornmeal and add, then stir in 1/2 c. milk, 1/4 c. melted butter, and 1/2 c. lemon juice, pour into an unbaked pie shell, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 568 — Oatmeal Chocolate Chip Cookies Cream 1 c. butter-flavored shortening with 1 1/4 c. brown sugar and 1/2 c. sugar, beat in 2 eggs, 2 Tbsp. milk, and 2 tsp. vanilla, add 1 3/4 c. flour, 1 tsp. baking soda, then stir in 2 1/2 c. oatmeal, 2 c. chocolate chips, and 1 c. chopped nuts, drop by tablespoon on ungreased sheets, and bake at 375°F for 10 to 12 minutes.

ID 569 — Dirty Pudding Crush 1 small pkg. Oreo cookies and spread half in a 9 x 13-inch pan. Mix 1 large Cool Whip with 1 (8 oz.) cream cheese and 1 c. powdered sugar. In another bowl mix 2 (3 oz.) pkg. French vanilla instant pudding with 3 c. milk, combine mixtures, pour over crumbs, top with remaining crumbs, and refrigerate.

ID 570 — Pickled Bologna Boil together 1 1/2 qt. white vinegar, 1/2 c. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 tsp. pickling spice for 10 minutes, pour hot syrup over sliced bologna packed in a glass jar, cover, refrigerate, and use the next day.

ID 571 — Nutty Oven Fried Chicken Mix 1 c. biscuit mix with 1/3 c. finely chopped pecans, 2 tsp. paprika, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. poultry seasoning, and 1/2 tsp. dried sage. Dip chicken in 1/2 c. evaporated milk, coat with pecan mixture, drizzle with 1/3 c. melted margarine, and bake until done.

ID 572 — Wayne’s Cajun Bean Soup Cook chopped potatoes, onion, and celery until tender, add 3 cans Northern beans, 1 qt. tomatoes, 1 or 2 cans tomato soup, 1 1/2 tsp. chili powder, and 1 lb. sliced smoked sausage, simmer, and serve.

ID 573 — Grandma’s Cheesecake Melt 1 stick butter, mix with 1 1/2 c. graham cracker crumbs and 4 Tbsp. sugar, press into a springform pan, beat 3 (8 oz.) cream cheese bars with 1 c. sugar, egg yolks from 5 eggs, 1 pt. sour cream, and 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, pour into crust, and bake at 350°F.

ID 574 — Preacher Cookies Bring 2 c. sugar, 1 stick butter, and 1/2 c. milk to a boil and cook 3 minutes, remove from heat, stir in 1/2 c. powdered cocoa, 2 c. quick oats, and 1 tsp. vanilla, drop by teaspoon onto waxed paper, and cool (yields about 3 dozen).

ID 575 — Punch Bowl Cake Bake an 18.5 oz. yellow cake mix in two layers as directed, prepare 1 large box instant vanilla pudding, then layer cake, pudding, cherry pie filling, crushed pineapple, Cool Whip, frozen coconut, and chopped pecans in a punch bowl.

ID 576 — Sour Cream Apple Pie Line an unbaked 9-inch pie shell with sliced apples made from 3 to 4 tart green apples, mix 3/4 c. sugar, 1/3 c. flour, spices, and 1/4 c. butter, sprinkle over apples, bake at 350°F for 25 minutes, spread 1 c. sour cream on top, and bake 15 minutes more.

ID 577 — Meat Loaf Mix 1 1/2 lb. ground round with bread soaked in 1 c. milk, 1 beaten egg, 1/4 c. chopped onion, 1 1/4 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, and 1 Tbsp. catsup, pack into a loaf pan, and bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 hours.

ID 578 — Cumin Rice Dish Sauté 1 c. uncooked rice with chopped onion and bell pepper in 2 Tbsp. bacon fat until browned, add 2 cans consommé, 3/4 Tbsp. cumin, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, bring to a boil, cover, and simmer 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 579 — Prune Punch Cake Mix 1/2 c. Crisco, 1 c. sugar, 2 eggs, 1 c. prune juice, 1 c. cooked prunes, 2 c. flour, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 3/4 tsp. salt, and 1 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, bake at 350°F until done, then top warm cake with sugar mixed with orange juice.

ID 580 — Danish Cake Mix 1 c. shortening, 1 3/4 c. sugar, 3 eggs, 3 c. sifted flour, 1 1/2 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, 1 c. buttermilk, 1 Tbsp. orange juice, 1 c. nuts, 2 c. chopped dates, grated orange rind, and 1 tsp. vanilla, bake in a tube pan at 350°F for 1 1/4 hours, and pour sauce over cake while hot.

ID 581 — Sherried Beef Mix 1/2 envelope onion soup mix with 2 cans cream of celery soup and 3/4 can dry sherry, pour over 3 lb. chuck cubes, cover, bake at 325°F for 3 hours, stirring occasionally and adding water if needed.

ID 582 — Hot Fruit Punch Combine 1 (32 oz.) jar cranberry juice cocktail, 3 1/2 c. water, 1 (6 oz.) can frozen orange juice, 6 cinnamon sticks, and 12 whole allspice, and heat until hot.

ID 583 — French Potato Soup Cook peeled and diced red potatoes in water until tender, add 1 can evaporated milk with salt and pepper to taste, sauté finely chopped onion in 1 stick Parkay margarine, stir into soup, and simmer about 20 minutes.

ID 584 — Walla-Walla Onion Pie Sauté 4 thinly sliced sweet onions in olive oil and butter until golden, mix 2 eggs with 1 c. half-and-half, 2 Tbsp. flour, 1 tsp. salt, 1/8 tsp. pepper, and a pinch of nutmeg, stir in onions and half the Swiss cheese, pour into a partially baked crust, top with remaining cheese, and bake at 375°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 585 — Coal Flowers Place a piece of coal in a clear glass bowl, add water, blueing, salt, and coloring, and allow crystals to form.

ID 586 — Raisin-Walnut Bread Bring 1 1/4 c. raisins, 1 1/4 c. water, 1 1/2 tsp. baking soda, and 3 Tbsp. oil to a boil, cool, then mix with beaten eggs, 1 c. sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla, 2 c. flour, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1 c. chopped walnuts, and bake in a greased loaf pan at 350°F for 50 to 60 minutes.

ID 587 — Sausage Stars Combine 2 c. cooked crumbled sausage with Cheddar and Monterey Jack cheeses, ranch dressing mix, olives, and red peppers. Press wonton wrappers into greased mini muffin cups, brush with oil, bake 5 minutes, fill with sausage mixture, and bake 5 minutes more.

ID 588 — Dijon Chicken Sprinkle chicken breasts with salt, pepper, and garlic powder, mix 1 1/2 c. sour cream with 1 1/2 c. Dijon mustard, dip chicken in mixture, coat with Italian breadcrumbs, place in pans, and bake at 375°F for 50 minutes.

ID 589 — Sweet Potato or Pumpkin Cake Beat 5 eggs with 1 3/4 c. brown sugar, 3/4 c. butter, and 1 tsp. vanilla, add mashed sweet potatoes or pumpkin, sift in dry ingredients and spices, stir in raisins, pineapple with juice, and pecans, and bake in a Bundt pan at 325°F until done.

ID 590 — Bouillabaisse Cook 1 cup minced onions and 1/2 cup minced leeks slowly in 1/2 cup olive oil until tender but not browned. Add 4 mashed garlic cloves, 1 1/2 cups drained canned tomatoes or 1/4 tomato paste, 2 1/2 quarts water, 6 parsley sprigs, 1/2 tsp. thyme, 2 big pinches saffron, and 4 lb. fish heads (or 1 quart clam juice and reduce water to 1 1/2 quarts). Cook uncovered at a moderate boil for 30 minutes, then strain the stock and add salt and pepper to taste. Add clams and mussels first, cover and bring to a boil, cook about 5 minutes until some open, then add 6 to 8 lb. assorted fish and shellfish and 3 to 4 lb. firm white fish. After about 3 minutes add scallops and prawns and cook just until shellfish are open and prawns are pink. Taste continually and serve immediately with crusty French bread and Rouille.

ID 591 — Earthquake Cake Grease and flour or spray a 9 x 13-inch pan. Spread 1 cup coconut and 1 cup chopped pecans over the bottom, pour 1 German chocolate cake mix prepared according to package directions on top, then cream together 8 oz. Philadelphia cream cheese, 1 stick oleo, and 1 lb. confectioners sugar and drop by spoonfuls over the batter. Bake at 350°F for 45 minutes; the cake will look messy but tastes wonderful.

ID 592 — Ham Cheese Ball Cream 1 (8 oz.) package softened cream cheese with 1/4 cup mayonnaise, then mix in 2 cups ground chopped ham, 2 Tbsp. chopped parsley, 4 chopped green onions, 1/4 tsp. dried mustard, and 1/2 tsp. hot Tabasco. Chill 2 hours, shape into a ball, roll in 1 cup chopped pecans, and serve with crackers.

ID 593 — Orange Julius Put a couple of oranges and 2 Tbsp. honey into a blender, add crushed ice to desired thickness, then add about 1 cup milk or enough to fill the blender and blend well.

ID 594 — Quick Potato Salad Cook 2 lb. quartered red potatoes in boiling water for about 14 minutes until tender, drain, then toss with 1/2 cup diagonally sliced green onions, 1 small coarsely chopped green pepper, 1/2 cup salad dressing, and 1 Tbsp. coarse ground mustard; refrigerate before serving.

ID 595 — Banana Bread Cream 2/3 cup margarine with 1 1/2 cups sugar, add 2 eggs, then mix in sifted 1 1/2 cups flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, and 1/4 tsp. salt alternately with 4 Tbsp. milk. Stir in 1 cup mashed bananas, 1/2 cup chopped pecans, and 1 tsp. vanilla, pour into a greased loaf pan or cupcake tins, and bake at 350°F for about 45 minutes for a loaf or 25 minutes for cupcakes.

ID 596 — Smooth-N-Creamy Frosting Combine 1 (4 oz.) package Jell-O instant pudding, 1/4 cup confectioners sugar, and 1 cup cold milk, beat slowly until blended, then fold in 1 (8 oz.) Cool Whip and spread immediately; makes about 4 cups.

ID 597 — Plattar (Swedish Pancakes) Sift 1 cup flour into a bowl, add 2 Tbsp. sugar and 1/4 tsp. salt, then gradually stir in 3 eggs and 3 cups milk until smooth and let stand 2 hours. Butter a hot pancake pan, beat batter again, pour by tablespoonfuls, and fry on both sides until lightly browned; serve immediately with lingonberries.

ID 598 — Rhubarb and Orange Marmalade Wash and finely cut 6 cups rhubarb, mix with 6 cups sugar and let stand at least 2 hours, then add 2 oranges ground fine and boil about 20 minutes until thickened.

ID 599 — Chinese Chicken Salad Fry 1/4 package saifon noodles a little at a time in 1 inch hot oil until they puff and drain. Thinly slice 1 to 2 cooked chicken breasts, 1 head lettuce, 1 to 2 cucumbers, 2 to 4 stalks celery, 1 bell pepper, 1 to 2 bunches scallions, and 1 bunch radishes, refrigerate, then toss with noodles, 1 can wide wonton strips, and toasted 6 Tbsp. sesame seeds.

ID 600 — Shirley Temple Fill a highball glass with ice, add 1 dash grenadine, fill with about 6 oz. ginger ale, garnish with a maraschino cherry and orange slice, and serve immediately.

ID 601 — Nannaw’s Jam Cake Sift together 3 cups flour, 1 tsp. baking powder, and 1 1/2 tsp. soda, dissolve soda in 1 cup buttermilk, cream 2 sticks oleo with 2 cups sugar, 1 cup blackberry jam, and 6 eggs, then alternately add dry ingredients and liquid. Bake in three greased 9-inch pans at 350°F and frost between layers and on top.

ID 602 — Marinated Cucumber and Sweet Onion Salad Slice 2 cucumbers and 2 medium sweet onions, sprinkle with 1/4 tsp. salt and set aside. Heat 1/2 cup dark vinegar, 1/2 cup water, 1/4 cup sugar, and pepper to taste until hot but not boiling, pour over vegetables, cool, and refrigerate.

ID 603 — Irish Stew Combine 2 cans Castleberry pork BBQ, 2 cans Castleberry beef BBQ, 1 large can all-white chicken meat drained, 2 cans creamed corn undrained, and 2 cans stewed tomatoes in a crockpot and simmer on low several hours or cook gently on the stovetop.

ID 604 — Flaky Pie Crust Mix 1 cup warm milk, 1 cup solid shortening, and 2 cups self-rising flour in a bowl, turn onto a floured surface, cover with flour, and shape into a ball.

ID 605 — Frozen Salad Mix 2 glasses pimento cheese with 1 large can crushed pineapple, fold in 40 sliced marshmallows, optional walnuts, 1 cup Miracle Whip, and 1 pint whipped cream, spoon into cupcake liners, and freeze up to 6 months.

ID 606 — Doughnuts Mix 3 1/4 cups flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1/4 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. nutmeg, 2 beaten eggs, 2/3 cup sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla, 2/3 cup milk, and 1/4 cup margarine, cut shapes, and fry at 375°F about 1 minute per side.

ID 607 — Holiday Broccoli Cook 2 (10 oz.) packages frozen broccoli with 1 or 2 bouillon cubes until just tender, heat 2 cans cream of celery soup, pour over broccoli, garnish with 1/2 cup grated sharp cheese and pimento, and serve hot.

ID 608 — Crystal’s Cherry Delight Sprinkle graham crackers in the bottom of a pan, mix 1 (8 oz.) cream cheese with 1 (14 oz.) Eagle Brand milk and spread over crackers, top with 1 (14 oz.) cherry pie filling, refrigerate, and serve after 2 hours.

ID 609 — Pretty Party Punch Mix 1 liter Sprite or ginger ale, 1/2 can frozen apple juice concentrate, 1 bottle white grape juice, and juice of 1 1/2 lemons, chill well, and optionally float lemon slices on top.

ID 610 — Vinegar Pie Crust Combine 4 cups flour, 1 Tbsp. sugar, and a pinch of salt, cut in 1 3/4 cups shortening, beat together 1/2 cup cold water, 1 Tbsp. vinegar, and 1 egg, add to flour mixture, and mix just until a soft dough forms.

ID 611 — Macaroni Pie Boil 2 cups macaroni in salted water, drain, mix with 8 oz. Cheddar cheese, 3/4 cup milk, 1 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. pepper, and 1 beaten egg, pour into a casserole, dot with 1 Tbsp. butter, and bake at 450°F until browned.

ID 612 — Ice Cream Mix 6 beaten eggs with 1 1/2 cups sugar, 2 cans evaporated milk, 1 can condensed milk, and 3 tsp. vanilla, pour into freezer, add 1/2 gallon whole milk to fill, then freeze using ice and rock salt.

ID 613 — Power Cookies Cream 2 cups brown sugar, 2 cups granulated sugar, 3/4 cup butter, and 1 cup shortening, beat in 4 eggs and 2 tsp. vanilla, add 3 cups flour mixed with 2 tsp. salt and 2 tsp. soda, then stir in oats, coconut, raisins, chocolate chips, and nuts.

ID 614 — German Potato Salad Boil 6 cups potatoes whole, cool, peel and slice. Fry 1/2 lb. bacon and reserve 1/4 cup fat, cook 1/2 cup onion in fat, add flour, sugar, salt, celery seed, vinegar, water, pepper, sliced eggs, bacon, and potatoes, heat until bubbly, and serve warm.

ID 615 — Zucchini Relish Mix 10 cups ground zucchini, 4 cups onions, and 4 Tbsp. coarse salt, let stand overnight, drain and rinse, then cook with vinegar, spices, sugar, peppers, and pepper for 30 minutes, pack into jars, and process 5 minutes.

ID 616 — Vienna Coffee Blend 1/4 cup powdered nondairy creamer, 1/3 cup sugar, 1/2 cup instant coffee, and 1/2 tsp. cinnamon; use 1 Tbsp. per cup with boiling water.

ID 617 — Strawberry Bottom Cheesecake Pie Beat 4 oz. cream cheese with 1/4 cup sugar, add 1/2 cup sour cream, 1 tsp. vanilla, and fold in whipped topping. Spread 1 cup strawberry glaze in a graham crust, layer 1 pint sliced strawberries, cover with remaining glaze, top with cheese mixture, and chill 4 hours.

ID 618 — 7-Layer Cookies Melt 1 stick margarine, layer graham crackers in a 9 x 13-inch pan, drizzle butter, then layer 1 cup coconut, chocolate chips, butterscotch chips, condensed milk, and 1 1/2 cups pecans; bake at 350°F for 20 minutes and cool.

ID 619 — The Clergy Special Lift the phone, call the pizza place, turn on the TV, sit down, wait 20 to 30 minutes, and enjoy pizza with tomatoes, onions, peppers, cheese, ham, sausage, and pepperoni.

ID 620 — Thomas Jefferson’s Macaroni and Cheese Pudding Make a white sauce with 1/4 cup butter, 1/4 cup flour, and 2 1/2 cups milk, add 1 1/2 cups Cheddar, stir in cooked macaroni, salt, and pepper, pour into a casserole, top with remaining cheese, and bake at 400°F for 20 to 25 minutes.

ID 621 — Broccoli Almond Cook 2 (10 oz.) packages frozen chopped broccoli in boiling salted water and drain very well. Sauté 1/4 cup chopped onion in 1/4 cup butter until soft, blend in 2 Tbsp. flour, then add 1/2 cup milk and cook stirring constantly until thickened; stir in 1 (8 oz.) jar pasteurized process cheese spread plus 1/2 tsp. salt and 1/8 tsp. pepper until smooth, then remove from heat. Slowly stir a little of the hot cheese mixture into 2 well-beaten eggs, then combine everything with the broccoli, spoon into a greased 1 1/2-quart casserole, top with 1/2 cup bread crumbs tossed with 2 Tbsp. melted butter and 1/4 cup toasted slivered almonds, and bake at 325°F for 40 to 45 minutes until set.

ID 622 — Blueberry Muffins Cream 1 cup sugar with 1/4 cup softened butter, then add milk, 1 egg, 2/3 cup flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, 1/4 tsp. salt, 3/4 tsp. cinnamon, 3/4 tsp. nutmeg, and 1/2 tsp. vanilla and blend well. Stir in the remaining 2/3 cup flour just until moistened, fold in 3/4 to 1 cup blueberries, fill paper-lined muffin cups 3/4 full, and bake at 375°F for 20 to 30 minutes to yield 1 dozen.

ID 623 — Baked Pork Tenderloin Preheat oven to 325°F, place a 3 lb. pork tenderloin roast in a shallow pan and sprinkle with 1 tsp. salt and 1/2 tsp. pepper, then lay 6 slices bacon over the top. Bring 2 cups apple juice to a boil with 1/2 tsp. cinnamon and 1/2 tsp. cloves, remove from heat, brush pork with the spiced juice, and bake 1 1/2 to 2 hours, basting frequently, until tender.

ID 624 — Spinach Layer Salad Wash and dry 1 lb. bag spinach and spread in a glass 9 x 13-inch dish, layer on 4 sliced hard-boiled eggs, 1 can real bacon bits, 1 (8 oz.) box frozen peas, and 1 sliced red onion. Mix 1 1/2 cups mayonnaise with 1 (8 oz.) carton sour cream, spread over the top like frosting, grate 1 pkg. Swiss cheese over all, and refrigerate 24 hours.

ID 625 — Hot Crab Meat Dip Mix 4 packages (8 oz.) cream cheese with 2 (6 oz.) frozen or canned crab meat, 1/4 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/3 cup lemon juice, and 1/2 cup sherry cooking wine, bake at 300°F for 35 minutes, and serve with crackers.

ID 626 — Baked Cabbage Grease a 13 x 9-inch pan, cut 1 head cabbage into medium pieces and spread in the bottom. Brown 1 lb. ground chuck with 1/2 cup chopped onion, then stir in 1/2 cup rice, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/2 tsp. pepper and spoon over the cabbage. Bring 1 can tomato soup and 1 1/2 cups water to a boil, pour over the mixture, cover with foil, and bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 hours, then sprinkle with 1/4 cup Mozzarella cheese if you like.

ID 627 — Mixed Vegetable Casserole Cook 10 oz. frozen mixed vegetables for 15 minutes and drain, then stir in 1 cup chopped celery, 1 cup chopped onions, 1 cup grated sharp cheese, 1/2 cup mayonnaise, and salt and pepper to taste. Spoon into a casserole dish, top with bread crumbs, and bake at 350°F for 20 minutes.

ID 628 — Taffy Apple Salad Drain 1 large can crushed pineapple and save the juice, stir pineapple with 2 cups miniature marshmallows and refrigerate overnight. Cook the reserved juice with 1 well-beaten egg, 1 1/2 Tbsp. white vinegar, 1/2 cup sugar, and 1 Tbsp. flour until thickened (it won’t be very thick), then refrigerate overnight; fold in 2 cups diced unpeeled apples, 1 cup finely chopped salted peanuts, and 1 large Cool Whip before serving.

ID 629 — Fresh Apple Cake Stir together 1 1/2 cups Wesson oil, 2 cups sugar, 3 eggs, 2 1/2 cups plain flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. baking soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1 cup chopped pecans, a pinch of salt, and 3 cups chopped raw red apples, pour into a 9 x 13-inch pan, and bake at 350°F for 1 hour and 10 minutes.

ID 630 — Chicken & Spaghetti Casserole Cook 1 box spaghetti and set aside, cook 3 chicken breasts until done then cool and chop. Sauté 1/2 cup chopped onion, 1/2 cup chopped bell pepper, and 1/2 cup celery in 2 Tbsp. oleo, then add 1 can mashed tomatoes, 2 cups chicken broth, 1/4 tsp. red pepper, and 1/2 tsp. garlic salt and simmer 20 minutes; stir in spaghetti, chicken, and 1/2 Tbsp. chopped cheese.

ID 631 — Old Fashioned Strawberry Shortcake Blend 2 cups sugar with 3 cups self-rising flour, add 1 cup shortening (Wesson) and beat until smooth, then beat about 3 minutes, add 4 eggs and beat 1 minute, add 2 tsp. vanilla flavoring and beat about 3 minutes. Line and grease a pan, bake at 400°F for about 15 minutes to make 3 layers, stack with seven minute icing, and top with strawberries so they run down the sides.

ID 632 — Chicken, Broccoli and Cheese Casserole Boil 4 large chicken breasts off the bone and season with salt and pepper, remove skin, then cube the chicken. Boil 2 bunches fresh broccoli in 1/2 cup water for 2 minutes and drain, mix 1 can broccoli and cheese soup with 1/2 can milk, spread chicken mixture in a dish, top with broccoli, add 1 lb. mild Cheddar cheese on top, and bake at 350°F until the cheese melts.

ID 633 — Peach Cobbler Melt 1 stick butter in a baking dish in a 350°F oven, mix 1 cup sugar, 1 cup milk, and 1 cup self-rising flour, pour over the melted butter, drain the juice from 1 large can peaches and place peaches on top, then bake at 350°F for 1 hour until browned; it makes its own crust.

ID 634 — Party Wieners Stir 1/3 cup mustard with 2/3 cup grape jelly (or apple jelly), put in a crockpot, add 1/2 package Bryan little Smokies, and cook on high until hot or on low all day.

ID 635 — Cabbage Soup Melt 6 Tbsp. butter or margarine in a kettle and cook 4 lb. shredded cabbage with 2 chopped onions about 15 minutes, sprinkle in 2 Tbsp. flour and mix, then gradually stir in 6 cups water and bring to a boil. Add 1 (10 oz.) can condensed chicken bouillon or 4 bouillon cubes, 1 (1 lb.) can chopped tomatoes, 2 Tbsp. lemon juice, 2 Tbsp. sugar, 2 Tbsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. pepper, and 1 tsp. caraway seed, then simmer on low about 1 hour.

ID 636 — Cherry Congealed Salad Blend together 1 can cherry pie filling, 1 can crushed pineapple, 1 can Eagle Brand condensed milk, and 1 carton Cool Whip, then refrigerate until chilled.

ID 637 — Hot Sauce (To Can) Scald and peel 1 peck tomatoes, cut up or mash, and start cooking; meanwhile peel and grind 3 lb. onions and 5 to 10 hot peppers to taste, add to tomatoes along with 1 cup vinegar and 2 cups sugar, then cook until very thick, stirring and cooking slowly near the end so it doesn’t stick, and seal in jars (1/2-pint jars work well).

ID 638 — Yellow Cake In a bowl combine 3 cups all-purpose flour, 2 cups sugar, and 1 Tbsp. baking powder, add 1 1/2 cups milk, 1/2 cup softened margarine or butter, and vanilla, beat on low until combined then on high for 2 minutes, add 2 eggs and beat 2 minutes more, pour into two greased 9 x 1 1/2-inch round pans, and bake at 375°F for 25 to 30 minutes until a toothpick comes out clean; cool 10 minutes, remove from pans, and cool completely.

ID 639 — Microwave Zucchini-Beef Bake Heat 3 Tbsp. olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat, add 3 medium zucchini sliced 1/2-inch thick and cook turning often until lightly browned, about 5 minutes, drain briefly on paper towels, then arrange overlapping slices in a microwave-safe 9-inch square dish. Brown 1 lb. ground sirloin (90% lean) with 1 chopped small onion and 1 minced garlic clove, then stir in 1 cup tomato sauce, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. cinnamon, and 1/4 tsp. pepper; mix 1/2 cup low-fat cottage cheese with 1 egg and 1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese, layer as desired, and heat until hot and set (remaining microwave timing isn’t included in the provided lines).

ID 640 — Pumpkin Dream Pie Prepare Dream Whip using 1 pkg. Dream Whip with 1/2 cup milk and 1/2 tsp. vanilla as directed, then combine 1 cup of the prepared Dream Whip with 1 pkg. Jell-O instant vanilla pudding, 2/3 cup milk, 1 cup canned pumpkin, and 3/4 tsp. pumpkin pie spice and beat slowly until mixed. Pour into 1 baked 8-inch pie shell, chill about 2 hours until set, and top with the remaining Dream Whip.

ID 641 — Dill Rye Bread Dip Combine 1 pint sour cream, 3 Tbsp. parsley flakes, 2 tsp. Beau Monde, 2 tsp. dill weed, 1 pint Hellmann’s mayonnaise (no Miracle Whip), and 2 Tbsp. minced onion, then tear 3 packages corned beef lunch meat into small pieces and mix in. Cut a round “lid” from 1 round rye bread, hollow out the center, pour dip into the bread bowl, and arrange the reserved bread pieces around it for dipping.

ID 642 — Lucy Policella’s Ricotta Cheese Cake Bake 1 box white cake mix as directed (a 9 x 13-inch pan works), cool and slice in half. Beat 1 lb. Ricotta cheese with approximately 1/2 cup sugar (or to taste), stir in chocolate mini morsels, sprinkle rum over the bottom half, spread the ricotta mixture, top with the other half, then whip 1 small whipping cream whip with sugar to taste and frost the top and sides; refrigerate and it’s best made the day before.

ID 643 — Brown Rice Sauté 1 cup uncooked rice in 3/4 stick butter in a large frying pan until dark brown, adding 1 chopped medium white onion when the rice is about half browned, then stir in 1 can cream of mushroom soup and 1 can beef bouillon and simmer on low, stirring occasionally, until liquid is absorbed, about 20 to 30 minutes.

ID 644 — Jane’s Cheese Cake Beat 1 large and 1 small package cream cheese with 2 eggs, 1 tsp. vanilla, and 1/2 cup sugar, pour into a crumb crust, bake 15 minutes at 350°F, and cool 15 minutes, then mix 1 pint sour cream with 2 Tbsp. sugar and 1 tsp. vanilla to finish as desired (the remaining steps aren’t included in the provided lines).

ID 645 — Tomato Soup Cake Mix 3/4 cup shortening with 1 1/2 cups sugar, add 1 can tomato soup and 3/4 cup water, then stir in 3 cups flour (1/2 and 1/2 whole wheat), 3 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. baking soda, 1 tsp. cloves, 1 tsp. nutmeg, 1 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1 cup soaked and drained raisins, and 1 cup chopped nuts. Pour into a greased and floured 9 x 13-inch pan, bake at 325°F for 40 to 50 minutes, and frost with cream cheese frosting.

ID 646 — Spicy Home Fried Potatoes Boil 4 medium red potatoes until just cooked through, cut into bite-sized pieces, melt 1/2 stick butter in a skillet and sauté 1 chopped medium onion about 5 minutes, add potatoes and cook about 3 minutes, then season with red cayenne pepper, white pepper, black pepper, garlic powder, basil, Spanish paprika, and salt to taste.

ID 647 — Hot Sausage Pick-Ups Melt 10 oz. grated sharp cheese over hot water, work in 3 cups biscuit mix and 1 lb. extra hot bulk sausage, shape into bite-sized balls, and bake at 350°F for 10 to 15 minutes until golden; freeze unbaked balls and bake from frozen at 350°F for 20 to 25 minutes.

ID 648 — Light and Crunchy Chicken Salad Combine 2 cups cubed cooked chicken, 1/2 cup unpared diced apple, 2 Tbsp. chopped green pepper, 2 Tbsp. chopped celery, 1 Tbsp. finely chopped onion, and 1/4 cup bottled low calorie Italian dressing, chill well, then just before serving add 6 slices lite-line cheese and serve on lettuce leaves.

ID 649 — Peanut Butter Fudge Combine 1/2 cup evaporated milk, 1/2 cup creamy or chunky peanut butter, 1/2 cup Karo light or dark syrup, 1/2 cup firmly packed brown sugar, and 1/2 tsp. salt in a double boiler and cook over boiling water, stirring frequently, 15 to 20 minutes until thick.

ID 650 — Scotch Broth Combine 2 lb. meaty soup bones, 2 quarts water, 6 whole peppercorns, and 1 1/2 tsp. salt in a large kettle, cover, and simmer about 2 1/2 hours until meat comes easily off the bones. Remove bones, strain broth, cool and chill, skim off fat, remove meat from bones and dice it, then return meat to broth with 1 cup chopped carrots, 1 cup chopped celery, 1/4 cup medium pearl barley, 1 cup chopped turnips, and 1/2 cup chopped onion. Bring to a boil, reduce heat, cover, and simmer about 1 hour until vegetables are just tender, yielding 6 to 8 servings.

ID 651 — Peaches and Cream Cheesecake Beat together 3/4 cup flour, 1 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. salt, 3 Tbsp. butter, 1/2 cup milk, 1 egg, and a 3 1/4 oz. package vanilla pudding (not instant) for 2 minutes, pour into a greased 9-inch pie plate, drain 1 lb. can peaches reserving 2 Tbsp. juice and arrange peaches over batter, then mix 1/2 cup sugar with 8 oz. cream cheese and 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, spoon over peaches, and bake as directed in the original recipe.

ID 652 — Ragu Cheese Potatoes Peel, slice, and boil 7 to 10 white potatoes, drain, then layer half in a 9 x 13-inch dish, sprinkle lightly with shredded Cheddar cheese, salt, and pepper, add remaining potatoes, pour over 1 jar Ragu cheese sauce, sprinkle with more cheese, add 1 1/2 cups milk, season with salt and pepper, and bake at 350°F for 20 to 25 minutes.

ID 653 — Chicken Casserole Arrange 8 slices day-old bread with crusts removed in a 13 x 9 x 2-inch dish, top with 4 cups chopped cooked chicken, 1 jar sliced mushrooms, and 1 can drained water chestnuts. Beat 4 eggs with 2 cups milk, 1/2 cup mayonnaise, and 1/2 tsp. salt, pour over chicken, add 6 to 8 slices American cheese, 1 can cream of celery soup, 1 can cream of mushroom soup, and 2 oz. drained chopped pimentos, cover and refrigerate overnight, then toss reserved bread crusts with 2 Tbsp. melted oleo, sprinkle on top, and bake at 325°F for 1 1/4 hours, letting stand 10 minutes before serving.

ID 654 — Cherry Wink Cookies Cream 3/4 cup shortening with 1 cup sugar, blend in 2 eggs, 2 Tbsp. milk, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1/3 cup chopped cherries, and 1 cup chopped dates. Sift together 2 1/4 cups flour, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. baking powder, and 1/2 tsp. salt, add to mixture, shape into balls, roll in crushed corn flakes, and bake at 375°F for 12 to 15 minutes.

ID 655 — Chocolate Icing Combine 2 cups sugar, 1/2 cup evaporated milk, 3 to 5 Tbsp. cocoa, and 1 stick butter, bring to a boil for 2 minutes, remove from heat, add 1 tsp. vanilla, and beat until thick enough to spread.

ID 656 — Bourbon Pound Cake Cream 1 lb. butter with 2 cups sugar until light and fluffy, separate 8 eggs and add yolks one at a time beating well, add 2 tsp. almond extract and 2 tsp. vanilla extract, then add 3 cups cake flour alternately with 1/3 cup bourbon. Stir in 1/4 cup chopped pecans and finish baking and assembling as directed in the original recipe.

ID 657 — Beef and Green Beans Heat 1 Tbsp. oil in a wok or skillet, stir-fry 3 pressed garlic cloves and 1 quartered onion for 1 minute, add 1 lb. beef and stir-fry 5 minutes, remove meat, add 1 lb. French-cut green beans with 1/2 cup water, cover and simmer 5 minutes, then return beef and add 1 tsp. salt, 1 Tbsp. soy sauce, 1 Tbsp. black pepper, and 1 quartered tomato, serving hot with rice.

ID 658 — Persimmon Cookies Beat 1 cup persimmon pulp with 1/2 cup shortening and 1 tsp. baking soda until creamy, add 1 beaten egg, then stir in sifted 2 cups flour, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1/2 tsp. cloves, 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1 cup chopped nuts, and 1 cup raisins or chips. Drop by teaspoons onto greased sheets and bake at 375°F for 12 to 15 minutes.

ID 659 — Apple Hermits Soak 1 cup seedless raisins in hot water and drain, cream 1 cup shortening with 1 1/2 cups brown sugar, blend in 1/4 cup molasses and 3 eggs, then add 3 1/2 cups flour, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. baking soda, 3 tsp. cinnamon, 1 1/2 tsp. cloves, 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, 1 cup finely chopped apple, and 1 cup chopped nuts, mixing well and baking according to the original directions.

ID 660 — Carrot Cake Sift together 3 cups flour, 2 cups sugar, 3 tsp. baking powder, 1 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, and 1/2 tsp. cloves, add 1 1/2 cups oil, 4 eggs, 3/4 cup walnuts, and 12 oz. strained baby carrots, pour into a 13 x 9 1/2-inch pan, and bake at 350°F until done, about 1/2 hour or longer as needed.

ID 661 — Cornbread Dressing Crumble 1 pan cornbread and 6 slices white bread, moisten with stock or water, sauté 1/2 lb. ground meat in 1 stick butter with 1 chopped onion, 1 chopped bell pepper, 6 minced garlic cloves, thyme, celery salt, salt, and pepper, mix with bread, toss lightly with 2 slightly beaten eggs, place in a greased dish, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.

ID 662 — Black-Eyed Mullet Break 1/2 lb. smoked or grilled mullet into pieces and set aside, lightly mash 2 cans black-eyed peas, cook peas with 1/2 cup chopped onions, 1/2 cup chopped green pepper, 2 tsp. minced garlic, 1 tsp. hot pepper sauce, 1 tsp. salt, and 1/4 cup cider vinegar for 10 minutes, then add mullet and heat through, serving immediately.

ID 663 — Sparerib Sauce Mix 1/4 cup dark molasses, 1/4 cup ketchup, 1/4 cup orange juice concentrate, 2 Tbsp. vinegar, 2 Tbsp. vegetable oil, and chopped onion, then spread over ribs before cooking.

ID 664 — Chilled Peanut Soup Blend 3/4 cup roasted peanuts with 1 can beef broth until smooth, pour into a saucepan, add remaining 2 cans broth, 1 1/2 cups half and half, and 3/4 tsp. chili powder, bring to a boil, simmer 15 minutes, chill well, and serve cold.

ID 665 — Cabbage Rolls Mix 3 lb. ground beef with 2 cups uncooked rice, 3 tsp. onion powder or 1 large onion, 1 tsp. garlic powder, 3 tsp. salt, 2 Tbsp. parsley, 2/3 cup Parmesan cheese, and 1 can tomato sauce. Scald 2 large cabbage heads, fill leaves with mixture, roll, layer with chopped cabbage and 1 can washed sauerkraut, add 1 large jar Ragu plus water, and cook 1 1/2 hours; makes about 40 rolls.

ID 666 — Broccoli Rice Casserole Cook 1 (16 oz.) package frozen chopped broccoli, mix with 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 1/2 cups uncooked Minute rice, 1 (8 oz.) jar Cheez Whiz, 1 stick margarine, and 1/2 cup chopped onion, pour into an 8-inch dish, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes or microwave as directed.

ID 667 — Easy Chicken Cacciatore Sauté cubed 1 lb. boneless skinless chicken breasts in 2 Tbsp. olive oil and 1 Tbsp. butter, season with garlic powder, onion powder, and Italian seasoning, add 2 cans diced tomatoes, 2 cans olives, and 2 cans mushrooms, simmer 10 minutes, and serve over pasta with Parmesan cheese.

ID 668 — Pineapple Cake Mix 1 box Duncan Hines butter cake mix with 1/2 cup oil, 4 eggs, and 1 (11 oz.) can chopped mandarin oranges with juice, then bake at 350°F for about 20 minutes in layers or a single pan.

ID 669 — Ambrosia Mold Dissolve 1 package orange gelatin in 2 cups boiling water, add reserved pineapple juice to measure 1 cup, chill until slightly thickened, whisk in 1 3/4 cups Cool Whip, then fold in crushed pineapple, mandarin oranges, marshmallows, and coconut, pour into a mold, and chill until firm.

ID 670 — Cranberry Soufflé Dissolve 2 envelopes unflavored gelatin with 1/4 tsp. salt in 1 cup water over low heat, add lemon juice and rind, chill until thickened, fold in beaten egg whites with 1/4 cup sugar, add cranberry sauce, walnuts, and mandarin oranges, pour into a mold, and chill thoroughly.

ID 671 — Bourbon Sweet Potatoes Mix 2 cans mashed sweet potatoes with 3/4 cup brown sugar, 1/2 cup melted butter, 1/4 to 1/3 cup bourbon, and 1/2 tsp. vanilla, chill overnight, bake at 350°F for 25 minutes, top with 2 cups marshmallows, and bake 7 minutes more.

ID 672 — Dry Meat Seasoning Mix 6 Tbsp. salt, 1 cup sugar, 1 tsp. dry lemon peel powder, 2 tsp. Accent, 2 1/2 Tbsp. black pepper, and 2 tsp. paprika and use as desired.

ID 673 — Stuffed Mushrooms Cook 1/2 to 3/4 lb. bacon until crisp, mix with 8 oz. softened cream cheese and Lawry’s seasoned salt to taste, stuff into 12 oz. mushroom caps, and bake until hot.

ID 674 — Party Mints Mix 4 oz. cream cheese with 1/4 tsp. oil of peppermint and 1 box powdered sugar, shape as desired, and chill to set.

ID 675 — Reuben Casserole Layer cooked wide noodles, drained sauerkraut, corned beef, and diced tomatoes in a 9 x 13-inch dish, dot with Thousand Island dressing, sprinkle with Swiss cheese, bake covered at 350°F for 40 minutes, uncover, top with crushed rye crackers, and bake 10 minutes more.

ID 676 — Cheese and Chilies Beat 2 eggs with 2 Tbsp. milk, mix in 2 cans chopped green chilies and grated Swiss and cheddar cheeses, pour into a square dish, top with Monterey Jack cheese, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes until bubbly.

ID 677 — Rhubarb Cake Layer 5 cups chopped rhubarb, raspberry Jell-O, 1 cup sugar, and 3 cups marshmallows in a greased 9 x 13-inch dish, pour prepared yellow cake mix over, bake at 350°F about 1 hour, invert onto foil to cool, and serve with whipped cream.

ID 678 — The Best Sweet and Sour Cook 1/2 cup green pepper chunks and 1/2 cup onion chunks in 1 Tbsp. oil, add a sauce of pineapple syrup, vinegar, brown sugar, water, soy sauce, cornstarch, and catsup, cook until thick, stir in pineapple chunks, and serve over meat or tofu.

ID 679 — English Toffee Bars Line a 13 x 9-inch pan with foil, cover with graham crackers, boil 1 cup brown sugar with 1 cup margarine, pour over crackers, bake at 400°F 5 minutes, sprinkle with chocolate pieces and nuts, chill, and break into pieces.

ID 680 — Fruit Cobbler Cream 1/2 cup sugar with 1/4 cup butter, add 1 egg, 1/2 cup milk, baking powder, salt, and vanilla, spread in an 8-inch pan, mix peaches with honey and boiling water, pour on top, and bake at 375°F until golden.

ID 681 — No Bake Cookies Boil 2 cups sugar, 1/2 cup milk, 1/2 cup margarine, and 4 Tbsp. cocoa for 2 minutes, remove from heat, add 1/2 cup peanut butter, 2 1/2 cups oats, 1/4 cup nuts, and 2 tsp. vanilla, drop by spoonfuls, and cool.

ID 682 — Cream Cheese Rolls Mix 8 oz. cream cheese with 8 oz. sour cream, 2 tsp. picante sauce, and 1/2 chopped onion, spread on 10 tortillas, roll tightly, chill overnight, slice, and serve.

ID 683 — Wedding Bell Lemonade Punch Combine frozen lemonade and pineapple concentrate with water, chill, then add ginger ale, sparkling water, and ice just before serving to make about 50 servings.

ID 684 — Zucchini Bread Blend 3 eggs, 1 cup oil, 1 Tbsp. vanilla, 2 cups sugar, and 2 cups grated zucchini, mix with dry ingredients, add raisins or pecans if desired, pour into pans, and bake at 325°F for 1 to 1 1/2 hours.

ID 685 — Barbecue Turkey Loaf Mix stuffing, vegetables, water, and butter and let stand, combine turkey, eggs, and barbecue sauce, layer with cheese and vegetable mixture, top with sauce, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes or microwave as directed.

ID 686 — Haupia Cook 3 cans coconut milk with 1/3 cup sugar, 1/2 cup cornstarch, and a dash of salt over medium heat until thickened, then pour into a greased 9-inch pan to set.

ID 687 — Onion Casserole Layer 4 cups sliced onions, mushroom soup, melted butter, almonds, and crushed cornflakes in a casserole and bake uncovered at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 688 — Warm Apple Crisp Toss 6 cups sliced apples with 1/3 cup sugar, cinnamon, salt, and melted butter, place in a greased dish, and top with a mixture of sugar, flour, and butter, baking until bubbly and golden.

ID 689 — Hamburger and Macaroni Casserole Brown 1 lb. hamburger with diced onion, cook and drain macaroni, mix with 2 cans tomato soup, combine everything, and bake at 350°F for 30 minutes, topping with cheese if desired.

ID 690 — One-Rise Monkey Bread Prepare a yeast dough with flour, sugar, salt, yeast, warm water, butter, and egg, knead briefly, cut into pieces, dip in melted butter, layer in a tube pan with optional poppy seeds, let rise once, and bake at 375°F for 20 to 25 minutes.

ID 691 — Easy “Apple Festival” Pie (Microwave) Layer 4 sliced apples with brown sugar and cinnamon, top with a crumb mixture of flour, oats, sugar, butter, cinnamon, and nutmeg, and microwave on high for 11 minutes total, rotating halfway.

ID 692 — Dressed Eggs Halve 12 hard-boiled eggs, mash yolks with sweet relish, celery seed, chives, sugar, salad dressing, salt, and pepper, refill whites, and sprinkle tops.

ID 693 — Strawberry Pizza Mix melted butter, flour, brown sugar, and pecans, press into a pan and bake at 350°F 20 to 25 minutes, cool, spread with a cream cheese and confectioners sugar mixture folded with Cool Whip, top with cooked strawberry glaze and fresh strawberries, and chill.

ID 694 — Pumpkin Bread Mix dry ingredients, add oil, water, eggs, and pumpkin, pour into greased loaf pans, and bake at 350°F for 55 minutes, adding raisins if desired.

ID 695 — Santa Fe Nachos Top tortilla chips with cheese and slices of summer sausage, microwave until melted, then garnish with jalapeños, olives, guacamole, and tomatoes.

ID 696 — Frozen Raspberry Salad Dissolve raspberry Jell-O in hot water, add raspberries, mix with cream cheese, sour cream, cranberry sauce, and salt, freeze until firm, cut, and serve.

ID 697 — Coconut Chews Cream shortening with confectioners sugar, add flour, press into a pan and bake briefly, top with a mixture of eggs, brown sugar, flour, baking powder, salt, vanilla, walnuts, and coconut, bake again, ice while warm, cool, and cut into bars.

ID 698 — Rice-Broccoli Casserole Sauté onion and celery in margarine, cook rice and broccoli, combine with soups and cheese spread, bake at 375°F 10 minutes, and serve or refrigerate before baking.

ID 699 — Party Mix Toss Cheerios, Corn Chex, pretzels, and nuts with melted butter, Worcestershire sauce, garlic salt, and celery salt, bake at 250°F for 30 minutes stirring once.

ID 700 — Fettucini with Lemon Vegetables Cook fettucini, sauté vegetables in butter with lemon peel, heat milk and cream cheese until smooth, stir in Parmesan, toss with noodles, season with salt and pepper, and serve vegetables on top.

ID 701 — Easy Banana Pudding Prepare 2 large pkg. instant vanilla pudding as directed on the package, then stir in 1 (12 oz.) container Cool Whip. Layer the bottom of a 9 x 13-inch dish with 1 box vanilla wafers, top with 1/2 of the bananas (about 6), pour on 1/2 of the pudding mixture, then add another layer of vanilla wafers and bananas, pour on the remaining pudding mixture, top with vanilla wafers, cover, and refrigerate overnight.

ID 702 — Apricot Nectar Cake Combine 1 box lemon supreme cake mix, 3/4 c. cooking oil, 1 c. apricot nectar, and 1/2 c. sugar, then add 4 eggs one at a time. Bake at 350° for 45 minutes to 1 hour.

ID 703 — Chicken Or Turkey Casserole Mix 1/2 Tbsp. garlic salt, 1 (8 oz.) sour cream, 1 small onion chopped (1/4 c.), 1/2 c. milk, and 1 can cream of chicken soup, then add about 2 c. chopped chicken or turkey. Top with crushed Ritz crackers, chip butter on top, and bake at 300° for 30 to 40 minutes.

ID 704 — Strawberry Salad Dissolve 2 large pkg. strawberry Jell-O in 2 c. boiling water, then add the remaining water to make 4 c. hot water total and let it set until it begins to thicken; stir in 1 pt. strawberries, 3 bananas diced, and 1 c. chopped pecans, let stand until firm, spread 1 large container Cool Whip on top, and refrigerate.

ID 705 — Maple-Bacon Oven Pancake Heat oven to 425°, grease and flour a 9 x 13-inch pan, beat 1 1/2 c. Bisquick, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 3/4 c. milk, 1/4 c. syrup, and 2 eggs with a hand beater along with 1 cup of the 1 1/2 c. shredded cheese (reserve bacon and the remaining cheese), pour into the pan, bake uncovered 10 to 15 minutes, sprinkle with bacon and the remaining cheese, then bake 3 to 4 minutes more until the cheese is melted (serves 8 to 10).

ID 706 — Coca-Cola Pork Chops Place 8 pork chops in a baking pan and season with salt and pepper to taste, mix 1 c. catsup with 1 c. Coca-Cola and pour over the pork chops, sprinkle with brown sugar, and bake at 350° for 1 hour.

ID 707 — Fruit Salad Cook 3 oz. pkg. vanilla pudding in the fruit juices until it boils, then pour over 2 cans mandarin oranges, 2 cans pineapple chunks, 4 bananas sliced, strawberries, and grapes; eat immediately or refrigerate, and it’s also great with vanilla ice cream.

ID 708 — Dirty Rice Bring 8 cups water and 1 tablespoon salt to a boil, add 3 c. raw rice, cover, bring back to a full boil, turn off the heat, and leave covered on the burner 30 minutes; sauté 1 lb. hamburger and 1 lb. hot sausage, sauté 1 green pepper chopped and 2 c. celery chopped, then combine everything with the cooked rice and add 2 c. green onions chopped (this makes a lot and can be cut in half).

ID 709 — Sunday Dinner Put 1 pick of the chick pack, 5 potatoes peeled and cut up, 3 carrots peeled and cut up, and 1 jar Chicken Tonight (French) into a roasting pan in the order given, cover, and bake at 325° to 350° from 8:30 a.m. until you get home from church; skin the chicken to remove as much fat as possible and serve with salad or applesauce.

ID 710 — Chocolate Macaroon Bars Preheat oven to 350°, combine 1 1/4 c. graham cracker crumbs, 1/3 c. sugar, 1/4 c. cocoa, and 1/3 c. melted margarine, press firmly into the bottom of a 13 x 9-inch baking pan, and bake 10 minutes.

ID 711 — Chicken Breasts In Lemon Sauce Cut 4 boneless, skinless chicken breast halves (about 1 1/2 lb.) horizontally to make 2 thin slices each, coat with 1/2 c. all-purpose flour, heat 1/4 c. butter in a 12-inch skillet over medium heat, and cook the chicken with 2 tsp. chopped garlic in the butter for 4 to 6 minutes, turning once, until browned; add 1 c. dry white wine or apple juice and 2 Tbsp. lemon juice, sprinkle with 1/2 tsp. pepper, heat until hot, and sprinkle with 1 Tbsp. large capers, drained, if desired.

ID 712 — Spaghetti Meat Sauce Brown 1 lb. ground beef in a small Dutch oven until crumbly and drain well, stir in 1 (8 oz.) can tomato sauce, 1 c. water, 2 Tbsp. dried onion flakes, 2 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/2 tsp. garlic powder, and 1/4 tsp. pepper, bring to a boil over medium heat, cover and simmer 20 minutes stirring occasionally, add 1 (14 oz.) jar spaghetti sauce and simmer uncovered 20 minutes, cook 8 oz. spaghetti as directed and drain, then spoon meat sauce over spaghetti and sprinkle with grated Parmesan cheese (yields 4 servings).

ID 713 — Old Fashion Punch Combine 2 Tbsp. sugar, 2 Tbsp. bitters, 2 1/2 c. whiskey, and 1/2 c. water, then just before serving add an ice ring and 2 quarts chilled 7-Up and decorate with sliced oranges and maraschino cherries.

ID 714 — Dill Dip Mix 1 c. Hellmann’s mayonnaise, 1 c. sour cream, 1 Tbsp. minced onion, 1 tsp. seasoned salt, and 1/2 tsp. dill weed together, then let sit for 1 hour.

ID 715 — Zucchini Stew Heat 1/4 c. oil in a large saucepot, add 2 large zucchini cut in large cubes, 2 green or red peppers cut up, 2 onions chopped, and 3 medium size tomatoes peeled and sliced, cover with a lid (do not add water because water cooks out of zucchini), cook until zucchini is soft about 1 hour, then add 1 can green beans drained last, and it’s especially good served with cooked smoked sausage or ham.

ID 716 — Party Potatoes Prepare 4 c. mashed potatoes as you normally would but do not use salt, then add 1 pkg. Hidden Valley Ranch dressing mix.

ID 717 — Gran’s Toll House Cookies Sift 1 1/2 c. sifted flour once before measuring, then sift with 1 tsp. soda and 1 tsp. salt; cream 1 c. shortening until soft, add 3/4 c. brown sugar firmly packed and 3/4 c. granulated sugar gradually and cream until light and fluffy, add 2 eggs (unbeaten) one at a time beating after each, add 1 tsp. hot water, then add the sifted dry ingredients, stir in 1 c. nut meats cut fine (optional), 2 (14 oz.) pkg. Nestle semi-sweet chocolate in pieces, and 2 c. oatmeal (quick or regular; uncooked), add 1 tsp. vanilla and blend well, drop by half teaspoons on a greased cookie sheet, and bake at 375° for 8 minutes (makes 100).

ID 718 — Hominy Casserole (Large Recipe; Make Half) Butter a dish and cook 1/2 large onion in 1/2 stick oleo, then add 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 2 cans yellow hominy drained, and 1 small jar hot Cheez Whiz (jalapeno Whiz), pour into the buttered dish, crush some Fritos on top, and bake at 350° until it bubbles, about 35 to 45 minutes.

ID 719 — “Glop” Cook and drain 2 c. dry macaroni (cooked) and 8 oz. rigatoni or other favorite pasta, then while it’s cooking heat 1/4 c. olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat, add 1 lb. medium shrimp peeled and deveined, 1 green pepper cut into short thin strips, 1 yellow or red pepper cut into short thin strips, 1 c. sliced mushrooms, 3 cloves garlic minced, and 1 Tbsp. dry basil crumbled, cook stirring frequently until shrimp are cooked through and peppers are almost tender (3 to 4 minutes), stir in 2 medium tomatoes coarsely chopped and 1 c. picante sauce and simmer 2 to 3 minutes stirring frequently, add pasta and mix well, and serve with grated Parmesan cheese and additional picante sauce if desired.

ID 720 — Poached Chicken Breast In Wine Place 4 (4 oz.) skinned, boned chicken breast halves between two sheets of heavy-duty plastic wrap and flatten to 1/4 inch, combine 3/4 c. Chablis or other dry wine with 2 1/2 c. sliced fresh mushrooms, 2 Tbsp. chopped fresh parsley, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. pepper in a large skillet and bring to a boil over high heat, arrange chicken in a single layer, cover and reduce heat and simmer 15 minutes or until tender, remove chicken to a serving plate, mix 1 Tbsp. cornstarch with 2 tsp. water and stir into the skillet, bring to a boil and boil 1 minute stirring constantly, then pour sauce over chicken (yields 4 servings).

ID 721 — Quick Spanish Rice Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground meat with 1 onion, season with salt and pepper to taste, add 2 cans Brown Beauty Spanish rice and 1 or 2 cans Ranch Style beans and heat to boiling, pour into a casserole, top with 1 lb. Cheddar cheese, add 1 tsp. chili powder if desired, and serve with Doritos and a salad (great for camping).

ID 722 — Glazed Pecans In one bowl beat 1 tbsp. water with 1 egg white until frothy but not stiff, in a second bowl mix 1 c. sugar with 1 tsp. salt and 1 tsp. cinnamon, preheat oven to 300 degrees, stir 1 lb. pecan halves into the egg white mixture until evenly coated, add the sugar mixture, spread on a large cookie sheet sprayed with Pam, bake at 300 degrees for 30 minutes stirring every 15 minutes (including after the last 15 minutes), then pour onto waxed paper until cooled and store in an airtight container.

ID 723 — Crock Pot Pizza Brown 1 1/2 pounds hamburger with 1 chopped onion and 1 chopped green pepper and drain, add 2 small jars pizza sauce and simmer, cook and drain 1 large bag noodles, then layer meat, noodles, 1 can mushrooms, 1 bag pizza cheese, and 1 package pepperoni in the crock pot and cook on low for 90 minutes.

ID 724 — Summer Squash Casserole Cook 2 lb. yellow sumer squash or zucchini sliced (6 c.) with 1/4 c. chopped onion in boiling salted water for 5 minutes and drain, mix 1 can condensed cream of chicken soup with 1 c. dairy sour cream and stir in 1 c. shredded carrot, fold in the drained squash and onion, mix 1 (8 oz.) pkg. herb seasoned stuffing mix (Pepperidge Farm; not cubed) with 1/2 c. butter or margarine melted, spread half the stuffing mixture in the bottom of a 9 x 13-inch baking dish, spoon the vegetable mixture on top, sprinkle with remaining stuffing, and bake at 350° for 25 to 30 minutes or until heated through.

ID 725 — Green Jello Salad Dissolve 2 pkg. lime Jell-O in 1 cup boiling water, add 1 cup cold water, mix in 1 carton cottage cheese, 1 can drained crushed pineapple, 1 Tbsp. sugar, and 1 tsp. white vinegar, then chill until set.

ID 726 — German Potatoes Brown 1 small onion chopped in 2 Tbsp. butter, add 6 medium potatoes cut in cubes plus 4 Tbsp. parsley chopped and salt and pepper, barely cover with hot water, cover and cook until potatoes are tender (serves 6).

ID 727 — Fullabull’s Shepherd’s Pie Brown 1 1/2 lb. ground beef with 1 onion chopped and drain well, spread in a 13 x 9-inch pan, pour over 2 cans mixed vegetables (drained), mix 2 envelopes of the 3 envelopes brown gravy mix and pour over the layers, then continue with the 8 servings instant potatoes as the topping (remaining steps are not included in the provided lines).

ID 728 — Sauteed Bananas Peel bananas, cut in half lengthwise and again cut in half crosswise, sprinkle with flour, sauté in butter until delicately brown, drain, and sprinkle with confectioners sugar.

ID 729 — Never Fail Jello Salad Dissolve 1 large jello (any flavor) in 1 c. boiling water, partly dissolve 1 c. small marshmallows in the jello mixture, then add 1 c. cottage cheese, 1/2 c. mayonnaise, 1 (20 oz.) can crushed pineapple (not drained), and 9 oz. Cool Whip or small Cool Whip, then pour into a mold or pretty glass dish, remembering not to drain the pineapple.

ID 730 — Fruit Cobbler Melt 3/4 stick margarine and pour into a 2-inch deep dish, add fruit of your choice (I use peaches, strawberries, blackberries, cherries, etc.), mix 1 c. sugar with 1 c. milk and 1 c. flour, pour over fruit without stirring, and bake at 350° until brown or fruit is done (approximately 30 minutes).

ID 731 — Poppy Seed Cake Beat 4 eggs, 1/4 c. poppy seed, 1/2 c. pineapple juice, 1 tsp. almond extract, 1/2 c. shortening, and 1/2 c. rum for 2 minutes, then add 1 pkg. white cake mix and 1 pkg. instant vanilla pudding and beat 2 more minutes, grease a Bundt pan, pour in batter, dust top with cinnamon-sugar, bake at 350° for 45 to 55 minutes, and when cool sprinkle with powdered sugar.

ID 732 — Magloubeh Soak 1 lb. rice for 1 hour in warm water, cook 2 lb. chicken or lamb in water, remove the meat and add a little butter or margarine to the water, use this leftover water with the rice, fry 2 large eggplant and 1 head cauliflower in cooking oil (and a few potatoes sliced thin if optional), then in a large pot layer the meat on the bottom, then the eggplant and cauliflower, then the rice and the meat water on top, cover and cook to a boil until the water begins to dry (about 15 to 20 minutes), turn heat down to low until it is all dry, turn heat off and let set for 20 to 30 minutes, then turn upside down onto a platter and serve with yogurt or salad (season with salt and pepper to taste and 1/2 tsp. bahar).

ID 733 — Whole Wheat Carrot Cake Blend 1 c. oil with 1 c. brown sugar and 1 c. sugar until mixed, add 1 tsp. vanilla and beat in 4 eggs one at a time, in another bowl blend 1/3 c. dry milk powder, 1 tsp. baking powder, 2 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, and 2 c. whole wheat flour, add dry ingredients to the egg mixture until well blended, stir in 3 c. finely shredded carrots and 1 c. chopped walnuts by hand, pour into a greased and floured tube or Bundt pan, bake at 350° for 50 to 60 minutes, cool in pan, invert onto serving plate, and sprinkle with powdered sugar (optional glaze or cream cheese icing).

ID 734 — Pickled Squash Soak 8 c. sliced squash, 8 c. sliced onions, and 5 bell peppers sliced in 1 gal. water with 1 c. salt for 1 hour, then drain and rinse well (remaining steps using 2 c. vinegar, 3 c. sugar, 2 tsp. mustard seed, 2 tsp. celery seed, and 1 tsp. curry powder are not included in the provided lines).

ID 735 — Pasta Salad Dice and mix together 1/4 lb. Provolone cheese, 1/4 lb. salami, 1/4 lb. pepperoni, 1 large pepper, 1 small jar olives, 3 tomatoes, 2 onions, 3 stems celery, and 1 box medium shells cooked and drained.

ID 736 — Vegetable Burger Soup Brown 1 lb. ground beef and drain off fat, stir in 2 cups of water plus 1 (16 oz.) can tomatoes, 1 (8 oz.) can tomato sauce, 1 (10 oz.) pkg. frozen mixed vegetables, 1/4 c. dry onion soup mix, and 1 tsp. sugar, bring to a boil, reduce heat, cover, and simmer 20 minutes (serves 6 to 8).

ID 737 — Corn Light Bread Mix 2 c. self-rising meal, 1/2 c. plain flour, 3/4 c. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. soda, 2 c. buttermilk, and 1 Tbsp. lard, pour into a regular size loaf pan, bake at 350° for 1 hour, and let cool before serving.

ID 738 — Salad Luncheon Beans Brown 1/2 to 1 lb. ground beef with 1 medium onion chopped and drain, then in a 2-quart baking dish mix (do not drain) 1 large (28 oz.) can Bush’s beans, 1 (15 1/2 oz.) can butter beans, 1 (15 oz.) can red kidney beans, and 1 (16 oz.) can pork and beans with the beef, then add 1/2 c. catsup, 1 Tbsp. mustard, 1/4 c. brown sugar, and 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce and bake on low heat for 5 to 6 hours.

ID 739 — Crustless Pumpkin Pie Beat 3 eggs, mix in 3/4 c. honey, 1/2 tsp. ginger, 1/2 tsp. nutmeg, 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1 3/4 c. pumpkin or sweetened squash, add 1 c. canned milk, butter or oil a deep 9-inch pie pan, pour in mixture, bake at 325° for 1 hour, and cool thoroughly before cutting.

ID 740 — D’s Danish Mix 4 c. flour with 3 tsp. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 c. oleo as for pie crust, dissolve 1 pkg. yeast in 1 c. warm milk and add to 3 eggs beaten, mix dry and liquid ingredients thoroughly and refrigerate overnight, then bring to room temperature and turn out onto a floured board, knead well and rest a bit, divide dough into 4 parts, roll one part thin as for pie crust and brush with melted butter, sprinkle with sugar, cinnamon, nuts and/or raisins or spread with a filling such as poppy seed or dates, roll tightly, bake as is or slice 3/4 inch thick and bake in muffin tins, bake at 375° about 20 minutes and use sugar/lemon icing if desired, then repeat with the other 3 parts.

ID 741 — Picnic Potato Salad Coarsely dice 1 1/2 cooked potatoes and 3 hard-boiled eggs with 3/4 tsp. salt, dash of pepper, and 1/2 tsp. celery seed, add 1/2 c. diced cucumbers, 1/2 c. chopped onion, 1/4 c. grated carrots, 1/2 c. diced celery, and 1/2 c. sweet pickles/relish, mix 3/4 c. salad dressing with 2 Tbsp. prepared mustard and pour over, toss until well coated adding more salad dressing as needed, then add 1/4 c. bacon bits or shredded cheese and garnish with 1 medium tomato wedged.

ID 742 — Ribbon Layer Jello Make 4 (3 oz.) pkg. jello separately using 1 c. hot water and 1/2 c. cold water for each, dissolve 2 pkg. Knox gelatine in 1/2 cup cold water and set aside, bring 2 c. milk with 1 c. sugar to a boil, add gelatine mixture plus 1 pt. sour cream and 2 tsp. vanilla, beat until thick about 10 minutes, divide into 3 parts, then layer jello and the creamy mixture in the desired order, letting each layer set 45 minutes before adding the next (for example red on top for Christmas or green on top for St. Pat’s day), and note it’s time consuming but very decorative.
