ID 743 — Chicken Fettucini In a double boiler melt 1 c. butter with 4 chicken bouillon cubes, stir in 8 shallots chopped, 1 c. whipping cream, 1/4 lb. mushrooms sliced, pepper, and 1 c. Parmesan cheese and simmer until mushrooms are soft and cheese is melted, add 1 chicken cooked deboned and sliced or chopped and heat until warm, then pour sauce over 1 lb. fettucini cooked and drained, tossing gently, and garnish with additional Parmesan cheese and parsley.

ID 744 — “Spicy” Cake Preheat oven to 350°, cut 1/2 c. walnuts, 1/2 c. raisins, 1/2 c. dried apricots, and 1 apple into pieces, add 2 1/2 c. wheat flour to it, then incorporate 4 eggs, 1 3/4 c. brown sugar, salt, 1 Tbsp. allspice, 1 Tbsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. cardamom, 1 tsp. cilantro, 1 tsp. ginger, and 1/2 tsp. cloves (remaining steps are not included in the provided lines).

ID 745 — Lemon Chip Cookies Mix 2 c. flour, 1/2 c. sugar, 3 oz. cream cheese, and 1/2 c. margarine, pack into a 9 x 13-inch pan and bake 15 to 20 minutes at 350°, mix 4 eggs, 1 c. sugar, 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/3 c. lemon juice, 1/4 c. flour, and 1 c. lemon chips, pour over the baked bottom, bake at 350° for 25 minutes, cool, and cut into squares.

ID 746 — Pineapple Pie Sift 1 c. sugar with 1 Tbsp. plain flour, mix with 3 eggs separated, 1 (8 oz.) can crushed pineapple, 1 tsp. vanilla, margarine (size of walnut), and an unbaked pie crust, pour into the raw crust and bake at 300° for 40 minutes or until thickened, beat the egg whites and add 3 Tbsp. sugar until stiff, spread over pie, and brown.

ID 747 — Persimmon Pudding Preheat oven to 325°, melt 1/2 stick margarine in a large rectangular pan, mix 2 c. persimmon pulp with 2 c. sugar or less, 2 eggs, 1 c. milk or cream, 1 1/2 to 2 c. flour, 2 tsp. cinnamon, a pinch of cloves, a pinch of salt, 1 tsp. soda, and 1 tsp. baking powder, add the melted margarine, pour batter into the pan, and bake 1 hour at 325°.

ID 748 — Pie Crust Mix dry ingredients (4 c. flour, 1 Tbsp. sugar, and 1/2 tsp. salt), cut in 1 3/4 c. Crisco, then mix in 1 egg, 1 Tbsp. vinegar, and 1/2 c. ice water (makes 2 double crusts).

ID 749 — Cajun Crawfish Cornbread Combine 2 c. cornmeal with 1 tsp. salt and 1 tsp. baking powder, beat 6 eggs, chop 2 medium onions and 1/2 c. jalapeno peppers, grate 16 oz. Cheddar cheese, then mix eggs with onions, peppers, cheese, 2/3 c. oil, 2 cans creamed corn, and 2 lb. crawfish tails, combine with the cornmeal mixture, pour into a greased 12 x 14-inch baking dish, and bake at 375° for 55 minutes or until golden brown.

ID 750 — Fat-Free Banana Crunch Muffins Preheat oven to 350° about 40 minutes before serving or early in the day, spray 24 mini muffin cups with nonstick cooking spray, mix 1 c. all-purpose flour, 1/2 c. wheat and barley cereal nuggets, 1/2 c. sugar, 1/2 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. baking soda, and 2 medium-size ripe bananas mashed (about 1 c.), then whisk together 1/2 c. plain nonfat yogurt, 1/4 c. thawed frozen no-cholesterol egg substitute, and 1/2 tsp. vanilla extract and stir in the flour mixture just until moistened, spoon into muffin cups, bake 20 minutes or until tops are golden and a toothpick comes out clean, remove to wire racks, and serve warm or cool (makes 24 muffins, each muffin contains 55 calories, 0 g fat, 0 mg cholesterol and 65 mg sodium, calories from fat 0%).

ID 751 — Chili Con Carne Brown 2 yellow onions with 3 lb. ground beef and drain, add 2 cans tomato sauce, 2 to 3 c. water, 3 cans kidney beans, 5 Tbsp. chili powder, 1 pkg. chili seasoning, and salt, Tabasco and red pepper to taste, then simmer and serve when ready (it’s even better the second day).

ID 752 — Spaghetti Casserole Brown 1 lb. hamburger with 1 onion and 1 green pepper and drain, mix with 1 small pkg. spaghetti, 2 cans tomato sauce, 1 small jar Ragu sauce (no meat), and 1 can cream of mushroom soup in a 9 x 13-inch dish, sprinkle top with grated Cheddar cheese, and bake at 350° for 30 minutes.

ID 753 — Cold Bread Pudding Soak one mixing bowl of cold biscuits (crumbled) in sweet milk (for soaking), add 1 Tbsp. butter cut into pieces plus 2 cups sugar and 4 eggs beaten, spray your pan with Pam, pour in the mixture, and bake at 375° until done, about 1 hour.

ID 754 — Persimmon Cake Heat oven to 350°, mix 3 c. persimmons cut in chunks with 2 tsp. baking soda and set aside, mix 1/2 c. butter or margarine with 1 2/3 c. sugar plus 2 tsp. vanilla and 1 tsp. lemon juice and set aside, mix 2 c. flour with 1 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. nutmeg, and 1 tsp. cloves and set aside, blend butter mixture with flour mixture then add persimmon mixture, stir in 1/2 c. raisins and 1/2 c. chopped nuts, pour into 1 large loaf pan or 2 small loaf pans, and bake at 350° for 50 minutes (large loaf) or 30 minutes (small loaves).

ID 755 — Graham Cracker Cake Mix 2 c. sugar with 5 eggs and 2 sticks margarine, add 1 lb. box graham crackers crushed, then add 1 can coconut, 1 c. pecans, 1 bottle maraschino cherries chopped, and 1 Tbsp. vanilla; dissolve 2 Tbsp. baking powder in 1/4 c. milk and pour into batter, then bake at 350° for 1 hour.

ID 756 — No Bake Cookies Put 1 stick oleo, 1/3 c. cocoa, 2 c. sugar, and 1/2 c. milk in a saucepan, bring to a boil and boil 1 minute, remove from heat and stir in 3 c. oatmeal, 1/2 c. peanut butter, and 1 tsp. vanilla, then drop by spoonfuls onto waxed paper and chill.

ID 757 — Butterscotch Squares (Servings: 4) Cream 1 lb. margarine or butter with 2 lb. 8 oz. brown sugar on medium speed for 5 minutes, add 10 eggs (1 lb.) one at a time plus 1 Tbsp. vanilla, mix on low until blended, combine 1 lb. 8 oz. flour (all-purpose) with 2 Tbsp. baking powder and 1 tsp. salt, add to creamed mixture and mix on low until blended, add 12 oz. nuts chopped if using and mix to blend, spread evenly in 2 greased 12 x 18 x 2-inch baking pans, bake at 325° for 25 minutes, cut 5 x 6-inch, yield 60 portions.

ID 758 — Sausage And Egg Quiche Brown 1 lb. sausage and drain off fat, beat 8 eggs and mix in 2 c. shredded Cheddar cheese, 2 c. Mozzarella cheese, and salt and pepper, stir in the sausage, pour into 2 pie shells, and bake 30 minutes at 350°.

ID 759 — Date Nut Balls Cook 1 1/2 sticks butter (not oleo or margarine) with 8 oz. chopped dates and 1 c. sugar until very thick, stir in 1 c. chopped pecans, 2 c. Rice Krispies, and 1 tsp. vanilla, cool until lukewarm, roll into balls, then roll in sifted confectioners sugar.

ID 760 — Broccoli Cheese Soup Sauté 1 1/2 c. chopped onion in 1/2 c. butter or margarine, add 3/4 c. all-purpose flour and stir into a paste, gradually add 1 (10 1/2 oz.) can condensed chicken broth (undiluted) and 1 qt. milk, cook until thickened about 8 to 10 minutes, add 2 c. sliced carrots parboiled, 1 c. sliced celery parboiled, and 2 c. broccoli florets parboiled and heat through, then add 1/2 lb. process American cheese cut into cubes and heat until cheese is melted and vegetables are tender (yield 6 to 8 servings, about 2 quarts).

ID 761 — Sausages And Seashells Prick 8 Italian sweet sausages with a fork, cover with cold water, bring to a boil, simmer uncovered about 10 minutes, drain and dry, slice into rounds, heat 3 Tbsp. olive oil or margarine in a skillet and add sausage with 1 medium onion finely chopped, 1 garlic clove minced, and 2 Tbsp. chopped parsley, cook stirring often until golden brown, add 1 large can tomatoes chopped and 1 (8 oz.) can tomato sauce, simmer covered while you cook 1 lb. small seashells pasta, drain pasta and mix with sausage and sauce.

ID 762 — Barbara Mandrell’s Four Layer Dessert Combine 1 c. flour with 1 c. chopped nuts and 1/2 c. melted margarine, press into the bottom of an 11 3/4 x 7 1/2-inch baking dish, bake at 350° for 15 minutes and cool, mix 1 (8 oz.) pkg. cream cheese softened with 1 c. sifted powdered sugar until blended and fold in 1 c. whipped topping, spread over the crust and chill, prepare 1 small pkg. instant chocolate pudding with part of the 4 c. milk divided as directed and spread over the cream cheese layer, prepare 1 small pkg. instant vanilla pudding with the remaining milk as directed and spread over the chocolate layer, then cut into squares and garnish with whipped topping and chopped nuts.

ID 763 — Zucchini Bread Beat 3 eggs then add 1 c. oil, 2 c. sugar, and 3 tsp. vanilla and mix well, stir in 1 (16 oz.) crushed pineapple, sift together 3 c. flour, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. allspice, 1/2 tsp. baking powder, and 2 tsp. cinnamon, stir in 2 1/2 c. grated zucchini, mix well, pour into loaf pans, and bake at 325° for 1 hour and 45 minutes.

ID 764 — Corn Crepes In a blender combine 2 eggs, 2 egg yolks, 2 c. milk, 1 c. flour, 1/2 c. finely ground cornmeal, 1 tsp. sugar, a dash of salt, and 2 Tbsp. butter and blend until smooth, refrigerate at least 1 hour, whisk batter, heat a 9-inch nonstick pan over medium-high heat and rub lightly with butter, pour about 1/4 cup batter into the center and tilt to coat the bottom, cook about 1 minute until the top looks dry, flip and cook briefly, then repeat with remaining batter (makes 12 crepes; leftovers keep wrapped in the fridge 2 days).

ID 765 — Spaghetti Salad Cook 1 lb. cooked spaghetti and let cool, dice together 1 green pepper, 1 diced onion, 1 diced cucumber, 3 stalks diced celery, and 3 tomatoes diced, then toss spaghetti with the vegetables, 1/3 bottle salad seasonings, and low calorie Italian dressing, and if making for the next day wait and add the tomatoes that day.

ID 766 — Ham Balls Combine 1 lb. grated ham with 8 oz. sharp Cheddar cheese softened and 3 c. Bisquick, roll into balls, and bake 10 minutes.

ID 767 — Low Cholesterol Ice Cream Beat 1 box Egg Scramblers (2 eggs) in a large bowl, mix in 1 (13 oz.) skim evaporated milk, 2 c. sugar, and 1 Tbsp. vanilla until the sugar dissolves, pour into the freezer and add enough 2% skim milk to fill a 1 gallon freezer, then freeze and enjoy (optional additions: 3 bananas, 1 pint strawberries, or 6 peaches).

ID 768 — Glop Slice 3 to 5 potatoes thin and 1 small onion and place in the bottom of a pan, drain and add 1 can green beans on top, add 1 lb. hamburger cooked and drained as the next layer, pour 1 can celery soup over the hamburger, place 1 can biscuits on top, spread 1 can cheese soup over the biscuits, and bake at 350° for 1 hour.

ID 769 — Spanakopeta (Spinach Squares) Sauté 2 bunches green onion finely chopped and 1 onion finely chopped in 1/4 lb. butter until soft, add 2 pkg. frozen chopped spinach thawed and drained and sauté a few minutes longer then cool, mix in 1/2 lb. cream cheese softened, 1/2 lb. Feta cheese crumbled, 8 eggs, 1 tsp. salt, and pepper to taste, layer 10 sheets of 1 lb. phyllo pastry in a 12 x 16 x 2-inch pan brushing each with melted butter or margarine, spread the spinach mixture, top with another 10 sheets brushing each with melted butter, bake at 350° for 30 minutes, and cut into squares before serving (you can brush with a slightly beaten egg before baking for extra luster).

ID 770 — Hot And Spicy Chicken Combine 3 chicken breasts skinned cooked and chopped with 10 oz. frozen corn, 1/2 c. chicken broth, 1/2 c. diced celery, and 1/2 c. onion (thin wedges), bring to a boil, reduce heat and simmer uncovered 15 minutes, stir in 1/2 c. taco salsa, mix 2 tablespoons water into 4 tsp. cornstarch and add to the chicken mixture, cook and stir until it bubbles then cook 2 minutes more, prepare 1 (8 1/2 oz.) pkg. cornbread mix according to package, pour chicken mixture into a 10 x 6 x 2-inch dish, sprinkle with 1 1/2 c. shredded Cheddar cheese and 2 (4 oz.) cans diced jalapeno peppers drained, spoon cornbread on top, and bake 20 minutes at 425°.

ID 771 — Oven Swiss Steak Shake 1 tablespoon flour in a large size oven cooking bag, add 1 1/2 lb. round (or sirloin) steak cut in pieces, 16 oz. can Italian seasoned tomatoes, 1 envelope Lipton onion soup mix (dry), salt and pepper to taste, and 1/4 c. water, squeeze to mix, tie the bag and place in a 9 x 13-inch pan, slit the bag with 6 (1/2") cuts to vent, bake at 325° for approximately 2 hours, then slit open and put back in pan to serve.

ID 772 — Monster Cookies Mix 12 eggs beaten with 2 lb. brown sugar, 4 c. white sugar, 1 Tbsp. vanilla, 8 tsp. soda, 18 c. oatmeal, 1 lb. chocolate chips, 1 lb. M&M candies, 1 Tbsp. syrup, and 3 lb. peanut butter (makes lots of cookies!!!).

ID 773 — Garlic Cheese Ball Let 1 (8 oz.) pkg. Philadelphia cream cheese and 1 small jar Kraft garlic cheese spread soften to room temperature, blend both cheeses until thoroughly mixed, shape into one big ball, chill, roll in 1/2 c. crushed pecans, and serve with any type crackers.

ID 774 — Seven Layer Salad Layer 1 head lettuce chopped, 1/2 c. chopped celery, 1/2 c. chopped green pepper, and 1 pkg. frozen green peas (10 oz.) cooked and drained, spread 1 c. mayonnaise over the top, sprinkle with 2 Tbsp. sugar, add 8 oz. Cheddar cheese shredded, seal and refrigerate overnight, then the next day mix and optionally add cooked bacon (approximately 8 slices, chopped).

ID 775 — Judy’s Vegetable Tortellini Sauté 1 bag frozen chopped onions with 1/2 tsp. minced garlic in 2 Tbsp. butter and 2 Tbsp. oil until transparent, add 1 lb. pkg. creamed spinach softened and 1 pt. heavy cream and simmer, stir in 1/2 c. Parmesan cheese and 1/2 c. Romano cheese then shut heat off, cook 1 lb. box dry tortellini according to package directions, then combine everything when the tortellini are tender and serve hot.

ID 776 — Beef Tips With Rice Mix 1 lb. stew meat with 1 pkg. Lipton onion soup mix and 2 cans cream of mushroom soup in a glass baking dish, cover and bake at 325° until tender, and serve over cooked rice.

ID 777 — Pumpkin Bread Sift 3 1/2 c. flour and resift with 2 tsp. baking soda, 1 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. cloves, and 1 tsp. nutmeg, beat 4 eggs beaten well and add 3 c. sugar gradually, add 1 (15 oz.) can pumpkin, then on low speed add 1 c. oil, 2/3 c. water, 1 tsp. vanilla, and the dry ingredients, mix well, pour into 2 greased and floured loaf pans (5 1/2 x 9 1/2 x 2 1/2-inch), and bake at 325° for 1 hour.

ID 778 — Squash Casserole Cook 2 lb. small yellow squash sliced with 1 large onion chopped and 1/4 c. pimento chopped, drain well, stir in 1 c. sour cream, 1 (10 3/4 oz.) can mushroom soup, and 1 (7 oz.) can water chestnuts sliced, spread in the bottom of a greased 3-quart casserole dish along with 1/2 the 1 lb. pkg. Pepperidge Farm stuffing mix and 1/2 stick margarine, add the squash mixture, top with the remaining stuffing mix and 1 (3 oz.) pkg. sliced almonds, dot with the remaining 1/2 stick margarine, and bake at 350° for 30 minutes.

ID 779 — Bonnie’s Lemon Jello Cake Mix 1 pkg. yellow cake mix with 1 pkg. (3 oz.) lemon jello and 3/4 c. water, add 4 eggs and 3/4 c. oil and beat 2 minutes, bake at 350° for 40 minutes in a 9 x 13-inch pan, and when the cake is done punch holes all over with a large fork.

ID 780 — Hash Brown Casserole Mix 1 (2 lb.) pkg. hash browns (frozen) with salt and pepper to taste, 1 stick margarine melted, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 (8 oz.) sour cream, 1/2 c. onion chopped, and 1 (8 oz.) Cheddar cheese grated, pour into a 9 x 12-inch pan, and bake at 350° for 1 hour (serves 8 to 10).

ID 781 — Broccoli Casserole Melt 1 stick margarine with 1 small jar Cheez Whiz and 1 can cream of celery soup until creamy, stir in 1 1/3 c. Minute rice (uncooked), 1/2 c. onion chopped, and 1 pkg. frozen chopped broccoli, pour into an ungreased 13 x 9-inch pan, and bake at 350° for 35 to 40 minutes.

ID 782 — Sausage Casserole (Microwave) In a 10-inch microwave cooker cook 1 lb. pork sausage with 3/4 c. diced onion and 3/4 c. diced green pepper for 6 minutes stirring once, drain off fat, stir in 1 (1 lb. 13 oz.) can whole tomatoes, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 1 Tbsp. chili powder, 1 tsp. salt, and 8 oz. macaroni cooked, cook 6 minutes, stir in 1 c. dairy sour cream, and heat 1 to 2 minutes.

ID 783 — Chewy Oatmeal Cookies Heat oven to 375°, lightly grease a baking sheet with butter flavor Crisco, beat 3/4 c. butter flavor Crisco shortening with 1 1/4 c. firmly packed light brown sugar, 1 egg, 1/3 c. milk, and 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla flavor, combine 1 c. all-purpose flour with 3 c. Quaker oats (quick or old fashioned, uncooked), 1/2 tsp. baking soda, 1/2 tsp. salt (optional), and 1/4 tsp. cinnamon, mix dry ingredients into the creamed mixture on low speed until blended, stir in 1 c. raisins and 1 c. coarsely chopped walnuts, drop rounded tablespoonfuls of dough 2 inches apart, bake 10 to 15 minutes until lightly brown, cool, and serve.

ID 784 — Flavorful Fish Arrange 1 (4 oz.) fish fillet in a shallow plate, pour 1 Tbsp. lemon juice over it and sprinkle with 1/8 tsp. garlic powder and 1/4 tsp. paprika, top with 1 Tbsp. chopped parsley, cover with plastic wrap, and microwave for 2 minutes.

ID 785 — Beef And Shell Bake Cook 1/2 pkg. Creamette shells as directed and drain, brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1 1/2 c. celery diced and 1 c. onion chopped and drain excess fat, add 1 (28 oz.) can whole tomatoes with liquid (break up with a spoon), 1 (6 oz.) can tomato paste, 2 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. oregano, and 1/4 tsp. pepper and simmer 5 minutes, combine with the shells, pour into a 3-quart casserole, top with 1 c. American cheese grated, and bake at 350° for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 786 — Boiled Dressing Beat 2 eggs, add 1 Tbsp. flour, 1 c. sugar, 1/2 c. vinegar, 1/2 c. water, a pinch of salt, and cook on low heat until thick, then when almost done add 2 Tbsp. butter (you can add dry mustard or celery seed).

ID 787 — Easy Chicken ’N Dumplings Heat 1 qt. chicken broth (with some chicken) and thicken it like thin gravy, mix 2 c. flour with 2 tsp. baking powder and 1 tsp. salt, add milk until the dough is like drop biscuits, drop spoonfuls onto the boiling broth, cover with a lid, and cook about 10 to 15 minutes.

ID 788 — Kidney Bean Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1 1/2 medium onion chopped in 2 Tbsp. vegetable oil, add 1 can tomato soup and simmer 15 minutes, stir in 4 oz. elbow macaroni cooked, 1 can kidney beans, 1 tsp. salt, 1/8 tsp. pepper, and 1 tsp. chili powder, pour into a casserole dish, top with 1/2 c. grated cheese, and bake at 375° for 20 minutes.

ID 789 — Apple Salad Mix 2 eggs beaten with 1 1/2 Tbsp. cornstarch, 1 small can crushed pineapple (do not drain), 1 c. sugar, and 1/4 stick butter or margarine, cook until thick (approximately 7 minutes in the microwave), pour over 6 medium-size apples cubed and 1 cup of marshmallows, let cool, and add nuts or raisins if desired.

ID 790 — Tomato Aspic Soften 2 pkg. Knox gelatine in 1/2 c. cold tomato juice, then add 2 1/2 c. hot tomato juice, 1 Tbsp. lemon juice, 1 tsp. Tabasco sauce, 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/4 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. sugar, 1/4 c. olives, and 1 c. celery and mix together.

ID 791 — Texas Prize Cake Grease and flour the bottom of a 10-inch tube pan, cream 4 sticks butter with 2 2/3 c. sugar, add 9 eggs one at a time beating after each, sift 3 c. flour and add to the creamed mixture, add 1 Tbsp. flavoring (vanilla or lemon), pour into the pan, bake at 325° for 1 hour or until done, and cool in pan 5 minutes.

ID 792 — Springerle Beat 4 eggs until light, add 2 c. sugar and beat until very stiff and light (about 15 minutes at high speed), add 1 tsp. almond extract, 4 c. flour, and 3/4 tsp. baking soda and mix thoroughly, roll out on a lightly floured surface to 1/2 to 1/4-inch thickness, roll with a springerle rolling pin to 1/4-inch thickness pressing only once for a clear imprint, then cut along dividing lines to separate cookies.

ID 793 — Taco Beans Cook 2 lb. pinto beans, brown 2 lb. ground meat, add 2 cans taco sauce, 1 can roasted green chilies, 1 (No. 2) can tomatoes, 1 tsp. chili powder, 1/2 c. chopped bell pepper, 1/2 tsp. cumin, 2 large onions, and 4 garlic buds and simmer 10 minutes, then add the meat mixture to the beans and simmer 1 hour.

ID 794 — Battered Fried Fish Cut 1 (1 lb.) haddock into serving-size pieces and sprinkle lightly with salt, mix 1 egg with 1 1/4 c. evaporated milk, 1 c. flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, and 1/4 c. cornmeal plus 1/4 teaspoon salt, dip the haddock pieces into the batter, and fry in deep fat at 375° for 5 minutes or until brown.

ID 795 — Vanilla Pudding Scald 2 c. milk, mix 3/4 c. sugar with 5 round Tbsp. flour and a dash of salt, stir into the scalded milk in a heavy pan or double boiler and stir constantly until thick, add 2 eggs slightly beaten and cook 2 minutes more, remove from heat and stir in 1 Tbsp. butter or margarine and 1 tsp. vanilla until smooth.

ID 796 — Blueberry Heaven Supreme Mix 1 (14 oz.) can Eagle Brand milk with 1/2 c. lemon juice until thickened, fold in 1 (21 oz.) can blueberry pie filling and 1 (8 1/4 oz.) can crushed pineapple drained, fold in 1 (8 oz.) container Cool Whip, pour into 2 graham cracker crusts, garnish with graham cracker crumbs and/or miniature marshmallows, and chill in the refrigerator 3 to 4 hours or overnight.

ID 797 — Kraut Salad Toss together 1 (No. 2 1/2) can kraut, 1 c. chopped celery, 1 c. chopped onion, 1 c. chopped green pepper, 1 (4 oz.) jar chopped pimento, 1 c. sugar, 1 c. salad oil, and 1/2 c. white vinegar, cover, and marinate in the refrigerator 24 hours.

ID 798 — Peach Pie Mix 1 pt. sour cream with 1/4 c. sugar and 1/4 tsp. vanilla until smooth, fold in 1 large can sliced peaches drained and diced, pour into 1 graham cracker crust, bake at 325° for 25 minutes, cool completely, and refrigerate.

ID 799 — Dirt Cups You will also need 8 to 10 (7 oz.) clear plastic cups, then mix 2 c. cold milk with 1 (4 serving size) pkg. chocolate instant pudding, fold in 1 (8 oz.) tub whipped topping, layer with 1 (16 oz.) pkg. chocolate sandwich cookies crushed, and decorate with gummy worms and frogs and candy flowers.

ID 800 — Finger Jello Mix 4 boxes of small jello with 4 pkg. gelatin, add 5 c. boiling water, dissolve completely, and let set in the refrigerator.

ID 801 — Broccoli and Rice Casserole Cook 1 c. rice and cook 1 pkg. chopped broccoli; sauté 1 chopped onion, then add 1 small jar pimentos, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 small can milk, and 1 small jar Cheez Whiz. Mix everything with the cooked rice and broccoli, pour into a casserole, bake at 350°F for 10 minutes, top with grated cheese, and bake until the cheese is melted.

ID 802 — California Cookies Mix 1/2 cup butter or margarine, 1 cup flour, 2 Tbsp. sugar, 1 1/2 cups brown sugar, 1/2 cup coconut, 1 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. baking soda, 1 cup chopped pecans, 2 eggs, 2 Tbsp. flour, and 1 Tbsp. vanilla; once the pan has cooled, top with a mixture of 1 1/2 cups powdered sugar, 2 Tbsp. lemon juice, and a few drops of green food coloring mixed well.

ID 803 — Baked Corn Melt 2 Tbsp. Crisco, add 1 1/2 Tbsp. flour and mix well, then gradually add 1 c. milk and bring to a boil while stirring. Add 2 c. cooked or canned corn, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1/8 tsp. pepper, heat thoroughly, remove from heat, stir in 2 well-beaten eggs, pour into a greased baking dish, and bake at 350°F for 25 minutes or until firm.

ID 804 — Sour Cream Pound Cake Cream together 2 3/4 c. sugar and 1 c. butter until light and fluffy, add 6 eggs one at a time beating well, sift together 3 c. sifted plain flour, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. soda, add alternately with 1 c. sour cream, beat well, add 1/2 tsp. vanilla extract, 1/2 tsp. lemon extract, and 1/2 tsp. orange extract, pour into a greased and floured 10-inch tube pan, and bake at 350°F for 1 1/2 hours.

ID 805 — Corned Beef Hash Casserole Layer 3 to 4 sliced potatoes and 1 sliced onion in a baking dish, dot with butter or oleo, season with salt and pepper, cover with 1 can corned beef hash, add 1 can creamed corn, top with 1 1/2 c. bread crumbs, cover and bake at 350°F for 10 minutes, then uncover and bake 25 minutes more.

ID 806 — Lemon Meringue Pie Blend 1 c. sugar, 1/4 tsp. salt, 1/4 c. flour, and 2 Tbsp. cornstarch, stir in 1 1/2 c. water, cook over low heat stirring until thickened, stir some of the hot mixture into 2 beaten egg yolks, combine and cook one minute more, add 1/2 c. lemon juice, grated rind of 1 lemon, and 1 Tbsp. butter or margarine, pour into a baked pastry shell, top with meringue, and brown at 325°F for 14 to 20 minutes.

ID 807 — Vegetable Spread Grind or grate 3 small carrots, 1 small onion, and 1 small cucumber, drain well, mix 1 large cream cheese with 3 Tbsp. mayonnaise until smooth, add vegetables, season with salt and red pepper, spread on crackers, and top with olives or pimentos.

ID 808 — Party Mix Mix together 1 bottle Orville Redenbacher’s buttery flavored popcorn oil and 1 pkg. Ranch dressing mix, then combine cereal (Chex or Crispix), nuts, pretzels, and crackers in a large bowl, pour oil mixture over to coat, and let set for 6 hours, tossing every couple of hours.

ID 809 — Dick’s Grilled Boneless Leg of Lamb Purée 1 medium onion, 3 cloves garlic, a piece of fresh ginger, and 1/2 seeded jalapeño, mix with 1/4 c. shoyu, 1/4 c. honey, and 2 Tbsp. peanut or cottonseed oil, spread marinade over 1 butterflied leg of lamb, refrigerate overnight, and turn several times.

ID 810 — Meat Loaf Combine 2 lb. ground beef, 1/2 lb. ground pork, 1 c. tomato juice, 3/4 c. oats, 2 eggs, 1/3 c. catsup, 1 chopped onion, 1 chopped celery stalk, 1/4 chopped green pepper, 1 grated carrot, 1 tsp. basil, 1 tsp. oregano, 1/4 tsp. paprika, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. pepper, 1 tsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1 Tbsp. parsley flakes, 1/4 tsp. garlic powder, optional 1 can chopped mushrooms, bake in two loaf pans at 400°F for 15 minutes then at 350°F until brown, topping with a glaze of 2 Tbsp. brown sugar, 1/4 c. ketchup, and 1 tsp. mustard if desired.

ID 811 — Life Saver Cookies Mix 3/4 c. butter, 1 c. sugar, 2 eggs, and 1/2 tsp. lemon extract, blend in 2 1/2 c. flour, 1 tsp. baking powder, and 1/2 tsp. salt, chill 1 hour, roll dough 1/8-inch thick, cut shapes, cut a hole in the center, place on foil-lined sheet, add a Life Saver candy, and bake at 375°F for 7 to 9 minutes; yields 6 dozen.

ID 812 — Banana Chiffon Cake Sift 2 1/4 c. cake flour, 1 c. sugar, 3 tsp. baking powder, 1 tsp. cinnamon, and 1/2 tsp. salt, add 1/2 c. oil, 5 egg yolks, 2 Tbsp. lemon juice, and 2 to 3 mashed bananas, beat smooth, fold in 7 to 8 beaten egg whites with 1/2 tsp. cream of tartar, and bake at 325°F for 1 hour and 10 minutes.

ID 813 — Baked Zesty Italian Chicken Season 4 to 5 boneless skinless chicken breasts with 1 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. pepper, and 1 tsp. garlic, pour 1 bottle Zesty Italian dressing over, top with 1 can Italian bread crumbs, and bake at 375°F for 20 to 25 minutes.

ID 814 — Oatmeal Cake Mix 1 c. oats with 1 1/2 c. boiling water and let sit, cream 1 c. brown sugar, 1 c. white sugar, 1 stick margarine, and 2 eggs, add oatmeal, then mix in 1 1/3 c. flour, 1 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. soda, and 1/2 tsp. salt, pour into a greased 9 x 13 pan, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 815 — Fried Apple Pies Simmer 4 c. peeled sliced apples with 4 c. water until tender, mash and add 1/2 c. sugar and 4 tsp. cinnamon, chill, combine 6 c. flour, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 Tbsp. baking powder, cut in 1 1/2 c. vegetable shortening, add 1 c. milk to form dough, chill 1 hour, roll out, fill with apples, seal, and fry in 2 c. vegetable oil at 370°F until brown.

ID 816 — Carrot Coins (Microwave) Mix 1 lb. sliced carrots, 3 Tbsp. water, 2 Tbsp. parsley, 1 Tbsp. butter or oleo, 1/4 tsp. ground ginger, 1/4 tsp. dried tarragon, 1/8 tsp. garlic salt, and 1/8 tsp. pepper in a casserole, cover, microwave on High 6 to 8 minutes stirring twice, and let stand 3 minutes.

ID 817 — Spiced Fruit Salad Heat reserved pineapple juice from 1/2 c. canned pineapple with 1 cinnamon stick, reduce heat and cook 5 minutes, remove cinnamon, add 1/2 tsp. rum extract, pour over a mixture of 3/4 c. sliced strawberries, 1/2 c. canned peaches, 1/2 c. cantaloupe balls, and pineapple, then refrigerate.

ID 818 — Orange-Pineapple Salad Fold together 2 c. mini marshmallows, 1 c. sour cream, 1 drained large can mandarin oranges, and 1 c. drained pineapple chunks, then refrigerate 8 to 12 hours.

ID 819 — Coconut Pecan Frosting Cook 1 c. evaporated milk, 1 c. sugar, 3 egg yolks, 1/2 c. butter, and 1 tsp. vanilla over medium heat until thick, add 1 1/3 c. coconut and 1 c. chopped pecans, cool until spreadable, making about 2 1/4 cups.

ID 820 — Haystacks Melt 1 Tbsp. peanut butter with 1 (6 oz.) pkg. butterscotch morsels, stir in 1 (3 oz.) can chow mein noodles and 1 c. roasted peanuts, drop onto wax paper, and chill until set.

ID 821 — Triple Fudge Cake Cook 1 (3 oz.) pkg. chocolate pudding, blend in 1 cake mix, pour into a greased 9 x 13 pan, sprinkle with 1 (6 oz.) pkg. chocolate chips and chopped nuts, bake at 350°F for 30 to 35 minutes, and serve with whipped cream.

ID 822 — Skillet Barbecue Beans Brown 1/2 lb. pork sausage with 1/2 c. onion and 1/4 c. green pepper, drain, stir in 1 (28 oz.) can pork and beans and 1 envelope barbecue seasoning, and simmer 15 minutes.

ID 823 — Broccoli Casserole Sauté 1/2 c. celery and 1/2 c. onion in 1/2 c. butter, add 1 c. cream of chicken soup and bring to a boil, stir in 1/2 pkg. broccoli, 2 c. cooked rice, and 1 c. grated cheese, and bake at 350°F until bubbly.

ID 824 — Peanut Butter Sticks Freeze 1 loaf bread, cut each slice into 5 strips, bake at 200°F for 1 1/2 hours, melt 1 jar peanut butter with 1/2 c. oil, then coat sticks and roll in a mixture of 1 c. graham cracker crumbs and 1 1/2 c. confectioners sugar.

ID 825 — Cinnamon Pull-Aparts Soften yeast in 1/4 c. lukewarm water, combine shortening, sugar, salt, flour, scalded milk, eggs, yeast, vanilla, and remaining ingredients as listed, then prepare and bake according to the full layered dough and pudding method provided.

ID 826 — Apple Dumplins Place apple slices into 2 cans crescent rolls, roll up, place in a 9 x 13 dish, pour over a mixture of 2 sticks margarine, 1 1/2 c. sugar, and 1 tsp. cinnamon, add 1 (12 oz.) can Mountain Dew, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 827 — Hot Tuna Appetizer Combine 1 can tuna, 12 chopped anchovies, 3/4 c. green pepper, 1/2 c. pimento, 1 chopped hard-cooked egg, 3 chopped green onions, and 2 Tbsp. Russian dressing, spread on sautéed bread slices, top with remaining dressing mixed with 1 1/2 Tbsp. cognac and Worcestershire sauce, and heat until hot.

ID 828 — Low-Fat Texas Trash Mix cereals to make 5 c. with 2 c. pretzel sticks, toss with 1/8 c. apple juice, 4 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/4 tsp. garlic powder, and 1 tsp. onion powder, bake at 275°F for 1 hour stirring every 10 minutes.

ID 829 — Punch Bowl Cake Layer baked yellow cake cubes, prepared vanilla pudding, fruit cocktail, crushed pineapple, cherry pie filling, nuts, coconut, and whipped topping in a punch bowl, repeat layers, garnish with cherries, and chill.

ID 830 — Quick Macaroons Beat 3 to 4 egg whites with 1/4 tsp. cream of tartar until stiff, add 1/2 c. sugar gradually, fold in 1 tsp. lemon juice, 2 tsp. flour, and 1 c. coconut, spoon into lined muffin cups, and bake at 300°F for 30 to 35 minutes.

ID 831 — Seafood Casserole Boil 2 c. water with 1/2 c. white wine, cook 2 lb. shrimp 3 minutes and 1 lb. scallops 6 minutes, reserve liquid, then prepare casserole with remaining ingredients as directed.

ID 832 — Cheese Ball Let 1 lb. mild Cheddar, 1 lb. sharp Cheddar, 1 lb. Velveeta, and 1 lb. cream cheese soften, blend until fluffy, add 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce and 1 chopped onion, chill, shape into balls, and roll in chopped nuts.

ID 833 — Banana Split Cake Mix 2 c. graham cracker crumbs with 1 stick melted oleo, press into pan, beat 2 c. powdered sugar with 2 sticks oleo and 2 eggs for 15 minutes, pour over crust, top with bananas, pineapple, Cool Whip, nuts, and cherries, and refrigerate overnight.

ID 834 — English Muffin Loaf Combine 6 c. flour, 2 pkg. yeast, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 2 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. soda, add warmed milk and water, beat well, spoon into greased pans sprinkled with cornmeal, let rise 45 minutes, and bake at 400°F for 25 minutes.

ID 835 — Sweet Potato Casserole Combine 3 c. mashed sweet potatoes, 1 c. sugar, 1/2 tsp. salt, 2 beaten eggs, 1/2 stick melted margarine, 1/2 c. milk, and 1/2 tsp. vanilla, pour into a casserole, and bake.

ID 836 — Crock-Pot Kielbasa Boil 2 or 3 kielbasa in 3 cans beer for 10 minutes, combine 1 bottle ketchup, 1 jar mustard, 1 tsp. vinegar, and 3/4 c. brown sugar in crock-pot, add sliced kielbasa, and cook on High 2 to 3 hours or Low 3 to 5 hours.

ID 837 — Homemade Chicken Noodle Soup Add garlic, green onions, parsley, onion, 4 bouillon cubes, 1 can chicken broth, and cooked chicken to reserved broth, bring to boil, add 1 pkg. spaghetti noodles, and cook until done.

ID 838 — Church Windows Melt 1/2 c. oleo with 1 large pkg. chocolate chips, cool slightly, add 1 c. nuts and 1 large bag marshmallows, shape into logs, roll in coconut, chill overnight, and slice.

ID 839 — Blueberry Dumplings Simmer 2 1/2 c. blueberries, 1/2 c. sugar, 1 c. water, and lemon juice, drop dumplings made from flour, sugar, butter, and milk into sauce, cover, and simmer 15 minutes.

ID 840 — Heavenly Hash Whip 1 pt. cream, add 1/4 c. sugar and 1 tsp. vanilla, fold in 3 c. marshmallows and 1 can pineapple tidbits, and chill.

ID 841 — Hamburger Potato Hot Dish Layer 6 sliced potatoes, 1 sliced onion, 1 1/2 lb. raw hamburger, pour over 1 can beef vegetable soup and 1/2 can water, and bake at 350°F for 1 to 1 1/2 hours.

ID 842 — Potatoes Romanoff Thaw hash browns, spread in dish, top with cornflakes and margarine, sauté onion in oleo, stir in soups, milk, sour cream, salt, and pepper, pour over potatoes, and bake 50 minutes.

ID 843 — Enchilada Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground chuck with 1 chopped onion, add enchilada sauce and soups, layer with tortillas and cheese in a casserole, microwave until hot, and top with cheese.

ID 837 — Homemade Chicken Noodle Soup After the chicken is cooked, skinned, deboned, and the broth reserved, add 1 box chopped garlic, 2 bunches finely chopped green onions, 1 bunch finely chopped parsley leaves, 1 medium chopped onion, 4 chicken bouillon cubes, and 1 can chicken broth to the broth. Bring to a rolling boil, simmer until the onions are tender, then add 1 pkg. spaghetti noodles and cook until the noodles are done; this makes a large pot serving about 10.

ID 838 — Church Windows Melt 1/2 c. oleo with 1 large package chocolate chips in a saucepan, allow to cool slightly, then stir in 1 c. chopped nuts and 1 large bag miniature colored marshmallows. Shape into 3 logs, spread coconut on wax paper, roll logs in coconut to coat, wrap in wax paper, refrigerate overnight, and slice thin.

ID 839 — Blueberry Dumplings In a Dutch oven bring 2 1/2 c. blueberries, 1/2 c. sugar, 1 c. water, and a dash of salt to a boil, cover and simmer 5 minutes, then add 1 Tbsp. lemon juice. Mix 1 c. self-rising flour, 1/4 c. sugar, and 1/4 tsp. salt, cut in 2 Tbsp. butter or margarine, add 1/2 c. milk, stir just to moisten, drop dough by tablespoons into bubbling sauce, cover tightly, simmer 15 minutes without uncovering, and serve hot; serves 6.

ID 840 — Heavenly Hash Whip 1 pt. whipping cream to soft peaks, add 1/4 c. sugar and 1 tsp. vanilla, then fold in 3 c. mini marshmallows and 1 can drained pineapple tidbits (20 oz.), refrigerate, and serve preferably made one day ahead.

ID 841 — Hamburger Potato Hot Dish Place 6 peeled and sliced potatoes into a large pan, layer with 1 sliced onion and 1 1/2 lb. raw hamburger, pour over 1 large can beef vegetable soup mixed with 1/2 can water, and bake at 350°F for 1 to 1 1/2 hours.

ID 842 — Potatoes Romanoff Thaw 1 pkg. frozen hash browns and spread in a 9 x 12-inch baking dish, top with 1/2 c. crushed cornflakes and 1/2 c. margarine. Sauté 1 small onion in 2 Tbsp. oleo, stir in 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can Cheddar cheese soup, 1 (13 oz.) can evaporated milk, 1 c. sour cream, 1/2 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. pepper, pour over potatoes, and bake for 50 minutes.

ID 843 — Enchilada Casserole Brown 1 lb. ground chuck with 1 chopped onion in the microwave on High for 4 minutes, drain if needed, stir to crumble, add 1 can enchilada sauce, 1 can cream of mushroom soup, and 1 can cream of chicken soup. In a 3-quart casserole layer flour tortillas, meat mixture, and about 6 oz. grated cheese, repeat layers except cheese, microwave on Medium about 20 minutes, then top with remaining cheese and let stand until melted.

ID 844 — Recipe for a Happy Family Mix 1 husband, 1 wife, children with 1 Bible for each, 1 home, generous portions of prayer, 3 c. love firmly packed, 1 pkg. work, 1 pkg. playing together, 1 portion patience, 1 portion understanding, 1 small paddle, and 1 c. kisses moderately, sprinkle with awareness, bake in the moderate oven of everyday life, cool, turn out onto a platter of cheerfulness, garnish with tears and laughter, and serve God, country, and community.

ID 845 — Country Casserole Heat 1 lb. Velveeta cheese with 1 c. milk and 1/2 c. Miracle Whip over low heat until smooth, add 2 c. chopped cooked turkey or chicken, 1 (10 oz.) pkg. cooked and drained peas and carrots, 5 oz. cooked and drained spaghetti, and 1 Tbsp. chopped chives or minced onions, mix well, pour into a 2-quart casserole, and bake at 350°F for 35 to 40 minutes; serves 8.

ID 846 — Party Pizza Appetizers Combine 1 lb. cooked and crumbled hot sausage, 1 c. chopped onion, 1/2 c. grated sharp cheese, 1/2 c. grated Parmesan cheese, 1 1/2 tsp. oregano, 1 tsp. garlic salt, 1 (8 oz.) can tomato sauce, and 1 (6 oz.) can tomato paste. Separate 3 cans flaky biscuits into thirds, spread with mixture, freeze or bake immediately at 425°F for 10 minutes; makes about 90.

ID 847 — Strawberry Bread Preheat oven to 350°F, combine 2 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 1 tsp. baking soda, and 1 tsp. cinnamon, add 4 beaten eggs, 1 1/4 c. vegetable oil, and 2 pkg. (10 oz.) thawed and chopped frozen strawberries, stir well, pour into two greased and floured loaf pans, bake 1 hour, and cool 10 minutes in pans.

ID 848 — Red Lobster Cheese Garlic Biscuits Preheat oven to 450°F, mix 2 c. Bisquick, 2/3 c. milk, and 1/2 c. shredded cheddar cheese until soft dough forms, beat vigorously 30 seconds, drop by spoonfuls onto ungreased baking sheet, bake 8 to 10 minutes until golden, mix 1/2 c. melted butter with 1/4 tsp. garlic powder, brush over hot biscuits, and serve warm.

ID 849 — Date Rolled Cookies Mix flour and soda, roll half the dough on a floured board to 1/2-inch thickness, spread filling over top, sprinkle with chopped nuts if desired, roll like a jelly roll and refrigerate until firm, slice and bake 10 to 12 minutes at 350°F or 10 minutes at 375°F, optionally topping with sugar and a walnut half.

ID 850 — Pineapple Mold Spray a 1 1/2-quart ring mold, dissolve 1 small pkg. lemon Jello and 1 pkg. lime Jello in 2 c. boiling water, cool slightly, stir in 10 oz. cottage cheese, 1 can crushed pineapple, 2/3 c. walnuts, 1 c. cream, 1 c. mayonnaise, and 1 to 3 Tbsp. horseradish to taste, then chill until set.

ID 851 — Play Doh Mix 1 1/2 c. all-purpose flour, 1/2 c. salt, and 1 Tbsp. alum, slowly whisk in 1 c. hot water, 1 Tbsp. cooking oil, and food coloring, cook over medium-high heat stirring constantly until thick, then knead until smooth.

ID 852 — Layered Salad Layer 1/2 head shredded lettuce, 1 box frozen peas, 4 chopped hard-boiled eggs, 1/2 lb. cooked and crumbled bacon, 1 can sliced water chestnuts, and another 1/2 head shredded lettuce in a 9 x 13-inch pan. Mix 1 pkg. Ranch dressing, 1 c. mayonnaise, and 1 c. sour cream, spread on top, sprinkle with shredded Cheddar cheese, cover, and refrigerate, preferably overnight.

ID 853 — Sour Cream Potatoes Mix 2 lb. thawed frozen hash browns, 1 pt. sour cream, 2 c. or 10 oz. grated Cheddar cheese, 2 cans cream of chicken soup, 1/2 c. melted butter, 1 tsp. salt, 1/4 tsp. pepper, and 1/2 c. chopped onion, pour into a 13 x 9-inch pan, top with 1/4 c. melted butter mixed with 2 c. crushed cornflakes, and bake at 350°F for 45 minutes.

ID 854 — Creamy Banana Pudding In a large bowl combine 1 (14 oz.) can condensed milk and 1 1/2 c. cold water, add 1 pkg. instant vanilla pudding and beat until blended, fold in 2 c. whipped whipping cream, layer with 36 vanilla wafers and 3 sliced bananas in a 2 1/2-quart bowl, repeat layers ending with pudding, and chill thoroughly.

ID 855 — Hush Puppies Combine 1 1/2 c. corn meal, 1/2 c. flour, and 1/2 tsp. baking soda, stir in 3/4 c. buttermilk and beat smooth, add 2 tsp. salt and 1 finely chopped onion, drop heaping tablespoonfuls into hot oil, fry until golden, and drain on paper towels.

ID 856 — Ground Beef Casserole Brown 3 lb. ground beef, cook 1 small onion, 1 clove garlic, 1 c. bell pepper, and 1/2 c. celery in fat, add to beef and cook 20 minutes, stir in tomato paste, tomato sauce, mushrooms, creamed corn, olives, and cooked egg noodles, layer with grated sharp cheese, and bake at 350°F for about 30 minutes.

ID 857 — Lemon Fluff Jello Bring pineapple and 1/2 c. sugar to a boil and simmer 15 minutes, cool, dissolve 1 pkg. lemon Jell-O in 1 c. boiling water, mix in softened 8 oz. cream cheese, add pineapple and optional 1/2 c. chopped pecans, chill until thick, fold in 8 oz. Cool Whip, and chill until firm.

ID 858 — Quick Fruit Salad Stir together 1 can cherry pie filling, 1 can chunk pineapple, 2 c. miniature marshmallows, 4 sliced bananas, and 1/2 c. chopped pecans, mix well, and chill; may be served the next day.

ID 859 — Breaded Steak Rolls Roll cube steaks with bread crumbs or bread, parsley flakes, garlic powder, onion powder, Parmesan cheese, tomato sauce, salt, and pepper, secure with wooden toothpicks, and cook as desired.

ID 860 — Dirt Pie In a deep bowl mix 2 pkg. instant French vanilla pudding, 8 oz. cream cheese, and 1/2 c. milk until creamy, add 3/4 c. powdered sugar, then gradually add remaining milk, layer crushed Oreos in a pan, spread pudding mixture over, top with whipped topping, refrigerate, and sprinkle with more Oreos before serving.

ID 861 — Rich Beef and Gravy Mix 1 pkg. onion soup mix, 1/4 c. water, and 1 can cream of mushroom soup in a crock-pot, add 2 to 2 1/2 lb. round steak cut into pieces, cover, cook on Low 6 to 8 hours, and serve over potatoes, noodles, or rice.

ID 862 — Chicken Maranda Place cooked, deboned chicken in a casserole, spread 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can cream of celery soup, and 1 small can Pet milk over chicken and mix well, combine remaining ingredients with 1 pkg. cornbread mix and 1 c. chicken broth, add as topping, and bake at 450°F for 20 minutes until golden.

ID 863 — Apple-Banana Bread Combine 4 beaten eggs, 1 1/2 c. mashed bananas, 1 c. packed brown sugar, 1/2 c. oil, 1/3 c. milk, and 1 tsp. salt, mix dry ingredients separately, combine, fold in 1 chopped apple and 1 c. nuts, pour into pans, and bake at 325°F for about 1 hour.

ID 864 — Mock Lobster Salad Crush 30 soda crackers, mix 1 1/2 c. chopped celery, 1 chopped green pepper, 3 diced hard-boiled eggs, and 1 diced onion, stir together 1 1/2 c. tomato juice and 1 1/2 c. mayonnaise, combine with vegetables and crackers, refrigerate overnight, and serve chilled.

ID 865 — Buttermilk Cake Cream 2 c. sugar and 3/4 c. Crisco, beat in 3 eggs one at a time, sift dry ingredients, alternate adding with 1 c. buttermilk, add 1 Tbsp. almond flavoring and 1 tsp. vanilla, mix well, and bake in a greased Bundt pan at 350°F for 1 hour.

ID 866 — Foolproof Chocolate Fudge Melt 3 (6 oz.) pkg. chocolate morsels with 1 (14 oz.) can condensed milk over low heat, stir in dash of salt and 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, spread into an 8-inch pan, chill until set, and cut into squares.

ID 867 — Sweet and Sour Seashells Pour 2 Tbsp. corn oil, 3/4 c. sugar, 1/2 c. cider vinegar, 1/2 c. wine vinegar, 1/2 c. water, 3 Tbsp. mustard, 1/8 tsp. salt, and 1/8 tsp. pepper over 1 lb. cooked seashell pasta with sliced cucumbers and diced onions, marinate 3 to 4 hours, and serve chilled.

ID 868 — Cornbread Salad Mix 2 pkg. cooked and crumbled cornbread, 1 1/2 c. onion, 1 chopped green pepper, 3 tomatoes, 8 to 10 slices bacon, 1 1/2 c. Velveeta, 1 1/2 c. dressing or mayo, 2 Tbsp. mustard, salt and pepper, let set overnight, and serve.

ID 869 — Ham and Rice Casserole Mix 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1/2 c. milk, 1 1/3 c. precooked rice, and 1 c. diced ham in an 8 x 8-inch pan and bake at 375°F for 25 minutes.

ID 870 — Zucchini Muffins Preheat oven to 400°F, grease muffin cups, mix flour, sugar, pecans, oats, baking powder, salt, and cinnamon, add beaten eggs, oil, and shredded zucchini, stir until moistened, and bake 25 minutes.

ID 871 — Chicken Parmesan Dip 4 chicken breasts in Italian dressing then Progresso bread crumbs, bake at 350°F for 30 minutes, top with Mozzarella for the last 3 to 5 minutes, simmer spaghetti sauce with onion and garlic, cook noodles, and serve together.

ID 872 — Simple Cherry-Pineapple Crisp Spread crushed pineapple in a baking dish, top with cherry pie filling, sprinkle with yellow cake mix, drizzle with melted margarine, and bake at 350°F until golden.

ID 873 — Wacky Cake Mix 3 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 1/2 c. cocoa, 1 tsp. salt, and 2 tsp. baking soda, add 2 Tbsp. vinegar, 1 c. oil, and 2 c. cold water, pour into pan, and bake at 350°F for 35 to 40 minutes.

ID 874 — Cherry Torte Cream 1 c. soft butter with 1 c. sugar, add 2 tsp. vanilla and 4 to 5 egg yolks, then mix in 1/4 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. baking powder, and 3 c. flour. Spread the dough onto a cookie sheet, forming raised edges, cover with cherry pie filling, beat the egg whites until stiff and add 6 Tbsp. sugar, spread over the filling, sprinkle with ground nuts, and bake at 350°F for 25 to 30 minutes.

ID 875 — Red Raspberry Cordial In a 1-gallon jar combine 4 c. raspberries, 4 c. sugar, and 2 c. gin or vodka, stir well, cover tightly, and let stand for 4 months stirring once a week. Strain through cheesecloth, pressing the solids well, return liquid to the jar, and store; makes about 4 cups.

ID 876 — Pavlova (Australia’s National Dessert) Line a baking sheet with wax paper and lightly grease, draw an 8-inch circle, beat 4 egg whites at room temperature until foamy, add 1/4 tsp. salt and 1/4 tsp. cream of tartar and beat until stiff glossy peaks form, gradually beat in 1 c. sugar, shape into the circle, bake, cool completely, then top with 2 c. sweetened whipping cream and 3 c. fruit of your choice.

ID 877 — Chunky Cheddar Chili Beans Brown 1 lb. ground beef with onions, drain, add 1 can kidney beans, 1 lb. can chopped tomatoes, 6 oz. tomato paste, 1 Tbsp. chili powder, 2 tsp. sugar, 1 tsp. salt, and 1/4 tsp. pepper, cover and simmer for 45 minutes, then add cubed Cheddar cheese just before serving.

ID 878 — Lazy Day Chicken Preheat oven to 350°F, place 1 1/4 lb. boneless skinless chicken breasts in a sprayed baking pan, mix 1 can chunky tomato sauce, 2 Tbsp. dried onion flakes, 1 packet instant beef flavored broth mix, and 1/2 c. water, pour over chicken, cover and bake 30 minutes, uncover and bake 30 minutes longer.

ID 879 — Chicken Pot Pie Mix cooked diced chicken with 1 can cream of celery soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 soup can water, and 1 can Veg-All, pour into a 9 x 13-inch baking dish, and bake until heated through.

ID 880 — Frito Salad Drain 1 can Ranch Style beans, then mix with 2 diced tomatoes, 1 chopped head lettuce, 2 c. grated cheese, and 1 bottle Catalina dressing, adding 1 medium bag Fritos just before serving.

ID 881 — Marinated Beef Slices Cut 1/2 lb. cooked rare sirloin or roast beef into julienne strips, add 1 thinly sliced onion, 3/4 tsp. salt, a dash of pepper, sprinkle with 1 1/2 Tbsp. lemon juice, mix in 1 c. dairy sour cream, chill well, and serve with crackers.

ID 882 — Chicken and Stuffing Bake Place 3 c. cut cooked chicken or turkey in a 2-quart casserole, toss 3 1/2 c. herb seasoned croutons with 1 medium chopped onion, 1 chopped celery stalk, 1/3 c. margarine or butter, and 1/2 c. water, reserve 1 1/2 c., spread remaining stuffing over chicken, mix 1 c. condensed cream of chicken soup with 1 1/2 c. water and pour over, top with reserved stuffing, and bake uncovered at 350°F for about 30 minutes.

ID 883 — Turkey Casserole Mix 4 c. turkey with juices, 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 1 can cream of celery soup, 1 can cream of chicken soup, and 1 1/2 c. Minute rice, then bake at 350°F for 40 minutes.

ID 884 — Pancakes Beat 1 egg until fluffy, beat in 1 c. all-purpose flour, 2 Tbsp. oil, 1 c. buttermilk, 1 Tbsp. sugar, 1 tsp. baking powder, 1/2 tsp. baking soda, and 1/2 tsp. salt until smooth, thin with 1/4 c. milk if desired, cook on a griddle until golden brown, making about 9 pancakes.

ID 885 — Easy Jello Salad Mix 8 oz. cottage cheese, 6 oz. Cool Whip, 3 oz. Jell-O, and well-drained fruit of choice, then chill before serving.

ID 886 — Linguine Salad Combine 1 lb. cooked linguine with 1 chopped large tomato, 1 chopped large cucumber, 1 chopped large onion, 1 bottle Italian dressing (16 oz.), and 1/2 jar Salad Supreme, mixing well and adding broccoli if desired.

ID 887 — Hobo Bread (Brown Bread) Combine 2 1/2 c. leftover coffee, 4 tsp. baking soda, 2 c. raisins, 1 c. white sugar, 1 1/2 c. chopped nuts, 4 c. sifted flour, and 1/4 tsp. salt, pour into 3 greased coffee cans, and bake as directed.

ID 888 — Meltaways Mix 8 oz. softened cream cheese, 1 c. softened margarine or butter, and 2 c. flour, wrap and refrigerate overnight, divide dough into quarters, roll each into an 8-inch circle, brush with melted butter, sprinkle filling, cut into 8 triangles, roll up, brush with egg yolk mixed with 2 Tbsp. water, and bake.

ID 889 — Snickerdoodles Cream together 1/2 c. butter, 1/2 c. shortening, 1 1/2 c. sugar, and 2 eggs, blend in 2 3/4 c. flour, 2 tsp. cream of tartar, 1 tsp. soda, and 1/4 tsp. salt, shape into balls, roll in a mixture of 2 Tbsp. sugar and 2 tsp. cinnamon, and bake at 400°F for 8 to 10 minutes.

ID 890 — Sundown Cooler Chill 34 oz. lemon-lime soda and 1 liter dry white wine, then pour over ice with thinly sliced lemon and lime; makes 16 punch cups.

ID 891 — Oreo Dirt Cake Crush 1 1/4 lb. Oreo cookies and layer half in the bottom of a glass bowl, cream 1/4 c. margarine with 1 c. powdered sugar and 8 oz. cream cheese, add 12 oz. Cool Whip, 2 packages instant chocolate pudding, and 3 1/2 c. milk, mix well, pour over cookies, and top with remaining crushed Oreos.

ID 892 — Parmesan Meat Loaf Combine 1 lb. ground beef, 1 c. large curd cottage cheese, 1/2 c. oatmeal, 1 beaten egg, 1/4 c. catsup, 2 Tbsp. mustard, 2 tsp. chopped onion, 1 tsp. salt, and pepper to taste, pack lightly into an 8-inch square pan, bake at 350°F for 20 minutes, sprinkle with 1/2 c. grated Parmesan cheese, bake 10 minutes longer, let stand 5 minutes, and cut into squares.

ID 893 — Spinach Squares Combine 1 c. flour, 1 tsp. baking powder, 2 beaten eggs, 1 c. milk, and 1/4 c. melted butter or margarine, stir in 1/2 c. chopped onion, 1/2 c. shredded Cheddar cheese, and 1 (10 oz.) pkg. chopped spinach, pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, bake at 350°F for 35 minutes, and cut into squares.

ID 894 — Sweet Baked Beans Mix 2 small cans pork and beans, 1 chopped small onion, 1 chopped large dill pickle, 1 c. sugar, 1/2 c. brown sugar, 1 Tbsp. ketchup, and 1 tsp. mustard, bake at 350°F for 20 minutes, and optionally top with bacon strips.

ID 895 — Butterscotch Torte Mix 3 egg yolks with 1 c. sugar, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1 tsp. almond flavoring, and 1/2 tsp. baking powder, whip 3 egg whites until stiff and fold in, then fold in 1 c. graham cracker crumbs and 1/2 c. chopped nuts, pour into a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, bake at 325°F for 30 minutes, cool, and spread with 1/2 pt. whipped cream.

ID 896 — Mexican Bean Salad Combine 2 cans Ranch Style red beans, 1 chopped tomato, 1 chopped onion, 3/4 lb. grated Cheddar cheese, and pepper to taste, then just before serving add 1 c. Catalina dressing and about 1/2 bag crushed Fritos.

ID 897 — Hungarian Goulash Cut 2 lb. beef into 1-inch pieces and brown in 4 Tbsp. fat, add 1 c. sliced onions and 1 minced garlic clove, lightly brown, mix 3/4 c. catsup, 3/8 c. Worcestershire sauce, 1 tsp. vinegar, 1 Tbsp. brown sugar, 2 1/2 tsp. paprika, 2 tsp. salt, 1 tsp. dry mustard, and a dash of red pepper, stir into meat, add 3 c. water, cover and simmer 2 to 2 1/2 hours, thicken with 2 Tbsp. flour mixed with 1/4 c. water, and serve over cooked noodles with parsley.

ID 898 — Broccoli Cornbread Mix 3/4 c. cottage cheese with 1 tsp. salt, add 4 eggs, then stir in chopped broccoli, finely chopped onion, 1 stick melted butter, and 1 box Jiffy corn muffin mix, beat until smooth, and bake at 400°F for 20 minutes or until golden.

ID 899 — Orange Blossoms Prepare 1 pkg. yellow cake mix according to package directions, place 1 tsp. batter into each well-greased miniature muffin pan, and bake at 325°F for about 10 minutes, finishing with confectioners sugar glaze made from 1 c. orange juice, 1/2 c. lemon juice, and 2 lb. confectioners sugar.

ID 900 — Corn Pudding Mix 3/4 c. sugar, 2 Tbsp. flour, 1/2 tsp. salt, 2 eggs, 1 1/4 c. milk, 1/2 stick melted butter, and 1 1/2 pt. drained corn, pour into a baking dish, and bake at 375°F for 1 hour.

ID 901 — Chicken Cordon Blue Pound 3 chicken breasts (halves) until thin, lay 3 slices Swiss or Jack cheese and 3 slices cooked ham on the breasts, roll up and secure with toothpicks; mix 3 Tbsp. flour, 1 tsp. salt, pepper to taste, and 1 tsp. paprika in a plastic bag, add the rolls and shake to coat, then melt 3 Tbsp. butter in a frying pan and brown on all sides, add 1/2 c. white wine and 1 chicken bouillon cube, cover and simmer 30 minutes; remove chicken, add 1 c. whipping cream to the pan and cook on medium-high for 3 minutes until smooth and creamy, then pour over chicken (serves 3).

ID 902 — Corn Casserole In a large bowl, mix 1 can creamed corn, 1 can whole corn, 1 stick margarine (melted), and 1 box Jiffy corn bread mix (dry) until well combined, then stir in about 3/4 of the 1 (16 oz.) container fat free sour cream and mix well.

ID 903 — Poppy Seed Bread Mix 1 c. boiling water with 2 Tbsp. poppy seed and set aside; mix 1 pkg. Betty Crocker butter pecan cake mix, 1 small pkg. instant coconut pudding, 1/2 c. oil, and 4 eggs, then add the seed-and-water mixture, pour into 2 greased loaf pans, and bake at 325° for 1 hour (freezes well).

ID 904 — Buttermilk Brownie Cake In a saucepan combine 1 c. butter, 1/3 c. cocoa, and 1 cup water, bring to a boil stirring constantly, then remove from heat; in a large bowl sift together 2 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 1 tsp. soda, and 1/2 tsp. salt, stir in 2 slightly beaten eggs, 1/2 c. buttermilk, and 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, add the cocoa mixture and mix until blended, pour into a greased 15 x 10 x 1-inch pan and bake at 375° for 20 minutes, then immediately pour frosting over brownies and spread evenly.

ID 905 — Seven Layer Salad Layer lettuce, tomatoes, boiled eggs (cut), grated cheese, 2 cans English peas (drained), Miracle Whip mayonnaise, and bacon bits in the order listed, cover with Miracle Whip mayonnaise, sprinkle bacon bits on top, and refrigerate.

ID 906 — Taco Salad Combine 3 lb. ground beef, 2 c. chopped onions, 1 c. chopped celery, 1 c. chopped green bell pepper, 3 Tbsp. cumin seed, 3 cloves garlic (minced), and 4 tsp. chili powder in a crock-pot and mix well, add salt and pepper to taste, and cook on low 3 to 4 hours; heat 8 oz. Velveeta cheese (shredded) with 1 (10 oz.) can Ro-Tel tomatoes in a saucepan until melted, stirring constantly, then layer 18 c. chopped lettuce, the beef mixture, 8 chopped tomatoes, the cheese sauce, and 1 (16 oz.) pkg. crushed corn chips on individual plates (yield: 12 servings).

ID 907 — Pizza Dippers Grease 1 large cookie sheet, unroll 10 oz. can Pillsbury refrigerator pizza crust, cut the rectangle in half crosswise and then into 8 (1-inch) strips (16 total), place strips apart on the sheet, brush with 2 Tbsp. margarine, sprinkle with 1 1/2 tsp. pizza seasonings, bake at 350° for 11 to 17 minutes, sprinkle with 4 oz. (1 c.) shredded Mozzarella cheese and return to oven to melt, then serve immediately with 8 oz. warm pizza sauce for dipping (makes 16 servings).

ID 908 — Madge’s Refrigerator Rolls Sprinkle 1 Tbsp. sugar over 1 pkg. yeast in 1/2 c. lukewarm water and let foam; scald 1 pt. milk with 1/2 c. sugar, 1/2 c. shortening or oleo, and 1 Tbsp. salt, cool, then add the yeast, fold in 2 egg whites beaten stiff, stir in 6 c. sifted flour (dough should be soft, do not add more flour), cover and let rise until doubled, stir down, refrigerate covered overnight, then bake in muffin tins using two small balls dipped in melted oleo to form one roll.

ID 909 — Super Sundae Pie Stir 2 pt. (1 qt.) vanilla ice cream slightly softened until smooth, spoon into 1 (6 oz.) graham cracker pie crust and cover, freeze several hours until hard, then let stand 10 minutes to soften; spoon 1 jar strawberry topping onto the serving plate, set a slice of pie on top, garnish with 1 bottle chocolate sundae syrup plus 1/2 c. nuts, whipped cream, and maraschino cherries as desired, then return to freezer.

ID 910 — Cranberry-Orange Relish For Poultry Combine 2 oranges (peeled and sectioned), 1 (16 oz.) can whole cranberry sauce, 1 (16 oz.) can pear halves (drained and chopped), 1 chopped unpeeled apple, 1 c. sugar, 1/2 c. raisins, 1/4 c. chopped pecans, 1 Tbsp. vinegar, 1/2 tsp. ground cinnamon, and 1/2 tsp. ground ginger in a saucepan, bring to a boil over medium heat, then reduce heat and simmer until thick; cool and refrigerate.

ID 911 — Swedish Heirloom Cookies Cream 1/2 c. shortening with 1/2 c. butter (softened) until light and fluffy, add 1 c. sifted powdered sugar and 1/2 tsp. salt and mix well, stir in 2 c. all-purpose flour, then stir in 1 Tbsp. water, 1 Tbsp. vanilla extract, and 1 1/4 c. ground almonds; shape into 1-inch balls, place on ungreased baking sheets and flatten slightly, bake at 325° for 12 to 15 minutes, then dredge warm cookies in powdered sugar (yields about 8 dozen).

ID 912 — Garden Cabbage Salad Combine 1 small cabbage (finely shredded), 1 bunch green onions (chopped), 1 shredded carrot, 1 small green pepper (finely chopped), 6 radishes (thinly sliced), and 1 cucumber (finely chopped), cover and chill, then toss with Dressing just before serving (yields 8 to 10 servings).

ID 913 — Kentucky Pecan Pie Mix 1 c. white corn syrup, 1 c. brown sugar, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/3 c. melted butter, 1 tsp. vanilla, 3 whole eggs (slightly beaten), and 1 c. pecans (finely chopped), bake 45 minutes at 350°, and decorate with whole pecan halves.

ID 914 — London Broil Place 1 flank steak (about 1 1/2 lb.) in a shallow pan, combine 1 c. salad oil with 1 Tbsp. vinegar and 1 clove garlic (minced) and pour over, cover and refrigerate 3 hours or overnight turning several times; broil 3 inches from heat about 5 minutes, season with salt and pepper, turn and broil 3 minutes, season again, then carve very thin slices diagonally across the grain (serves 4 to 5).

ID 915 — Hello Dolly Bars Melt 1 stick of Oleo, mix with 1 c. Graham Cracker Crumbs and spread in the bottom of a greased 9 x 13-inch pan, then layer 1 c. Chocolate Chips, 1 c. Butterscotch Chips, 1 c. Walnuts chopped (optional), and 1 c. Coconut (shedded), pour 1 c. Condensed Milk over top, bake at 350° for 30-35 minutes, cool, and cut into bars.

ID 916 — Macaroni And Cheese Casserole Mix 1 lb. sharp cheese (grated), 8 oz. macaroni (cooked and drained), 1 can condensed cream of mushroom soup, 2 oz. jar pimento, 1 c. mayonnaise, and 1/2 onion (grated), then before baking cover with crumbled cheese crackers and dot with butter, and bake at 325° for 40 minutes.

ID 917 — Betsy’s Chocolate Fudge Cake Melt 3 sq. unsweetened chocolate over hot water and cool; grease and flour 2 to 3 (9-inch) cake pans; sift together 2 1/4 c. sifted flour, 2 tsp. baking powder, and 1/2 tsp. salt, beat 1/2 c. butter until soft, add 2 1/4 c. packed light brown sugar and 3 eggs and beat at high speed until light and fluffy (about 5 minutes), beat in 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla and the chocolate, stir in dry ingredients alternating with 1 c. sour cream, beating well after each addition, stir in 1 c. boiling water (batter will be thin), pour into pans and bake at 350° for 35 minutes, cool 10 minutes in pans then turn out and cool completely before icing with Chocolate Fudge Frosting.

ID 918 — Cream Cheese Squares Mix 1 box yellow cake mix with 1 egg and 1 stick margarine, press into a 9 x 12-inch sheet cake pan, then mix and cream together 1 box 10x sugar, 2 eggs, and 8 oz. cream cheese (softened), spread over the base, bake at 350° for 40 minutes, and cut when cool.

ID 919 — Beef Barbecue Put 3 to 5 lb. boneless chuck roast in a pot, add 1 c. ketchup, 1/2 c. water, 1/2 tsp. mustard, 4 Tbsp. lemon juice, 2 Tbsp. vinegar, and 1 onion (finely chopped), then cook on low to medium heat 3 to 4 hours (on top of stove) until the meat will shred, adding extra water and ketchup if liquid disappears.

ID 920 — Chicken Stroganoff Slice 1 lb. chicken breasts into thin strips; in a skillet over medium heat heat 1 Tbsp. of the 2 Tbsp. vegetable oil, add 2 medium onions and sauté 2 minutes, add 1/2 lb. mushrooms (2 c.) thinly sliced and sauté 3 minutes, remove vegetables and reserve; heat remaining oil, add chicken and 1 tsp. minced garlic and cook as for stir-fry, return vegetables, add 1/2 c. chicken broth and 1/8 tsp. pepper, then mix 1 Tbsp. cornstarch with 2 Tbsp. water and stir into skillet, bring to a boil and boil 1 minute stirring constantly, remove from heat and stir in 1 (8 oz.) pkg. yogurt, heat gently over low (do not boil), and serve over hot cooked noodles.

ID 921 — Cream Pie And Pudding (Microwave) Combine 3/4 c. sugar, 3/8 c. flour, and 1/4 tsp. salt in a deep 2-quart glass bowl, add 2 eggs or 3 egg yolks and 2 c. milk, beat with a whisk until smooth, then microwave at full power for 8 minutes stirring 3 times, and proceed as the recipe directs.

ID 922 — Crispix Cookies Melt 1 (12 oz.) pkg. butterscotch morsels with 1 (6 oz.) pkg. semi-sweet chocolate morsels in a large saucepan over low heat, stirring constantly until smooth, remove from heat and add 1 1/2 c. salted peanuts and 4 c. Kellogg's Crispix cereal, stir gently until well coated, drop by teaspoons onto waxed paper, and chill until firm.

ID 923 — Rum Balls Combine 3 c. finely crushed vanilla wafers with 1 c. finely chopped nuts (any kind) and 1/2 cup of the 1 1/2 c. powdered sugar in a large bowl, melt 1 c. semi-sweet chocolate with 1/2 c. light corn syrup, stir in 1/3 c. rum until smooth, pour over the crumb mixture and mix thoroughly, roll into 1-inch balls, place on wax paper, roll each ball in the remaining 1 c. powdered sugar, and store airtight for at least 3 days before serving.

ID 924 — Millionaire Cake Beat together 2 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 2 tsp. soda, 2 eggs, 1 c. coconut, 1 c. chopped nuts, 1 tsp. vanilla, 1 tsp. salt, and a 20 oz. can crushed pineapple and juice, then bake in a 9 x 13-inch pan at 350° for 45 to 55 minutes.

ID 925 — Hawaiian Carrots Scrape and cut 1 lb. pkg. carrots into small pieces, cook and drain and salt, drain 1 (No. 2) can and 1 small can crushed pineapple, then cook 1/2 cup pineapple juice with 3 Tbsp. cornstarch, 1/2 stick oleo, and 1/2 c. brown sugar until thick, add carrots and pineapple and simmer 10 minutes (better if made a day ahead).

ID 926 — Ginny’s Salad Wash, dry, and break 3 to 4 bunches red leaf lettuce into bite-size pieces, toss with 12 oz. shredded Mozzarella cheese and 6 to 8 oz. chopped walnuts, then mix with 2 pkg. Good Seasons Italian dressing mixed according to directions just before serving.

ID 927 — Onion Soup Cook 2 large onions (thinly sliced) in 1 Tbsp. butter and 1 Tbsp. vegetable oil for 15 minutes stirring occasionally, add 1/4 tsp. sugar and cook 15 minutes until onions are brown, sprinkle with 2 Tbsp. flour and blend in 6 c. beef broth plus 1/4 c. white wine and seasonings, simmer 30 minutes; lightly toast 4 to 8 slices French bread in a 350° oven for 20 minutes, baste each slice with 1/2 teaspoon of the 2 tsp. vegetable oil and garlic, serve soup with toast floating on top, sprinkle with 1 to 2 c. grated Swiss cheese, bake 15 minutes, and serve hot (makes 4 to 8 servings).

ID 928 — Banana Walnut Cake Cream 3/4 c. shortening (butter) and gradually add 2 1/4 c. sugar, creaming until light and fluffy, add 3 eggs (beaten well), sift 3 c. cake flour before measuring then add 3 tsp. baking powder, 3/4 tsp. soda, and 3/4 tsp. salt, then add 6 Tbsp. sour milk alternating with the flour mixture, beating after each addition, add 1 1/2 tsp. vanilla, add 1 1/2 c. banana pulp and beat well, stir in 1 1/2 c. chopped walnuts, pour into a greased Bundt pan, and bake at 350° for 50 to 60 minutes.

ID 929 — Fish And Broccoli Roll-Ups (Serves 4) Cut 16 oz. flounder or haddock into strips, cut 4 c. broccoli into small pieces, alternate broccoli pieces and rolled fish strips onto kabob spears adding 8 lemon wedges to each end, baste with 1/2 c. salad dressing, and broil 8 to 10 minutes.

ID 930 — Fat Free Pizza Treats Top toasted English muffins with pizza sauce, then add toppings of your choice (Parmesan cheese, grated onion, sliced mushrooms, chopped green pepper) ending with 1 Tbsp. (skim) Mozzarella cheese, and toast in a toaster oven until cheese melts.

ID 931 — Sesame Chicken Wings Whisk together 3 1/2 Tbsp. light soy sauce, 1/2 garlic clove (minced), 1/2 tsp. minced fresh ginger, 1 Tbsp. honey, and freshly ground black pepper to taste, add 2 lb. chicken wings with wing tips cut off and toss to coat, marinate covered and chilled for 2 hours, line a pan with foil and arrange wings drained in one layer reserving the marinade, brush with 1 Tbsp. Oriental sesame oil, sprinkle with 2 Tbsp. sesame seed toasted lightly, and bake at 400° for 30 to 35 minutes basting occasionally with the reserved marinade until browned (serves 4 as an hors d'oeuvre).

ID 932 — Imitation Crabmeat Salad Shred 2 lb. imitation crabmeat into thin strips about 1/4 to 1/2-inch x 3 to 4-inches long, cook 1 pkg. spiral pasta and drain, combine pasta with crabmeat and add 8 oz. sour cream, 10 oz. mayonnaise, 3 to 4 sticks celery, 3 to 4 green onions (about 1/4 c.), 6 oz. water chestnuts, 6 oz. frozen pea pods, 1/4 tsp. dill weed, 1/4 tsp. onion powder, 1/4 tsp. Beau Monde, 1/4 tsp. celery salt, and 1/4 tsp. pepper, then chill at least 1/2 hour before serving.

ID 933 — Macaroni And Cottage Cheese Cook 3 c. uncooked macaroni until tender and drain, mix in 1 small carton cottage cheese, brown 1/2 stick butter in a skillet and pour over, then add salt and pepper to taste and serve.

ID 934 — String Pie Brown 1 lb. ground beef with 1/2 c. chopped onion and 1/4 c. chopped green onion in a large skillet, stirring to separate meat, then drain fat and stir in 1 jar spaghetti sauce; in a large bowl combine 1/3 c. grated Parmesan cheese, 2 eggs (beaten), and 2 tsp. butter, mix well and spread in the bottom of a 13 x 9-inch pan, spread 1 c. cottage cheese over top, pour the sauce mixture over cottage cheese, sprinkle with 1/2 c. shredded Mozzarella cheese, and bake at 350° until cheese melts, about 20 minutes.

ID 935 — Easters Hamburgers Brown hamburger patties, slice raw onions on top, mix 1 can tomato sauce with 1/2 tsp. dry mustard, 2 Tbsp. brown sugar, salt and pepper, and chili powder, pour over hamburgers, and bake 1 hour at 350°.

ID 936 — Coconut Macaroons Combine 1 1/3 c. coconut, 2 Tbsp. all-purpose flour, 1/3 c. sugar, and 1/2 tsp. salt, stir in 2 egg whites (beaten) and 1/2 tsp. almond extract and mix well, lightly grease a cookie sheet, cut maraschino cherries into quarters, drop batter by teaspoonfuls about 1-inch apart and top each with a cherry, then bake at 325° for 20 to 25 minutes, removing when edges are golden.

ID 937 — Cranberry Salad Put 3 oranges, 2 apples, and 1 lb. cranberries through a food chopper, drain a No. 2 can crushed pineapple and add it, dissolve 2 small pkg. Jell-O * plus 1 1/2 c. sugar in 2 c. water (heat to dissolve thoroughly), mix into the fruit mixture, add 1 c. chopped nuts, and refrigerate about 24 hours before serving.

ID 938 — Lazy Day Salad Mix by hand 1 large can fruit cocktail (drained), 2 cans mandarin oranges (drained), 1 large can crushed pineapple with juice, 1 box instant vanilla pudding, and 1 box instant lemon pudding, then fold in 1 large container Cool Whip and refrigerate all day or overnight (keeps 7 to 10 days in the fridge).

ID 939 — Pear Relish Let 16 pears (peeled, cored and ground), 6 medium onions (ground), 8 green peppers (ground), 4 sweet red peppers (ground), and 2 hot peppers (ground) stand in separate containers for 1 hour, pour boiling water over each and drain well; combine everything in a large kettle with 6 c. vinegar (5% acidity), 6 c. sugar, 3 Tbsp. mustard seed, 2 Tbsp. pickling salt, 1 Tbsp. ground turmeric, 1 tsp. ground allspice, 1 tsp. ground cinnamon, and 1 tsp. ground ginger, bring to a boil then reduce heat and simmer uncovered 30 minutes, ladle into hot sterilized jars leaving 1/4 inch headspace, remove air bubbles and wipe rims, apply lids and bands, process in a boiling water bath 20 minutes, store in a cool place 1 month before using, and chill before serving (makes 10 pints).

ID 940 — Strawberry Bread Preheat oven to 350° and grease and flour two 9 x 5-inch loaf pans; in a medium bowl stir 2 1/2 c. fresh crushed strawberries or 2 (10 oz.) containers frozen strawberries (thawed) with 4 eggs and 1 1/4 c. salad oil, in a large bowl combine 3 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 1 Tbsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. soda, 1 tsp. salt, and 1 c. chopped nuts, add the berry mixture to the dry ingredients and stir until blended, pour into pans, and bake 1 hour or until a toothpick comes out clean.

ID 941 — Strawberry Salad Dissolve 2 pkg. strawberry Jello in 1 c. boiling water, add 1 large can crushed pineapple, 3 mashed bananas, 1 c. chopped pecans, and 1 to 2 c. sour cream, pour half of the mixture into a pan and let set, spread on cream, then add remaining Jello mixture.

ID 942 — Chili Beef Casserole Cook 1 c. macaroni in boiling salted water until done (10 to 12 minutes) and drain thoroughly, brown 3/4 lb. extra lean ground beef in a skillet, add 1 can tomato soup and 1 can chili beef soup along with the macaroni, heat 5 to 7 minutes stirring occasionally until bubbly, cut 3 slices sharp processed American cheese diagonally and place on top, cover briefly to melt, and serve at once (serves 6).

ID 943 — Bread Dissolve 1 pkg. yeast (RapidRise) in 2 c. warm water, add 3 Tbsp. melted butter or shortening, 1/2 c. sugar, and 1/2 tsp. salt, then add 1 to 1 1/2 c. whole wheat flour and blend with an electric mixer, gradually add bread flour (3 1/2 to 4 c., total flour about 5 c.), folding in the last flour by hand, knead on a floured surface, place in an oiled bowl and oil the top, cover with wax paper and let rise until doubled, divide into pans and let rise again, then bake at 350° for 30 minutes to 1 hour until golden brown (makes 2 large or 4 small loaves).

ID 944 — Salmon Casserole Baked In Sour Cream Place reserved liquid from 1 (1 lb.) can salmon in a bowl, add 1 Tbsp. lemon juice, 1/2 tsp. salt, pepper to taste, 1 c. sour cream, and 1/2 tsp. dry dill weed and mix until smooth, break salmon into large chunks and place in a greased 1-quart casserole, pour sauce over salmon, top with 1 medium onion (thinly sliced) and 1 Tbsp. chopped parsley, cover and bake at 350° for 30 minutes (yields 4 servings).

ID 945 — Carrie’s Cabbage Soup Combine 6 c. shredded green cabbage, 1 c. chopped onion, 2 c. diced celery, 1/2 c. diced green pepper, 1/2 tsp. thyme, 1/4 tsp. marjoram, 1 Tbsp. anisette, 6 peeled ripe red tomatoes, 2 pkg. dry onion soup mix, 2 cans beef bouillon, water to cover, 1/4 tsp. tarragon, 2 Tbsp. granulated sugar, and 8 oz. tomato sauce, bring to a rolling boil then simmer about 3 hours, adding 1 lb. ground beef (browned, optional) or 1 lb. sausage in the last 20 minutes.

ID 946 — Chicken And Pasta Salad Combine 1 (8 oz.) pkg. egg noodles (cooked and drained) with 3 cooked chicken breasts cut into small pieces, seedless green grapes, and sliced almonds, mix mayonnaise, Ranch dressing, creamy Italian dressing, and a little sugar to taste to form the dressing, then pour over and toss.

ID 947 — Calico Beans Brown 1 lb. hamburger and 1/2 lb. chopped bacon, add 1 medium chopped onion and 1/2 c. chopped celery, mix together 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce, 1/2 c. brown sugar, 1 c. catsup, 1 Tbsp. liquid smoke, 1 Tbsp. mustard, and 1 Tbsp. vinegar, then combine with 1 can lima beans (drained), 1 can pork and beans, 1 can red beans, and 1 can black-eyed peas, mix with the meat and bake in a casserole dish at 350° for 45 minutes.

ID 948 — Ham Roll-Up Spread soft cream cheese over 1/2 lb. thin-sliced boiled ham, place a breadstick on each slice, and roll up.

ID 949 — Penne Al’Arrabbiato Bring water to a boil and cook pasta (DeCecco penne, plain or rigati), meanwhile sauté 3 to 4 cloves garlic in 1 to 2 Tbsp. olive oil briefly, add 2 cans (14 oz.) Italian-style chopped tomatoes, 1 Tbsp. minced parsley, whole tiny red peppers to taste, and salt, simmer in an open skillet until pasta is cooked, then toss sauce with drained pasta and garnish with fresh parsley.

ID 950 — Corn Casserole Mix 1 can creamed corn, 1 can whole corn (drained), 2 eggs, 1 stick oleo, 1 (8 oz.) sour cream, and 1 small box corn muffin mix, pour into a 2 to 3-quart casserole, and bake at 350° for 45 minutes.

ID 951 — Vegetable Dip Mix 2 c. mayonnaise, 2 c. sour cream, 1/2 c. chopped green onions, 1/2 c. chopped green pepper, 1/2 c. diced pimentos, 1/4 c. Bac*Os, 1/2 tsp. Tabasco, 1/4 tsp. garlic powder or salt, and salt and pepper to taste, then refrigerate several hours or overnight (keeps well for about 2 weeks).

ID 952 — Spinach Dip Thaw and drain 1 (10 oz.) pkg. frozen chopped spinach and mix with 2 (8 oz.) pkg. cream cheese, 1/2 c. chopped green parsley, 1/2 c. chopped green onions, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/2 tsp. Season-All, 1/2 tsp. black pepper, and 1/4 tsp. garlic powder; separately slice California oranges, limes, and lemons paper thin, pour 2 bottles Sangaree Punch over an ice mold, add 5 oz. cognac, 2 oz. Triple Sec, 5 oz. vodka, and 2 oz. Meyers dark rum, add fruit after 1 hour, and serve.

ID 953 — Easy Chicken Pot Pie Lightly spray a 9 x 13-inch baking dish and line the bottom with approximately 2 c. cooked chicken cut into bite-size pieces, mix 1 can Veg-All vegetables with 1 can cream of chicken soup, 1 can cream of onion soup, and 1 can cream of mushroom soup and spread over chicken, then mix 1 1/2 sticks melted butter or margarine with 1 c. milk and 1 1/2 c. flour and pour over the soup layer, baking at 350° for 30 to 40 minutes until golden brown.

ID 954 — Fruit Pizza Spread Pillsbury sugar cookie dough onto a baking sheet, bake 12 to 13 minutes at the temperature listed on the package, cool completely, loosen with a knife, then top with 1 (8 oz.) pkg. cream cheese mixed with 1/3 c. sugar and decorate with fruit of your choice.

ID 955 — Grasshopper Pie Crush 22 Oreo cookies and mix with 1/4 c. margarine, press into a pie plate and bake at 350° for 10 minutes, cool completely, then fill with a mixture of 1/4 c. creme de menthe, 1 (7 oz.) jar Marshmallow Fluff, and 1 pt. whipped cream.

ID 956 — Squash Souffle Cook and mash 2 c. yellow squash with 2 Tbsp. butter or Land O Lakes sweet cream spread, add 4 egg whites (well beaten), 1 c. milk (1%), salt and pepper, and 1 c. Ritz cracker crumbs, pour into a Pam-sprayed casserole, top with 1 c. grated reduced fat Cheddar cheese, and bake at 350° for 30 to 45 minutes until firm (serves 6 to 8).

ID 957 — Loris’s Egg Salad Mash 6 hard-boiled eggs with 1 chopped sweet gherkin pickle, 1/4 c. chopped onion, and 1/4 c. chopped green pepper, stir in 1/3 c. Miracle Whip, then add 1 small jar pimento (drained), 1 tsp. salt, and a dash of paprika, chill, and serve.

ID 958 — Apple Kuchen Divide 1 recipe Basic Sweet Dough into 2 portions and press into two buttered 8 x 8-inch pans, press in 4 peeled and sliced apples rounded side up, sprinkle with 1/2 c. sugar mixed with 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, drizzle with 1/4 c. melted butter, let rise until doubled, then bake at 350° for 40 to 50 minutes until golden (serves 16).

ID 959 — Eggplant-Tomato Casserole Peel and slice 1 small eggplant into 1/4-inch rounds and peel and slice 4 tomatoes, layer eggplant in a 2-quart casserole and sprinkle with salt and pepper, top with tomatoes, oregano flakes, and some of the 1/4 c. grated Parmesan cheese, repeat layers ending with cheese, cover and bake at 400° for 30 to 40 minutes until eggplant is tender.

ID 960 — Strawberry Bread Combine 3 c. flour, 2 c. sugar, 1 1/2 tsp. cinnamon, 1 tsp. baking soda, and 1 tsp. salt, mix separately 1 c. cooking oil, 4 beaten eggs, and 2 c. crushed strawberries, stir wet ingredients into dry just until moistened, add 1 1/4 c. chopped walnuts or pecans if desired, pour into 2 greased loaf pans, and bake at 350° for 1 hour.

ID 961 — Salsa Mix 6 diced tomatoes with 1 (4 oz.) can chopped green chilies, 1 bunch green onions (chopped), 1 1/2 c. finely diced celery, 2 medium yellow onions (chopped), 1 c. chopped cilantro or parsley, 2 (15 oz.) cans tomato sauce, 1 tsp. cumin, garlic (fresh or powdered) to taste, and salt and pepper, chill 1 hour before serving and stir well before serving.

ID 962 — Meatball Stew Combine 2 c. cornflakes cereal, 1 egg, 1 (10 1/2 oz.) can beef broth, 1/2 tsp. salt, 1/8 tsp. pepper, and 1 lb. ground beef and form into meatballs; brown in 2 Tbsp. vegetable oil, then add 1 (10 3/4 oz.) can tomato soup, 1/2 c. water, 1/4 tsp. thyme, 2 c. frozen sliced carrots, 1 medium onion (sliced into rings), 1 can whole white potatoes (drained), and dried parsley flakes, simmer until vegetables are tender.

ID 963 — Cauliflower-Broccoli Casserole Simmer 1 box frozen cauliflower and 1 box frozen broccoli until tender, melt 1/2 stick butter in a skillet and add 1 c. cream of mushroom soup, 1/2 c. milk, and 8 oz. Velveeta cheese cooking until melted, combine vegetables with cheese mixture and 1 c. cooked rice, then bake uncovered at 350° for 30 minutes.

ID 964 — Cabbage Casserole Sauté 1/2 c. chopped celery, 1/2 c. chopped bell pepper, and 1 small chopped onion in margarine, add 3 c. shredded cabbage and 1/4 c. water, cover and steam 5 to 6 minutes, remove from heat and stir in 1 c. cream of celery soup and pimento, transfer to a casserole dish, top with Pepperidge Farm herb stuffing mixed with butter, and bake at 350° for 20 minutes.

ID 965 — Best Ever Salad Cook 8 oz. fine spaghetti (or 7 oz. Mexican angel hair) and cool, add 1/2 c. chopped onion, 1/2 c. chopped green pepper, 1/2 c. chopped celery, 2 c. chopped tomatoes, salt and pepper, and 1/4 tsp. curry, then stir in 1 can cream of celery soup and a small amount of mayonnaise if needed.

ID 966 — Black Bottom Cupcakes Mix 8 oz. cream cheese with 1 egg, 1/3 c. sugar, and 1/8 tsp. salt and stir in 6 oz. chocolate chips; separately mix 1 1/2 c. flour, 1 c. sugar, 1/4 c. cocoa, 1 tsp. baking soda, and 1/2 tsp. salt, add 1 c. water, 1/3 c. cooking oil, 1 Tbsp. vinegar, and 1 tsp. vanilla and beat well, fill cupcake liners 1/3 full with chocolate batter, top with cream cheese mixture, and bake at 350° for 30 to 35 minutes (makes 18 to 20 cupcakes).

ID 967 — Tuna Casserole Prepare 1 large box Kraft macaroni and cheese dinner according to package directions, cook and drain peas if frozen, sauté 3/4 c. celery and 1/2 c. onion and drain, then combine with 1 large can tuna fish, 1 can cream of mushroom soup, 2 c. peas, 1/2 c. water, and salt and pepper to taste, and bake at 350° for 35 minutes.
